# Skyrim:Breton (dead)

## Overview

**Bretons** are unnamed and deceased [Bretons](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") scattered around Skyrim.

| Breton (RefID: 000648E7, 000BB422, 0004BAF6, 0008BA08, 00051A3F, 0005BA37, 0010C251, 000E78D2) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Breton "Lore:Breton")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Race | [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 1 | Class | [Citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000648E7 000BB422 0004BAF6 0008BA08 00051A3F 0005BA37 0010C251 000E78D2 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 000457F6 |
| Other Information | | | |
| [Health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") | 0 (**Dead**) | [Magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Magicka "Skyrim:Magicka") | 50 |
| [Stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") | 50 | | |
| Voice Type | [MaleCondescending](/wiki/Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending "Category:Skyrim-Voice-MaleCondescending") | | |
| Respawns | Yes | | |

.jpg)

A dead Breton male in [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave")

These **Bretons** are all male [citizens](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") and wear randomly determined farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") (7 variations) or a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") (4 variations), with a 50% chance for a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat") (3 variations). Additionally there is a slim chance they may carry a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a small amount of gold.

They can be found in the following locations:

|  |
| --- |
| - [Stony Creek Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Stony_Creek_Cave "Skyrim:Stony Creek Cave"), in the entrance. - [Rannveig's Fast](/wiki/Skyrim:Rannveig%27s_Fast "Skyrim:Rannveig's Fast"), inside a cage in [Sild the Warlock's](/wiki/Skyrim:Sild_the_Warlock "Skyrim:Sild the Warlock") chamber. - [Sunderstone Gorge](/wiki/Skyrim:Sunderstone_Gorge "Skyrim:Sunderstone Gorge"), locked inside a cage near the [Word Wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Word_Wall "Skyrim:Word Wall"). - [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), on the floor next to a table. - [Cidhna Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Cidhna_Mine "Skyrim:Cidhna Mine"), at the entrance to a small dead end off the main cavern. - [Soljund's Sinkhole](/wiki/Skyrim:Soljund%27s_Sinkhole "Skyrim:Soljund's Sinkhole"), at the bottom of a sinkhole. - [Fort Greenwall](/wiki/Skyrim:Fort_Greenwall "Skyrim:Fort Greenwall"), in front of a fire in a kitchen. - [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook"), inside a cage. - [Nilheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Nilheim "Skyrim:Nilheim"), on a rock near the tower. |

| Breton (RefID: 000648E8, 0007A608, 00047178, 00077B90) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Breton "Lore:Breton")) | | | |

| Respawns | Yes | | |

_02.jpg)

A dead Breton female in [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild")

These **Bretons** are all female [citizens](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") and wear randomly determined farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") (7 variations) or a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots") (4 variations), with a 50% chance for a [hat](/wiki/Skyrim:Hat "Skyrim:Hat") (3 variations). Additionally there is a slim chance they may carry a [lockpick](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpick "Skyrim:Lockpick") and a small amount of gold.
They can be found in the following locations:

|  |
| --- |
| - [Yngvild](/wiki/Skyrim:Yngvild "Skyrim:Yngvild"), in [Arondil's](/wiki/Skyrim:Arondil "Skyrim:Arondil") throne room. - [Lost Tongue Overlook](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Tongue_Overlook "Skyrim:Lost Tongue Overlook"), just outside an open cage. - [Bloodlet Throne](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodlet_Throne "Skyrim:Bloodlet Throne"), on a single bed in a bedroom. - [Cronvangr Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Cronvangr_Hall "Skyrim:Cronvangr Hall"), on a table in a small building. |

If [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") is installed, another dead female Breton will be added to the game.

_03.jpg)

A dead Breton female in [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave")

This female **Breton** can be found in [Darkfall Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave"). In addition to her outfit and inventory (which are also randomly determined as listed above), she also carries a [Darkfall Cave note](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkfall_Cave_Note "Skyrim:Darkfall Cave Note").

# Skyrim:Breya

## Overview

| Breya (RefID: 00056555, 00056556) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | [Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel") | | |
| Race | [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") | Gender | Female |
| Level | 4 | Class | [Warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:Warrior_(class) "Skyrim:Warrior (class)") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 00056555 00056556 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0004C724 0004C754 |

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [Dwarven Automaton Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Automaton_Faction "Skyrim:Dwarven Automaton Faction"); [Player Ally Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Player_Ally_Faction "Skyrim:Player Ally Faction") | | |

Breya's ghost

**Breya** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost "Skyrim:Ghost") in [Avanchnzel](/wiki/Skyrim:Avanchnzel "Skyrim:Avanchnzel"). She appears to be generated when given the quest [Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths") as her RefID will change.

Breya's corpse can be found near the pedestal in the final chamber of Avanchnzel, next to a dead [centurion](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Centurion "Skyrim:Dwarven Centurion"). On her corpse is a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor") with matching pairs of [gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets") and [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Unfathomable Depths](/wiki/Skyrim:Unfathomable_Depths "Skyrim:Unfathomable Depths")**: Uncover the [memories](/wiki/Skyrim:Lexicon "Skyrim:Lexicon") of the Dwemer.

### Unfathomable Depths

As you first enter Avanchnzel you will see the ghost of Breya speaking to the other ghosts:

:   **Drennen**: *"I don't like this place. It feels like we're being... watched."*
:   **Breya**: *"It's a simple job, Drennen. We get in, we steal the Lexicon, we leave. Don't get jumpy."*
:   **Fathoms**: *"If you two cannot handle this, we can find others to hire."*
:   **Roots**: *"Enough. Their services will be more than adequate. Let us continue."*

Just before the doors to Avanchnzel Animoncultory:

:   **Breya**: *"Why are all these metal... things... ignoring us?"*
:   **Roots**: *"Anavchnzel*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *is waiting."*
:   **Breya**: *"Waiting for what?"*
:   **Roots**: *"No one seems to know. Perhaps the return of the Dwemer. Perhaps the ending of the world."*
:   **Breya**: *"Best get rid of the ones we see. Just in case."*

In the first chamber of the Animoncultory, you will yet again encounter the ghosts, this time trying to break into one of the many hidden chambers of Avanchnzel. At this point, it is clear the place is starting to get to them:

:   **Breya**: *"I told you we should have hired a thief."*
:   **Fathoms**: *"We are thieves, you fool. We're stealing the cube."*
:   **Breya**: *"And yet none of us can pick a damned lock."*

In Avanchnzel Animoncultory at the campsite:

:   **Drennen**: *"This place is huge."*
:   **Roots**: *"It is large, indeed. I did not anticipate Avanchnzel's size or the time needed to uncover the entrance. A few hours sleep and we should be ready to continue through."*
:   **Drennen**: *"Maybe we should turn back. I don't want to sleep here."*
:   **Roots**: *"Drennen, you do understand that the Lexicon at the bottom of this place holds the accumulated memories of centuries of Dwemer."*
:   **Breya**: *"Not to mention our pay."*
:   **Drennen**: *"So?"*
:   **Fathoms**: *"So we're not turning back, you fool."*
:   **Breya**: *"Besides, you're not afraid of a few sleeping metal men. Are you, Drennen?"*

Further in the Animoncultory in a storage room:

:   **Breya**: *"I thought you said these things were "sleeping"?"*
:   **Roots**: *"You said they were sleeping. I said they were waiting. It seems a few of them were "waiting" for someone to try and take the Lexicon."*
:   **Breya**: *"Great."*

Just before the doors to the Avanchnzel Boilery:

:   **Drennen**: *"I can't do this. We shouldn't be here. I'm sorry."*
:   **Breya**: *"Drennen!"*
:   **Fathoms**: *"Let the field mouse run. Your pay will be double."*
:   **Breya**: *"My pay will be nothing if we die in here!"*
:   **Roots**: *"Calm yourself, Breya. We are closing in on the Lexicon. I can feel it calling. We'll continue without Drennen."*

As you enter the Boilery:

:   **Roots**: *"We are close now. Can you feel the Lexicon calling out?"*
:   **Fathoms**: *"Sure."*
:   **Breya**: *"So we get it and get out, right?"*
:   **Roots**: *"Once we have the Lexicon, we'll need to take it to its podium. I know what to do from there. Soon the Lexicon's knowledge will be mine."*
:   **Fathoms**: *"Ours. Soon the Lexicon's knowledge will be ours."*
:   **Roots**: *"Of course."*

Just before the trapped room where you find Watches-The-Roots' body:

:   **Roots**: *"We're almost there. I can hear the Lexicon. Come on, quickly!"*
:   **Breya**: *"Something doesn't feel right. Wait!"*
:   **Roots**: *"Aaaaaaaaaaa...."*

## Notes

- There are 13 different dialogue scenes set up for the quest Unfathomable Depths, but not all of them contain dialogue. The first scene **MS04Vision01Scene**, appears to have been a conversation between Fathoms and Breya, but its contents are unknown. Scene 7 **MS04Vision07Scene** also has a single entry for Breya alone, but no accompanying dialogue.
- Unused scripting in the quest would've given every member of the party a full set of Dwarven armor, although this never happens, and it's unknown what purpose this would've served.

## Bugs

- A scene near the giant Dwemer factory may be missing, since the trigger for it is located outside of the map. **?**

:   **Fathoms**: *"The Lexicon had better be worth all this trouble."*
:   **Roots**: *"I assure you, it is. The knowledge contained in the Lexicon created everything you see around you. Properly controlled, it has knowledge enough to turn paupers into kings."*
:   **Drennen**: *"You sure that's power we're meant to have?"*
:   **Roots**: *"Absolutely."*

- Due to a spelling error in the game code, the final scene near the Centurion will never play as intended. It was meant to describe the death of Breya and how Fathoms escaped:

:   **Fathoms**: *"I have the Lexicon! Where's the podium?"*
:   **Breya**: *"I can't hold these things! We need to leave!"*
:   **Fathoms**:*"I did not come all the way here just to walk out empty-handed."*
:   **Breya**:*"The way out is right there! Run, damn it!"*

- This scene was originally fixed by version 1.3.3. of the Unofficial Skyrim Patch, however, this was reverted by version 2.0.0., due to the changes actually breaking the scene further.

# Skyrim:Briarheart Necropsy

## Overview

[Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") wants to know the secret

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Talk to [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)").
2. Find a [Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart") of the [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn").
3. Return to Neloth for your reward.

### The Briarhearts

When you ask [Neloth](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth "Skyrim:Neloth") if you can help him with his research, he may respond: *"I've been having difficulties with my heart stone experiments. Have you heard of the Briarhearts? They are fierce warriors of the Forsworn tribes. They actually remove their own hearts, and replace them with large briar seeds. It puts their lifesparks in direct connection to the natural forces. I need you to examine one of them. Just investigate as much as you can. I'm going to put this memory trace spell on you, so you won't have to worry about taking notes. I doubt you could know what was important anyway."* He then reveals that he has been experimenting with similar theories but all his test subjects died in the process. Lastly, he will point you towards Skyrim and [The Reach](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reach "Skyrim:The Reach") to find a specimen in a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") hideout. Before you leave, he will cast [Neloth's Memory Spell](/wiki/Skyrim:Neloth%27s_Memory_Spell "Skyrim:Neloth's Memory Spell") so you can remember what you observe.

### Harvest a Heart

You will have to travel all the way back to Skyrim, so hire the boat in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") or simply fast travel to [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). Then go west to the Reach, where hold capital [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") has its fair share of problems with the Forsworn. They can be found in most locations where the Forsworn have set up camp, such as [Lost Valley Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Valley_Redoubt "Skyrim:Lost Valley Redoubt"), [Broken Tower Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Redoubt "Skyrim:Broken Tower Redoubt"), or [Hag Rock Redoubt](/wiki/Skyrim:Hag_Rock_Redoubt "Skyrim:Hag Rock Redoubt"). After you have killed a Forsworn Briarheart you will be given two options, either "Harvest" or "Search". Choose "Harvest" and the quest will update and tell you to return to Neloth on Solstheim.

### Extracting Memories

Back in [Tel Mithryn](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(settlement) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (settlement)"), a trio of [ash spawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Spawn "Skyrim:Ash Spawn") will be waiting outside to attack upon your return. Inside his [tower](/wiki/Skyrim:Tel_Mithryn_(tower) "Skyrim:Tel Mithryn (tower)"), Neloth will be awaiting your arrival. When you tell him you examined the Briarheart warrior, he will comment: *"Oh have you? Well, let me just extract those memories and I'll see if you found anything useful. I promise that any unrelated memories I run across will be kept in the strictest of confidences. Here, you deserve a bit of reward for your efforts... that was a lengthy trip for you, I'm sure!"* He will then hand you 250 gold for all your hard work and the time you spent traveling back and forth.

## Notes

- Pickpocketing a Forsworn Briarheart for its briar heart will not give you the option to "Harvest" when trying to loot its body. You must kill it in another way.

## Bugs

- After the quest is finished it is possible for Briar Hearts you acquire to be erroneously marked quest items making them impossible to remove from your inventory, even though the quest has been completed.
  - It is possible to fix this by completing [Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial"), if it is in progress. Note that the quest may be considered in progress if the player has received the [Letter from Quintus Navale](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Quintus_Navale "Skyrim:Letter from Quintus Navale") after completing [The White Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Phial_(quest) "Skyrim:The White Phial (quest)") but has not yet read it to initiate [Repairing the Phial](/wiki/Skyrim:Repairing_the_Phial "Skyrim:Repairing the Phial").
- The Briarheart body may not swap the body for the one with no Briar Heart inside due to an error in the quest specific perk script assigned to it.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.1.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Briarheart Necropsy (DLC2TTR5) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 100 |  | Neloth has asked me to examine a Briarheart warrior of the Forsworn tribes. He couldn't direct me to a specific one, but he said they live in the hills on the western edge of Skyrim. *Objective 100:* Examine a Briarheart warrior |
| 200 |  | Neloth has asked me to examine a Briarheart warrior of the Forsworn tribes. I found one and saw how the heart was implanted. *Objective 200:* Talk to Neloth |
| 300 | ☑ |  |

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage DLC2TTR5 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest DLC2TTR5`.

# Skyrim:Briehl

## Overview

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [CrimeFactionRift](/wiki/Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift "Skyrim:CrimeFactionRift"); [Riften Temple of Mara Faction](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften_Temple_of_Mara_Faction "Skyrim:Riften Temple of Mara Faction"); [TownRiftenFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction "Skyrim:TownRiftenFaction") | | |

Briehl enjoying a relaxing drink

**Briehl**, a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"), is an acolyte at the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), where he works under [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu") and [Maramal](/wiki/Skyrim:Maramal "Skyrim:Maramal").

Briehl never leaves the Temple of Mara and will wander around the chapel day and night, at random times eating, sleeping, conversing, or cooking. During the wedding ceremonies held at the Chapel, Briehl will sit silently in attendance while Maramal performs the ceremony.

His only possessions are the clothes he is wearing, a set of [monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Monk Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Boots").

## Dialogue

:   **Which of the Eight Divines do you serve?**
:   *"This temple is dedicated to Mara, and the light of love she shines on us all. I'm only a humble acolyte, though. If you wish to avail yourself of Mara's blessing, you should speak with Dinya Balu or Maramal."*

If you are doing the quest [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love") for Dinya, he will add:

:   *"They should be back shortly. You're welcome to wait here if you like."*

## Notes

- Briehl does not have a unique facial model, he instead uses the default male Nord face. He shares this quirk with numerous other NPCs, including [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur"), [Sond](/wiki/Skyrim:Sond_(bandit) "Skyrim:Sond (bandit)"), [Lynoit](/wiki/Skyrim:Lynoit "Skyrim:Lynoit"), [Barknar](/wiki/Skyrim:Barknar_(Dawnguard) "Skyrim:Barknar (Dawnguard)"), and many other generic NPCs.

# Skyrim:Brill

## Overview

| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001A6A3 | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001A6A2 |

Brill in Jorrvaskr

**Brill** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), and can be found in either [Jorrvaskr](/wiki/Skyrim:Jorrvaskr "Skyrim:Jorrvaskr") or [Dragonsreach](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonsreach "Skyrim:Dragonsreach"), depending on the status of the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War").

Brill wears a set of farm [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006c1d8 "Skyrim:Clothing") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0003452f "Skyrim:Clothing"). He wields a [Skyforge steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Skyforge_Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Skyforge Steel Dagger") and carries a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

Brill is frequently seen in the company of [Vignar Gray-Mane](/wiki/Skyrim:Vignar_Gray-Mane "Skyrim:Vignar Gray-Mane"), to whom he owes a debt of gratitude for saving him from a troubled lifestyle. He sees Vignar as a father figure, and acts as his aide. Consequently, if the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") take over Whiterun and install Vignar as the new Jarl in place of [Balgruuf](/wiki/Skyrim:Balgruuf_the_Greater "Skyrim:Balgruuf the Greater"), then Brill will likewise replace [Proventus](/wiki/Skyrim:Proventus_Avenicci "Skyrim:Proventus Avenicci") as the steward of Dragonsreach. Like Avenicci, he will sell [Breezehome](/wiki/Skyrim:Breezehome "Skyrim:Breezehome") and its furnishings, as well as [Tundra Homestead](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Homestead_(place) "Skyrim:Tundra Homestead (place)")[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Homestead "Skyrim:Tundra Homestead").

## Dialogue

His greetings:

:   *"I'd be dead if not for Vignar. He took me in and helped me turn my life around."*
:   *"I had a bad time a few years back, an' I turned to drink. But Vignar, he wouldn't let me stay weak."*
:   *"Ah, hello my good friend. Would you do me a kindness? I seem to be down to my last drop of spirits. Let me tell you, sobriety is highly overrated."*

If there is a fight going on in Jorrvaskr he can say:

:   *"Could you move? You're in the way."*
:   *"Hope they don't get carried away here."*
:   *"Good fight going, here."*
:   *"Great, back to the fight."*

When spoken to:

:   **Why did you join the Companions?**
:   *"Oh, I'm not a Companion, myself. I just help Vignar. He took me in when I was having a tough time, and... well, I owe him."*

:   **There's still the threat of a dragon attack.**
:   *"And we've done as much as we can to prepare for that. But remember, Whiterun is home to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions"). Any dragon that comes here will get more than he's bargained for, I think."*

:   **Who are the Companions?**
:   *"To hear Vignar tell it, they're a bunch of layabouts and useless whiners who used to know how to fight. But he thinks everything used to be better. I, for one, would trust any Companion with my life."*

His goodbyes:

:   *"Take care."*
:   *"Farewell, sir."*
:   *"Farewell, my lady."*

### Steward Dialogue

His new greetings:

:   *"Vignar and I have our hands full. It's no small task, running an entire hold."*
:   *"When I became Steward, I had to give up the bottle. The people of the hold need me at my best."*

When spoken to:

:   **You must have your hands full with the change in government.**
:   *"Well, it could be worse. The former steward, Proventus, kept very detailed records. But yes, it's been a lot of work. Vignar doesn't want the change to disrupt the lives of his people. They've got enough to deal with already"*

Brill may comment on a [dragon](/wiki/Skyrim:Odahviing "Skyrim:Odahviing")'s [capture](/wiki/Skyrim:The_World-Eater%27s_Eyrie "Skyrim:The World-Eater's Eyrie") atop Dragonsreach:

:   *"Capturing that dragon was a mighty deed. In my younger days, I'd have been the first to join in the attempt."*

## Conversations

*"That's just you getting skinnier every day, old man."*

**Vignar**: *"You ain't made me that stew in a long time."*
**Brill**: *"Which, the mutton or the vegetable?"*
**Vignar**: *"Mutton."*
**Brill**: *"Hmm. So I haven't. All right, I'll buy the ingredients tomorrow and we can have it for dinner."*

**Brill**: *"Fancy a game of Iron Hearts later?"*
**Vignar**: *"You going to lose horribly, and then say you let me win?"*
**Brill**: *"Probably."*
**Vignar**: *"Then you're on."*

**Vignar**: *"There's a chill in the air. Ysmir's beard, it gets colder in here every day."*
**Brill**: *"That's just you getting skinnier every day, old man. You're losing your padding. You need to eat more."*
**Vignar**: *"Well if my layabout manservant fed me more, that wouldn't be a problem."*
**Brill**: *"Oho! Manservant? Is that what I am now?"*
**Vignar**: *"My mistake. A manservant wouldn't let me starve or freeze. I let you live here, and now I'm two steps closer to the grave."*
**Brill**: *"Old man, without me, you would have withered away a long time ago."*
**Vignar**: *"Hmph. Damn you for being right."*

## Notes

- Brill can be told that there is still the threat of a dragon attack before Mirmulnir attacks. Additionally, his reply makes little sense unless he is steward. Nonetheless, this dialogue is always available.

## Bugs

- If Brill is killed while he is steward to Vignar Gray-Mane (after the [Battle for Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Whiterun_(Stormcloaks) "Skyrim:Battle for Whiterun (Stormcloaks)")), Proventus Avenicci will return from exile to replace him in this position. He will offer the same dialogue as if Jarl Balgruuf still controlled Whiterun.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, addresses this issue. Like other stewards, Brill has been made [essential](/wiki/Skyrim:Essential_NPCs "Skyrim:Essential NPCs").
- Brill may not replace Proventus Avenicci as steward. **?**
- Attacking Brill may reward you with bounties in wrong holds, like The Reach and Eastmarch. **?**

Brina Merilis

*"The Jarl and I have our disagreements."*

**Brina Merilis** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") who owns a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina%27s_House "Skyrim:Brina's House") in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"). She is a retired [Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") legate and fought in the [Great War](/wiki/Lore:Great_War "Lore:Great War"), and her former subordinate [Horik Halfhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Horik_Halfhand "Skyrim:Horik Halfhand") still follows her around at all times. Brina will become [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Dawnstar should you side with the Legion in the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War") and take control of the Pale from the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks"). If she is deposed again, she and Horik will take residence in [the Winking Skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Winking_Skeever "Skyrim:The Winking Skeever").

She gets out of bed at 8am and always starts the day with a one-hour breakfast with Horik. She then leaves the house and starts patrolling around town. She pauses at noon and 6pm for one-hour meals. At 8pm she returns to her house and spends a bit of time with Horik before she goes to bed at midnight. If she is appointed Jarl, she will abandon her house and move into the White Hall, still with Horik by her side as [Housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl"). She holds court every day between 8am and midnight.

She wears upper class attire, specifically [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000f8715 "Skyrim:Clothing") and [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000cee82 "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), her [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Brina%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Brina's House"), and a selection of [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Thane of the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_the_Pale "Skyrim:Thane of the Pale")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [the Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

When you enter Dawnstar for the first time, you will witness her having a heated argument with Skald the Elder in front of the jarl's hall. Like all other Dawnstar citizens, Brina has trouble sleeping before [Waking Nightmare](/wiki/Skyrim:Waking_Nightmare "Skyrim:Waking Nightmare") is complete. She can tell you about the issue.

:   *"You come to Dawnstar at a bad time. Tempers are... fiery."*
:   **I came at a bad time? What's wrong?**
:   *"Not a single man or woman in Dawnstar has gotten a good night's rest in days. We keep having the same nightmare, over and over.
    If people aren't tired, they're angry, and if they aren't angry, they're afraid. It's made keeping order a mess.
    I hear [Mara](/wiki/Lore:Mara "Lore:Mara") has sent one of her [priests](/wiki/Skyrim:Erandur "Skyrim:Erandur") to the inn to try to calm people down, but I don't know how much words will do now."*

She will also apologize for the public argument with Skald.

:   *"The Jarl and I have our disagreements. Sorry if you had to overhear one of them."*
:   **Did I see you arguing with someone?**
:   *"Skald supports Ulfric's rebellion, and he doesn't like having a couple of old Legionnaires living in his town.
    He's a fool. A dragon has attacked [Helgen](/wiki/Skyrim:Helgen "Skyrim:Helgen"). Dawnstar needs the Empire now more than ever."*

Lastly, she will readily provide information on where to drink and where to work.

:   **I was looking for a drink. Or some work.**
:   *"Drowning your troubles in mead? A lot of folks are doing that these days. You'll want the [Windpeak Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Windpeak_Inn "Skyrim:Windpeak Inn").
    As for work, you could try to catch Skald in a good mood, but your best bet would be working in the mines. They're on opposite ends of town."*

She has several other greetings.

:   *"I wasn't born in Skyrim, but when I served in the Legion this land became my home."*

:   *"Horik and I have lived here ever since I retired. He's a good soldier."*

When you exit a conversation with her, she may say:

:   *"Stay out of trouble, now."*

*"I will serve Dawnstar as I always have."*

If she is appointed jarl, she seems confident in her ability to rule.

:   *"I will serve Dawnstar as I always have."*

:   *"You should see the grin on Horik's face now that we're in charge. I know he hides it, but I can tell."*

If you ask her about the safety of Dawnstar from [dragons](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon "Skyrim:Dragon") she will tell you the worrying truth. You can also ask her about the war, to which she'll give you a summary of how it's going.

:   **Is Dawnstar prepared for dragon attacks?**
:   *"No. We're completely exposed. Bows and arrows are in short supply. Every building is made of thatch and wood.
    I've given standing orders to the guards to prepare water bucket runs to the harbor in case of a fire, but that's all we can do."*
:   **How's the war going?**
:   *"The Empire has stretched itself too far. This rebellion in Skyrim is one problem, but solving it won't fix everything.
    But that's the kind of talk an old warhorse shouldn't be making. Don't worry. I have my problems with the Empire, but I'm still a soldier first.
    We'll keep peace and order in Dawnstar."*

### Conversations

The current Jarl of Dawnstar, [Skald the Elder](/wiki/Skyrim:Skald "Skyrim:Skald"), is a staunch Stormcloak supporter, and spends most of his funds and personnel to help [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") battle the Legion. Brina can do very little about it, although she tries. When you arrive in Dawnstar for the first time, you will find her outside [the White Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:The_White_Hall "Skyrim:The White Hall"), engaged in a hefty argument with Skald:

:   **Brina:** *"Divines*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *sake, Skald. Who do you think we're threatening with our old war wounds? We're not soldiers, anymore."*
:   **Skald:** *"Your man Horik is wearing his old Legion armor. What should I make of that?"*
:   **Brina:** *"He's proud of his service, Skald. The Legion taught us loyalty. And we're loyal to Dawnstar."*
:   **Skald:** *"This isn't over. I catch you sending one letter to [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius"), I'll have you both executed."*

After the argument, Brina will return to her regular duties.

After a long day of patrolling, she will often have conversations with her old friend Horik when they spend time in the house before bedtime. Horik occasionally asks Brina how she's holding up.

*"I'm fine, Horik. I just... are you worried about this war?"*

:   **Horik:** *"Are you all right? You seem tired."*
:   **Brina:** *"I'm fine, Horik. I just... are you worried about this war?"*
:   **Horik:** *"No. If we must fight, we will, and you will lead us to victory. As you always have."*
:   **Brina:** *"With you by my side, is that right Horik?"*
:   **Horik:** *"Of course. I would have it no other way."*
:   **Brina:** *"So much for old soldiers settling down to a life of luxury, eh?"*

Sometimes, Brina asks Horik about himself.

:   **Brina:** *"You never talk much about yourself, do you Horik? I swear, these past 30 years you've been at my side, and I think I barely know you."*
:   **Horik:** *"What's to say? I was born on a farm, joined the Legion when I came of age, and I've served you ever since."*
:   **Brina:** *"What about your family? There must have been someone waiting for you back at the farm. Wondering if you were ever coming home?"*
:   **Horik:** *"No. Can't say there was. My parents died when I was young. You and the Legion have been my only family since."*
:   **Brina:** *"I see. You're a good soldier, Horik. I'm sorry for intruding."*
:   **Horik:** *"You weren't. There's just not much to it."*

The staff in the White Hall will also notice the difference between their new jarl and her predecessor. While Skald the Elder spent all day trying to persuade his [court wizard](/wiki/Skyrim:Court_Wizard "Skyrim:Court Wizard") to aid the Stormcloaks, Brina takes a more peaceful approach.

:   **Brina:** *"[Madena](/wiki/Skyrim:Madena "Skyrim:Madena"), I was wondering if you could help me with something. Your magic would be invaluable."*
:   **Madena:** *"If this is about battle magic, forget it. I've told every Jarl I've served under that I won't...."*
:   **Brina:** *"Actually, I was just wondering if you could make sure people are tended to if they get hurt. I'm sure you wouldn't object to that."*
:   **Madena:** *"I, well, no of course not. I would be glad to help."*
:   **Brina:** *"Thank you, Madena. I appreciate your assistance."*

Brina and Horik's relationship will also change somewhat, with new responsibilities and more formality.

:   **Brina:** *"Just like old times, huh Horik? You and me fighting in a war over some forsaken scrap of land."*
:   **Horik:** *"Brings back memories. Do you have any orders for me, Legate?"*
:   **Brina:** *"Keep the guard alert. I want to make sure no townspeople get hurt if there's trouble."*
:   **Horik:** *"Yes, Legate. No one is getting through us."*
:   **Brina:** *"Shor's bones, I hope you're right."*

Horik and Brina occasionally talk about the ongoing civil war.

:   **Horik:** *"We should go over our strategy again in case the Stormcloaks attack."*
:   **Brina:** *"I don't think that's needed, Horik. It's the same strategy we used for every major defense during the Great War. It'll serve just as well now."*
:   **Horik:** *"Considering how the Great War ended, I think we need to be cautious about what we rely on."*
:   **Brina:** *"Maybe you're right. I guess the battles I won yesterday won't win today's wars."*
:   **Horik:** *"I'm sorry, Legate. I didn't want to imply anything about your ability to lead. You're a hero to the Empire, and I...."*
:   **Brina:** *"Oh, don't be such an old stick, Horik. I was joking. I can do that, you know. Redo the battle plans. I'll look over them later."*
:   **Horik:** *"Yes, Legate."*

## Notes

- In the *[Prima Official Game Guide](/wiki/Books:The_Elder_Scrolls_V:_Skyrim:_Prima_Official_Game_Guide "Books:The Elder Scrolls V: Skyrim: Prima Official Game Guide")*, the summary for her reads:

:   *"Brina was once renowned throughout the Legion for her leadership and her tactical ability. She is a stern woman who tolerates no foolishness from those under her command. She does have a warm side that sometimes shows through, although it is rarely seen since the start of the war."*

- The court of Dawnstar, whether under the control of Skald or Brina Merilis, is the only one that doesn't employ the services of a steward.
- Although Brina says she was not born in Skyrim, she seems to have moved there early, as [Frida](/wiki/Skyrim:Frida "Skyrim:Frida")'s dialogue indicates Brina having been a respected citizen of Dawnstar since well before the Great War.
- Game data lists Brina's relationship with Horik as lovers, as their relationship rank is 4.

## Bugs

- [Bounty quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty_Quests "Skyrim:Bounty Quests") turned in to Brina will not be removed from the quest journal upon completion, and cannot be removed with the console.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- Both beds at Brina's house are marked as owned by her, making it impossible for Horik to sleep when they're there.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.
- With [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire"), when she is made Jarl, Brina may be asked if the property she mentioned is still available, even if she hasn't mentioned it before.
  -  The [Unofficial Hearthfire Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Hearthfire_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Hearthfire Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- If Dawnstar is transferred to Legion control via Season Unending or completion of the Civil War in favor of the Empire before visiting Dawnstar and witnessing Brina's argument with Jarl Skald, she may stand on the steps of the longhouse permanently. This will not affect her dialogue or any quest related behavior.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

:   -  Bypass the conversation by using the console to `SetStage DialogueDawnstarIntroBrinaHorikSkaldScene 100`.

# Skyrim:Brina's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Brina's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brina%27s+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| *[The Importance of Where](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Importance_of_Where "Skyrim:The Importance of Where")* | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DawnstarBrinasHouse | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| Center of [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Brina's House

**Brina's House** is a small house in [Dawnstar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnstar "Skyrim:Dawnstar"), located next to [Leigelf's House](/wiki/Skyrim:Leigelf%27s_House "Skyrim:Leigelf's House"), opposite [The Mortar and Pestle](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mortar_and_Pestle "Skyrim:The Mortar and Pestle").

It is the home of [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") and her guard, [Horik Halfhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Horik_Halfhand "Skyrim:Horik Halfhand"). It consists of one area only: *[Brina's House](#Brina.27s_House)*.

This house will be permanently abandoned if [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") is given to the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") in [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and subsequently retaken by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Brina Merilis](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis")\*  [Horik Halfhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Horik_Halfhand "Skyrim:Horik Halfhand")\* |

\* These people will be no longer available if [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") is given to the [Empire](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion") in [Season Unending](/wiki/Skyrim:Season_Unending "Skyrim:Season Unending") and subsequently retaken by the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

### Exterior

The house faces the bay, with a decking out front. There is a pile of firewood on the left side of the decking, and a wooden bench on the right. The house is protected by a novice lock when neither of its inhabitants are home; [Horik Halfhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Horik_Halfhand "Skyrim:Horik Halfhand") acts as [Brina Merilis's](/wiki/Skyrim:Brina_Merilis "Skyrim:Brina Merilis") [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") or bodyguard, and as such travels around the town with her at all times.

### Brina's House

Brina's home

The house is a typical one-room dwelling. On the left as you enter, there is a chair and [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrel in the corner. Next to them, against the east wall, is a cupboard holding four bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") and two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). There is another collection of barrels in the southeastern corner. Against the south wall, there is a long wooden table with two bottles of alto wine and a single bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top. Hanging above the table are three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), and a rack holding three [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). Further along on the right is a food barrel and a set of shelves holding four more bottles of alto wine and four bottles of wine. To the right of this, still on the south wall, lies a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and a kettle containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") placed on the hearth. To the right of the fireplace is a pile of firewood and a basket containing a copy of the [One-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "Skyrim:One-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Importance of Where](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Importance_of_Where "Skyrim:The Importance of Where")*.

Coming out of the west wall are two owned single beds, with an end table holding a bottle of Nord mead and an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of each bed, both of which contain leveled items. Against the north wall is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), with a [steel mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Mace "Skyrim:Steel Mace") placed on top. To the right of the wardrobe, next to the door, is a small round wooden table and two chairs. On the table is a bottle of alto wine, a bottle of wine and two loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread").

## Notes

- With the exception of most barrels and sacks, all containers in the house are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- Both beds are marked as owned by Brina, making it impossible for Horik to sleep when they're here.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Brinewater Grotto

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Brinewater Grotto ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brinewater+Grotto)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | No |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |
| [Horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker"), [Frostbite Spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"), [Dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog"), [Bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") (see [notes](#Notes)) | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BrinewaterGrottoExterior, BrinewaterGrottoStart | |
| Region | |
| [Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Haafingar "Skyrim:Haafingar") | |
| Location | |
| North of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") Southeast of [Broken Oar Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Oar_Grotto "Skyrim:Broken Oar Grotto") | |

Brinewater Grotto

**Brinewater Grotto** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [horkers](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker "Skyrim:Horker") or [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains only one zone, *[Brinewater Grotto](#Brinewater_Grotto)*.

Before the quest [Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly"), it is simply a small cave that is home to three horkers, with the rest of the grotto inaccessible (see [Notes](#Notes) for a workaround). During the quest, it will be occupied by bandits.

## Related Quests

- **[Scoundrel's Folly](/wiki/Skyrim:Scoundrel%27s_Folly "Skyrim:Scoundrel's Folly")**: Squeeze a [reluctant informer](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") for information.

### Exterior

Brinewater Grotto is on the coast near the path that leads to [Solitude Lighthouse](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Lighthouse "Skyrim:Solitude Lighthouse"). As you approach the lighthouse, the path splits, with a branch to the northwest leading past a small jetty with a rowboat moored to it. At the end of the branching path is a lantern hanging from a post. There is an unlocked wooden [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") beside a barrel in a corner of the rock face to the left. On the barrel is an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and two loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). The entrance is just to the left of the barrel and chest.

### Brinewater Grotto

There is quite a bit of vegetation throughout the cave; however, none of it is harvestable. The main floor is shallowly flooded, with several rock pillars supporting the roof, and a ledge around most of the cave. There is a concealed stone door in the western wall when entering the cave near the lighthouse, but you cannot open the door from this side; it will serve as your exit at the end of the related quest (see [notes](#Notes)). The ledge in this small area can be reached by jumping from a rock to the left of this door, although there is nothing of interest on the ledge. During the related quest, you will enter the cave from the [East Empire Company Warehouse](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Warehouse "Skyrim:East Empire Company Warehouse").

Entering through the East Empire Company Warehouse leads into a tunnel with a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") a short distance along that triggers a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap. Ahead you will hear two bandits talking; they are standing on a jetty behind shelves stacked with crates stamped with the East Empire Company logo. There is a [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") on the ground at the exit of the tunnel. The cave seems to be long and narrow, with the left half a deep stream allowing small rowboats to navigate; hence the jetty. Among the crates on the shelves are nine bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), seven bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), a [silver ingot](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ingot "Skyrim:Silver Ingot"), five [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), two random [potions of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), two random [potions of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Strength "Skyrim:Potion of Strength"), and a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina").

At the end of the shelves is a narrow flight of wooden stairs next to an opening blocked by thick cobwebs that you can cut or burn through. Behind the cobwebs is a short tunnel leading to more thick cobwebs; a small cave beyond the second set of cobwebs contains three [frostbite spiders](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Spider "Skyrim:Frostbite Spider"). On the other side of the small cave is another tunnel past two more sets of thick cobwebs that opens on a ledge back in the main area, serving as a shortcut through a section of the main area.

Return to the stairs and climb them to a wooden platform, lit by widely spaced [torches](/wiki/Skyrim:Torch "Skyrim:Torch") that can be taken to darken the cave and help conceal you. Ahead you can see two bandits; one is a magic user. Just past the bandits, under the water to the left is an unlocked chest containing minor loot. There are wooden steps leading down into the water that you can use to regain the path. On your right is the ledge where the spider cave exits, with stairs leading down from the ledge. Ahead is a wooden bridge crossing to the other side of the water, and on the far side is a bandit archer. A short distance farther along is an opening on your left leading into a brightly lit area, with a tripwire partway along that triggers another swinging mace, and another tripwire and mace at the far end. Between the two tripwires are two bear traps hidden among vegetation. Just past the second tripwire is a [dog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dog "Skyrim:Dog") that you can hear barking, and possibly a dead [skeever](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeever "Skyrim:Skeever"). There are [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ceiling near the dog, and a piece of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat") on the ground in a wooden bowl. The tunnel emerges back into the main area opposite a campfire, with several [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels all around and two bandits standing by the fire.

Staying in the main area instead of turning left and entering the side tunnel, the path winds around a corner before recrossing the water to the right-hand side, leading to a platform and stairs down. On your left are more stairs that lead down into the water, with another bear trap at the top. Around another corner is the campfire and crossing near the exit from the side tunnel, accessed on the left over an earthen bridge. There are several food barrels and an adept-locked chest by the fire, and two metal pots each containing two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish") steaks hanging over the fire. There is a rock pillar between the fire and the stream, and a pressure plate behind the pillar that triggers a [battering ram](/wiki/Skyrim:Battering_Ram "Skyrim:Battering Ram") to stop anyone trying to sneak past the guards from the side tunnel. Ahead is another wooden bridge crossing the water, with bone chimes hanging under it to catch anyone trying to sneak through the water. The bridge crosses to a small ledge, with bone chimes hanging from the ceiling by another bridge that crosses back to the final area. Beyond the second bridge are two rowboats moored to another small jetty, with a bandit standing nearby and another patrolling the area. The rowboats each hold a chest, one apprentice-locked, and the other unlocked. Under the water throughout the length of the cave are many clusters of [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), although there are no [slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Slaughterfish").

To the east is a large area with shelves stacked on either side, another campfire in the middle, and several large cages along the back wall. [Gulum-Ei](/wiki/Skyrim:Gulum-Ei "Skyrim:Gulum-Ei") and yet another bandit are standing by the fire. Just before the fire, by a rock pillar on the left, is a long wooden table with benches on either side. There are two bowls of [horker stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Stew "Skyrim:Horker Stew"), a seared slaughterfish steak, a slaughterfish egg, and some [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales") on the table. Opposite the table are some wide wooden stairs leading up and behind the shelves on the right to a ledge, where four unowned bedrolls and a barrel with an [eidar cheese wedge](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge") on top are found. There is a random cuirass on one of the shelves that can only be reached from this ledge. Dropping off the western edge of the ledge leads you to a smaller ledge, with two small [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") on the ground.

From the ground, the right-hand shelves hold three chests: one is on the ground and is unlocked, and the next with an expert lock is on the first shelf, along with a leveled enchanted dagger, a random helmet, and a random cuirass. There is an angled ladder you can climb to retrieve an empty random soul gem and a [Dibella statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dibella_Statue "Skyrim:Dibella Statue") from the second shelf; the third chest is also unlocked, and is on the third shelf with a [Markarth guard's shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Guard%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Markarth Guard's Shield") and a [Solitude guard's shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude_Guard%27s_Shield "Skyrim:Solitude Guard's Shield"). The shelves on the left hold two more chests, one master-locked, the other expert-locked. Also on these shelves is a random shield, six common [books](/wiki/Skyrim:Books "Skyrim:Books") in an open crate, two random swords, a random war axe, and copies of some rarer books: *[Hanging Gardens](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Gardens "Skyrim:Hanging Gardens")*, *[2920, Evening Star, v12](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Evening_Star,_v12 "Skyrim:2920, Evening Star, v12")*, *[Wraith's Wedding Dowry](/wiki/Skyrim:Wraith%27s_Wedding_Dowry "Skyrim:Wraith's Wedding Dowry")*, and *[Children of the Sky](/wiki/Skyrim:Children_of_the_Sky "Skyrim:Children of the Sky")*. To the east are three levers that open two large cages as well as a concealed door between them. Nearby is a crate with three fillets of horker meat and three [horker tusks](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk") on top, and a bucket containing two [salmon](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_(dead) "Skyrim:Salmon (dead)") beside it. The cages contain a total of five more salmon. The concealed door opens to reveal the small section of the cave that can be accessed from the entrance near the lighthouse.

## Notes

- The bandits don't respawn and the concealed exit doesn't reset to the closed position, allowing you to enter the cave near Solitude Lighthouse and easily loot the entire cave once the items found inside the cave have respawned.
- The related quest won't advance if you enter the cave near the lighthouse. Enter instead from the East Empire Company Warehouse.
- If you enter the cave near the lighthouse, you can glitch through the concealed stone door by holding a wooden plate against it then running against the plate or using the [Whirlwind Sprint](/wiki/Skyrim:Whirlwind_Sprint "Skyrim:Whirlwind Sprint") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts") until you clip through the door; you may then activate the middle lever beyond the wooden gate to open the door. The loot will be intact, but the bandits that occupy the cave during the related quest won't be present, making the three frostbite spiders and the dog the only enemies in the entire cave.
  - If you glitch through the stone door, don't approach the door to the East Empire Company Warehouse too closely, as it will be key-locked (and unpickable) and getting too close will start a broken version of the related quest: there will be no quest description, and since Gulum-Ei won't be present anywhere, the game will direct you to [The Ragged Flagon - Cistern](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ragged_Flagon_-_Cistern "Skyrim:The Ragged Flagon - Cistern"), which isn't accessible unless you join the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)"). To exit the cave, you will need to return to the entrance near the lighthouse.

## Bugs

- The swinging maces may already be hanging down, even though the tripwires are still intact.
- You may only be able to manually open and close one of the metal cage doors after activating the corresponding lever. **?**
- If you exit the cave and then reload a save file from inside, the Markarth and Solitude guard's shields may not spawn where they should. Exiting to the main menu and reloading the game from there should resolve the issue. **?**
- The dog here isn't attached to the bandit enable marker and respawns when the bandits themselves don't.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Brinewater Grotto

# Skyrim:Bring It!

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Deliver [Harrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Harrald "Skyrim:Harrald")'s sword.** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Harrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Harrald "Skyrim:Harrald") |
| Location(s): | [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep") |
| Reward: | Two [leveled](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems#Valuable_Gems "Skyrim:Gems") gems |
| [Disposition](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition"): | min 1 ([Harrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Harrald "Skyrim:Harrald"), only happens when install ussep) |
| ID: | FreeformRiften16 |

Only a dagger for the son of the jarl?

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Speak to [Harrald](/wiki/Skyrim:Harrald "Skyrim:Harrald") in [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep").
2. Retrieve his blade from [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund").
3. Return to Harrald.

### The Slain Wall

Harrald is the son of Jarl [Laila Law-Giver](/wiki/Skyrim:Laila_Law-Giver "Skyrim:Laila Law-Giver") and lives in [Mistveil Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Mistveil_Keep "Skyrim:Mistveil Keep") in [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"). Take a look at him and you may find something strange. As the son of the jarl, he has only a dagger. If you ask him, he will tell you why: *"I was practicing in the yard when the guard I was sparring with feinted when I specifically told him to duck! My blade bit right into the stonework next to the keep and needed serious repairs."* He'd like you to fetch his blade from [Balimund](/wiki/Skyrim:Balimund "Skyrim:Balimund").

Talk to Balimund right outside [The Scorched Hammer](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Scorched_Hammer "Skyrim:The Scorched Hammer"), "a stone's throw" from the keep. He will give the sword to you and comment on Harrald's laziness and carelessness.

Hand over the sword to Harrald and he will be rather ungrateful. *"Took your sweet time getting it to me. Here you go, for your trouble."* He will then reward you with two [leveled](/wiki/Skyrim:Gems#Valuable_Gems "Skyrim:Gems") gems.

## Notes

- Although this is not a [favor quest](/wiki/Skyrim:Favors "Skyrim:Favors"), it does count towards [becoming thane](/wiki/Skyrim:I_Done_Got_Thaned! "Skyrim:I Done Got Thaned!").

## Bugs

- After you finsh the quest, Harrald's disposition towards you won't improve.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 4.3.2, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Bring It! (FreeformRiften16) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 20 |  | *Objective 10:* Pick up Harrald's Sword from Balimund |
| 30 |  | *Objective 20:* Deliver Harrald's Sword |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 10, 200, 250.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage FreeformRiften16 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest FreeformRiften16`.

# Skyrim:Bristleback Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Bristleback Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Bristleback+Cave)) | | |
