Bristleback Cave

**Bristleback Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") in the northwest of Solstheim island containing [bristlebacks](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback "Skyrim:Bristleback") and [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"). It contains only one zone, *[Bristleback Cave](#Bristleback_Cave)*.

This is a long, deep, and winding cave, home to rieklings which have a tendency to hide in [riekling barrels](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Barrel "Skyrim:Riekling Barrel") and snow piles. There is a riekling village in the depths of the cave.

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

### Exterior

Bristleback Cave exterior

The entrance is guarded by a small riekling camp consisting of two riekling tents separated by a lookout platform, with several food and ingredient barrels and a campfire. There are a total of seven rieklings in and around the camp, with four of them toward the south of the camp, one hiding in a riekling barrel, one hiding behind a bush, and the final one to the north. There is also an unlocked chest flanked by the riekling barrel and a fish barrel to the north of the tents, beside a cart without wheels filled with empty wine bottles. There are numerous clams and a few [pearl oysters](/wiki/Skyrim:Pearl_Oyster "Skyrim:Pearl Oyster") along the shore near the camp, while the cave entrance is to the northeast of the tents.

### Bristleback Cave

Intruding reavers

The cave system has a large number of [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Cup "Skyrim:Cup"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), [jugs](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug"), and other crockery, as well as huge amounts of clutter throughout. The entrance leads directly into an icy tunnel, with two dead [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") in the middle of the tunnel ahead by a T-junction, where one tunnel continues to the north, and a second tunnel branches to the west. To the right is a riekling barrel that will burst open to reveal a riekling as you approach, scattering a few items in the area. Behind the reavers on the ground is an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and nearby is an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), three [blue mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"), a [butterfly wing](/wiki/Skyrim:Butterfly_Wing "Skyrim:Butterfly Wing"), an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), and a [chitin plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Chitin_Plate "Skyrim:Chitin Plate").

The tunnel to the west rises to a cart in the middle of the tunnel, with a rock surrounded by fencing and a mounted goat's head lying against the rock. The tunnel turns to the south and continues to rise. At the top, it opens into a rounded rock chamber, with a pile of [firewood](/wiki/Skyrim:Firewood "Skyrim:Firewood") and two loose firewood pieces to the left. To the right are a couple ledges holding nothing of interest. High up the wall opposite is a balcony that will serve as a shortcut exit from the end of the cave system.

Riekling camp

The tunnel descending to the north has a riekling wandering around on the left; once it is attacked, it will alert a second riekling. On the left in a small spur off the main tunnel is a small encampment, with a patch of planking on the ground. A riekling will burst from a snow bank ahead along the main tunnel as you near the planking. There is a riekling barrel in front of you to the right of the tent in the encampment which will burst open as you approach, spreading items all over this area, and making it impossible to specify exactly where items started or where they will be found. In this area is a barrel on its side with a cooking stand to the right holding a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"), and a mead barrel farther to the right. Behind these items is a large rock, on top of which is a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") in a kettle. There is an ice pillar in the middle of the camp. In the northwest corner is a tent with a campfire in front of it. To the right of the tent is an open chest with a potion of minor healing inside. There are various crates and a barrel in the camp, with the following items found in and around them: three bottles of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma"), three pieces of chitin plate, a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots"), a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), four [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), and three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic").

Farther along the main tunnel where the riekling burst from the snow, by rocks jutting from the ice, are two further barrels with a goat horn on a stand lighting the area. Leaning against the stand is an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"). Beside this is an open box containing a piece of [burnt spriggan wood](/wiki/Skyrim:Burnt_Spriggan_Wood "Skyrim:Burnt Spriggan Wood"). The tunnel continues, then narrows ahead and descends to the north. At the bottom, you can see several rieklings running around, and various items strewn everywhere.

At the bottom of the ramp, you are faced with a camp of rieklings; eight will attack as soon as you are spotted or initiate the fight. At the mouth of the narrow part of the tunnel, two [boar tusks](/wiki/Skyrim:Boar_Tusk "Skyrim:Boar Tusk") are on the ground. In front of you is an overturned cart, with a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat") on top and three [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") underneath. Moving forward, on your right is an empty tent, with two unusable barrels to the right and an empty open box on a rock behind the barrels. The path then bears to the northwest around an ice pillar and a large rock in the middle of the tunnel. To the left is another empty tent. On top of the large rock are two sacks, a practice dummy on its side, and an empty [common soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Common_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Common Soul Gem") on top among clutter that has been arranged into some kind of idol or sculpture. To the west of the large rock is another short spur with a campfire surrounded by more barrels, a crate with a chitin plate on top, and an open chest containing three bowls, with a boar tusk on the ground to the left of the chest, and a riekling hut in the back with fencing on either side.

Another camp

The tunnel turns to the east, with another spur to the north with two tents, one on the immediate left, and one at the back of the spur. There are four goblets on the ground at this junction. Inside the tent on the left is a bucket containing a piece of [orichalcum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Orichalcum_Ore "Skyrim:Orichalcum Ore") and a leather strip. To the right is more fencing, with a bowl upside down on one of the spears. There is a campfire in front of the second tent, and on the left is an unlocked chest with a barrel behind. There is a leg of goat by the fire. To the right of the tent is an ingredient barrel, with a leveled [potion of lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Potion of Lockpicking") and an [elixir of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Strength "Skyrim:Elixir of Strength") on top. On the ground is a bowl containing a piece of [boar meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boar_Meat "Skyrim:Boar Meat"), with a sheaf of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat"), a boar tusk, a chitin plate, and a random defender potion next to it. To the right of the ingredient barrel is an open chest holding a roll of carpet and two bowls, one of which contains another random defender potion. To the right of the chest is an open box containing a goblet, a [potion of lasting potency](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Lasting_Potency "Skyrim:Potion of Lasting Potency"), a random potion, and an [elixir of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Health "Skyrim:Elixir of Health").

Defenders

Just past the junction to the east is a bowl on the ground. You can see large rocks and several ice pillars on either side ahead, a tent followed by fencing on the left, and another tent in the distance in front. There are a couple rieklings running around, and sniping one of them will cause five more to attack you; however, you have time to take them all out with a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") or ranged magic from just past the junction due to the distance they have to run to reach you. As you move forward, a riekling will burst from a barrel to the left of the first tent on the left, scattering two bowls, a piece of boar meat, and three boar tusks around the area.

You will pass an unusable barrel and a crate on the right. At the next pillar, the tunnel opens into a large open space, with more large rocks and tents in view separated by ice pillars and formations. Continuing ahead to the tent seen from the previous junction, you pass two unusable barrels and a crate in a gap between two bits of fencing on your left, with a set of [large antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Large_Antlers "Skyrim:Large Antlers") in front of them. There is an open box containing a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") by the next bit of fencing on the left. Along the left wall beyond the box is a tent set back slightly so it couldn't be seen from the other end of the path, containing a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and an unlocked strongbox on a block of wood. In front of the tent is a bucket containing two pieces of [clam meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Clam_Meat "Skyrim:Clam Meat") and a [small pearl](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Pearl "Skyrim:Small Pearl"). There is a campfire between this tent and the other tent. To the right of the first tent are three unusable barrels and a crate, with a large piece of [charcoal](/wiki/Skyrim:Charcoal "Skyrim:Charcoal"), a [knife](/wiki/Skyrim:Knife_(weapon) "Skyrim:Knife (weapon)"), and a [fork](/wiki/Skyrim:Fork_(weapon) "Skyrim:Fork (weapon)") on top of one of the barrels. To the right is an open box containing an [elixir of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Elixir of Regeneration"), a random [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") potion, and an [elixir of lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Elixir_of_Lockpicking "Skyrim:Elixir of Lockpicking"). To the right of the box is an open chest, a food barrel, and a master-locked chest. This is followed by fencing along the side of the tent seen from the other end of the tunnel, which contains a [deer pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer_Pelt "Skyrim:Deer Pelt").

Wagon wheel camp

The next area is to the southwest. As you approach, there are two barrels on your left by a large rock, one of which will burst open to reveal a riekling. The barrels are somewhat hidden among vegetation. Around the next ice formation and rock to the right is a [riekling hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Hut "Skyrim:Riekling Hut") next to a crate and two open boxes. In the first open box is a random [paralysis poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Paralysis_Poison "Skyrim:Paralysis Poison"), a [Skirmisher's elixir](/wiki/Skyrim:Skirmisher%27s_Elixir "Skyrim:Skirmisher's Elixir"), and a [draught of illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Illusion "Skyrim:Draught of Illusion"). In the second box are three random [poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"). A [horker tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Tusk "Skyrim:Horker Tusk") is on top of the crate. In front of the hut is a campfire. Farther around to the right past more fencing is another tent containing an open box with a [rock warbler egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Rock_Warbler_Egg "Skyrim:Rock Warbler Egg") inside. In front of this tent are two [ash yams](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam"). There is a large rock in the middle of this area, with a large caravan wagon wheel on top along with a goblet and a mounted horker head. Following the ice pillar and rocks on your left to the east is a stretch of fencing with a barrel behind, past which is a tunnel heading down to the east. Opposite on the other side of the tunnel is more fencing, with two more barrels behind. To the right of this fencing is an open chest, in front of which is a chitin plate. To the right of the chest is another empty tent, with fencing to the right.

Surprise attack

Following the narrow tunnel to the east, as the tunnel widens, two rieklings simultaneously burst from snow banks on either side. On the left is a large rock with a sack, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), and a wooden bowl containing a [green apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on top. As the tunnel turns to the north, on your right is a large rock, a crate, and an unusable barrel, and an ingredient barrel, all lit by a goat horn on a stand. In front of the crate and barrels on the ground is a horker tusk and a potion of resist element. You can see several rieklings running around in front of you as you turn the corner to the north, with an ice pillar ahead on the left. You can also see two tents ahead. Sniping one of the rieklings will cause two or three more to attack. As you move forward, you will pass some fencing on your right. At the end of the fencing is a tunnel branching off to the east that quickly turns and descends to the south. There is a riekling patrolling up and down this tunnel, who might attack with the others if it is near the top of the tunnel when you attack the first. Opposite the tunnel entrance to the west is a riekling hut, with a riekling barrel that will burst open to reveal a riekling to the right of the hut next to a tent. Four barrels are to the left of the hut, and in the middle is a crate with a sample of [hawk feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hawk_Feathers "Skyrim:Hawk Feathers") and an open box on top. The open box contains a drum and a flute. There is a rock and fencing to the right of the hut, and a lit goat horn on a stand to the right of this. Two barrels near the now destroyed riekling barrel are to the right of the horn, one of which has a [horse hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Hide "Skyrim:Horse Hide") on top. Farther to the right between two empty tents is an open chest full of [empty wine bottles](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"). A crate and a large rock are to the right of the second tent, and fencing begins after this along the wall to the tunnel to the east.

At the top of the eastern tunnel is another lit goat horn on a stand, surrounded by an unusable barrel, a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"), a chitin plate, and a set of [small antlers](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Antlers "Skyrim:Small Antlers"), all on the ground. At the bottom of the tunnel are three more rieklings running around another small campsite. On your left is a tent, with fencing on either side, and a pile of four [riekling spears](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Spear "Skyrim:Riekling Spear") in front. Around to the right of an ice formation and a rock is an open chest containing two random [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") potions, a random poison, and a bottle of [Honningbrew mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Honningbrew_Mead "Skyrim:Honningbrew Mead"). To the right of the chest are two badly stacked crates and three barrels, with an expert-locked [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") on top of one of the barrels. To the right of the strongbox is an open box containing a copy of *[Ahzidal's Descent](/wiki/Skyrim:Ahzidal%27s_Descent "Skyrim:Ahzidal's Descent")* in front of another open chest. To the right again are two more barrels.

Hidden treasure

Passing a small rock and more fencing to the right, you come to a riekling hut, with an open chest containing three goblets and more empty wine bottles to the left of the hut. In front of the hut is a flat rock formation, with a neat stack of three baskets hiding an unlocked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox") underneath. Beside the strongbox on the flat rock is a bucket containing a gourd, a basket holding two [eidar cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wheel"), a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), two chitin plates, two pieces of firewood, and a cabbage. Next to the flat rock is a campfire, with two fillets of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat") warming beside it. To the right of the hut is a crate and some fencing. At the end of the fencing is another tent containing two crates. Farther along to the right, the tunnel descends again to the west.

At the bottom of the tunnel is a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter"), a bowl, a goblet, a jug, and a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick"). As you approach these items, a riekling will burst from the snow in front of you. Just after the riekling, there is a second candlestick on the ground, and the tunnel narrows and turns sharply to the north. A riekling then bursts from a barrel in front of you, next to which is a crate with a random [health](/wiki/Skyrim:Health "Skyrim:Health") potion on top. The tunnel immediately turns again to the east, back to the north, and then to the west again. Where the tunnel turns to the west, there is an open box containing only empty wine bottles.

The tunnel descends again to the west, with three loose riekling spears and a piece of [iron ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore "Skyrim:Iron Ore") next to a small rock on the right. There is a brightly lit area ahead on the right, and you may see a riekling running from the right away up the tunnel to the west. Just before the brightly lit area is a metal bowl on your left containing a bottle of wine. The tunnel then bears to the west and rises quite steeply. At the corner, on the left is a crate holding a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)"), a bulb of garlic, and a blue mountain flower, with a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") and two sheaves of [wheat](/wiki/Skyrim:Wheat "Skyrim:Wheat") on the ground nearby. On the right to the north is a tent with a campfire inside which is creating the light. In front of the tent are four [soul gem fragments](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gem_Fragment "Skyrim:Soul Gem Fragment"), a bottle of [skooma](/wiki/Skyrim:Skooma "Skyrim:Skooma") (see bugs), and a chitin plate. To the left of the tent is a barrel and a crate. On the barrel are three more bottles of skooma. To the right of the tent is an unusable barrel and an open chest containing four empty wine bottles and seven more soul gem fragments.

At the top of the tunnel to the west is a large rock on your left with an animal skull and a chitin plate on top. In front of you is a hut with a riekling standing to the right; as you advance, two more rieklings will burst from the snow in front of you, and a third will emerge behind you. There are two huts here: one on your right, and the other in front. There is a pile of three loose spears in front of the huts. To the right of the right-hand hut is an unusable barrel, while to the left is a large stack of crates with an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") on top. More crates are to the right of the other hut, and a deer pelt is on the ground in front of it. The tunnel now turns to the south.

Main camp, part I

The tunnel turns to the east by a large rock, with an oar on top and a deer pelt beside it. Ahead is the start of a large chamber, with some fencing at the edge of a ledge. When you reach the fencing, you will be on the ledge overlooking a camp, with the path following the walls of the chamber down to the left. To the south in the distance is a bridge over a chasm, with several rieklings running around, while behind the bridge is a lookout platform, with several fences and tents beyond. Sniping the first riekling will cause four more to search for and attack you, including a mounted riekling. As you turn north to descend from the ledge, just after a gap in the fence to the right is a basket containing a set of small antlers, an open chest on its side containing a [chicken's egg](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg") and some clutter, and a deer pelt on the ground. The path follows the cavern wall around and descends to the east.

At the bottom is a pile of crates and an open chest with two bottles of skooma, three candlesticks, three boar tusks, a random potion of stamina, and a drum in and around them. To the right is a fence beside another two tents, with two pieces of firewood behind the fence, and a stack of crates and a campfire in front. In the first tent are two candlesticks. Between the tents is a pile of firewood, and in the second tent are only empty wine bottles. Another fence is to the right of the tents, with an open chest and a crate in front. On and near the crate are two boar tusks, a piece of boar meat, a random [potion of vigor](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigor "Skyrim:Potion of Vigor"), a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Magicka"), a candlestick, and a chitin plate.

Main Camp, part II

To the south, on the near side of the chasm are some crates stacked together, among which is an empty petty soul gem, two bottles of wine, two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"). Directly below the crates, on a small ledge along the wall of the chasm, is an unlootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") half buried in the snow with an enchanted Nordic [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger"). Between the bridge and the crates is a [pickaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Pickaxe "Skyrim:Pickaxe") on the ground.

Across the bridge is the main riekling camp, so expect a tough fight. Initiating the fight via bow or ranged magic allows you to meet the charging rieklings and [mounted rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Mounted_Riekling "Skyrim:Mounted Riekling") on the bridge, meaning they can only face you a couple at a time, allowing you to thin their numbers before they reach you and making the fight far easier to handle. You'll be faced by about nine rieklings, two of which are mounted, and most are leveled. There are also four additional bristlebacks in two open pens just over the bridge, with two to the right, and two on the left in the distance at the rear of the chamber.

After you cross the bridge, on your left is a tall lookout platform where one of the rieklings was standing, beside which is a tent containing some crockery. To the left of the bristleback pen to the west is a second tall lookout platform, and behind this platform is an icy ramp leading up to the southwest and the shortcut to the exit. There are three large ice pillars in the middle of the chamber. Behind the first pillar and to the left of the second platform is a riekling hut. On the ground to the right of the hut are two boar tusks and several empty wine bottles. Around the back of the hut are piles of barrels and crates as well as two chests. One chest is unlocked and contains loot, and the other is open and contains more empty wine bottles. Among the crates and barrels are two fillets of horker meat, two bottles of [ale](/wiki/Skyrim:Ale "Skyrim:Ale"), and a horker tusk. To the left of the hut is the second open bristleback pen, and to the left of this pen is an iron dagger on the ground. In the southeast corner of the chamber is a tunnel heading down to the east.

The chasm

Down the tunnel to the east, at the bottom the tunnel turns to the north, with a rock on your right with a horse hide on top. On your left after the turn is a riekling hut, with a pile of crates and an unlocked chest to the left of the hut. There is also a chitin plate, two goblets, and a plate on the ground. Among the crates is a bucket containing an iron helmet. Past the hut, the tunnel descends again. At the bottom is a rock with a crate beside it. The tunnel turns again to the west, and exits into the chasm spanned by the bridge above in the large chamber. Along the chasm is a candlestick and various pieces of crockery, and at the end is a master-locked chest.

Dead man's treasure

Returning to the main level of the chamber and climbing the ice ramp behind the lookout platform to the southwest, you will reach a ledge running to the east along the cavern wall, with a small platform built out from the side of the ledge behind the hut. Before the start of this ledge on the right is a wide tunnel heading southwest. At the start of the tunnel, on the right is a cart holding a [lute](/wiki/Skyrim:Lute "Skyrim:Lute"), a drum, and a fishing rod, while on the ground next to the cart is another drum, a piece of firewood, and a crate. On the other side of the tunnel is a pair of [fine boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Boots "Skyrim:Fine Boots") and a large piece of charcoal on top of a block of wood. The tunnel bears to the south and rises a long way. Where the tunnel turns to the east and continues to climb, a riekling hut is in the corner. In front of the hut, against the west wall of the tunnel is a crate holding a chitin plate, a bowl containing a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), and an open box containing a bottle of alto wine and an empty petty soul gem on a small holder. In front of the crate on the ground is a stalk of wheat. There is a pile of crates with a [cow hide](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide") on top to the left of the hut, and an unlocked boss chest in front of the crates. Farther up the tunnel to the east, a leather strip is on the ground. At the top after another long climb, the tunnel turns to the north and then to the west. In the corner to the north is a large rock, with a caravan wagon wheel on top, and two barrels and a crate beside it. At the next corner, the tunnel turns to the north again, with a rock in the corner with an oar on top, and a deer pelt on the ground beside a crate. At the end of this tunnel, you reach a balcony overlooking the rounded rock chamber with a pile of firewood found very early in the cave system, providing a quick shortcut to the exit.

## Notes

- In [Survival Mode](/wiki/Skyrim:Survival_Mode "Skyrim:Survival Mode"), this dungeon will not warm you up, unlike most interior locations.

## Bugs

- You may not be able to interact with some of the skooma bottles.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 2.0.2, fixes this bug.

Britte

*"Look at you! You're as filthy as a pig in a pen!"*

**Britte** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [child](/wiki/Skyrim:Child "Skyrim:Child") living in [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") with her father [Lemkil](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil "Skyrim:Lemkil") and her twin sister [Sissel](/wiki/Skyrim:Sissel "Skyrim:Sissel"). The family is rather dysfunctional, and a frustrated Lemkil makes no attempt to hide his disdain for his children, claiming that they are useless farmers, as well as blaming them for his late wife's untimely death during labor. Britte, in turn, takes out her hatred on the meek and unfortunate Sissel.

Britte wakes up every morning at 6am and leaves the house. She then proceeds to spend twelve solid hours chasing and harassing Sissel, until 6pm, when she returns home and stays there for the rest of the evening, going to sleep at 12am before beginning her routine again the next day.

She wears a set of [child's clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Child%27s_Clothes "Skyrim:Child's Clothes") with [shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000e80a8 "Skyrim:Clothing"). She carries the [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Lemkil%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Lemkil's House Key") and a selection of [food and toys](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Child "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Hide and Seek](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_and_Seek_(game) "Skyrim:Hide and Seek (game)")**: Play a round of Hide and Seek with some [children](/wiki/Skyrim:Children "Skyrim:Children") in town. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Tag, you're it!](/wiki/Skyrim:Tag,_you%27re_it! "Skyrim:Tag, you're it!")**: Play a round of Tag with the children of a city. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

When first greeted by her, it becomes clear she very much dislikes her twin sister:

:   *"If you beat up my sister Sissel, I won't tell."*
:   *"Sissel thinks she's so special. No way she's more special than me."*
:   *"I'm the older sister, by nearly five minutes. Sissel's barely worthy to walk in my shadow."*

## Conversations

She can be rather cruel, and can be observed taunting her sister;

:   **Britte**: *"You're going to get it, Sissel!"*
:   **Sissel**: *"Why? What did I do?"*
:   **Britte**: *"I told you to weed the garden by sunset, and you didn't do it. Now you're in big trouble!"*
:   **Sissel**: *"Papa told you to do that, not me! Now leave me alone!"*

:   **Britte**: *"Look at you! You're as filthy as a pig in a pen!"*
:   **Sissel**: *"I am not! You're lying!"*
:   **Britte**: *"You smell like a pig's pen, too. What a stink! Have you been rolling in the dirt all day?"*
:   **Sissel**: *"You're a liar! I won't listen to you. Leave me alone!"*

## Bugs

- Britte doesn't own the bed assigned to her so she just sandboxes near it all night. **?**

# Skyrim:Brittleshin Pass

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Brittleshin Pass ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brittleshin+Pass)) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Brittleshin_Pass "Lore:Brittleshin Pass")) | | |

Brittleshin Pass

**Brittleshin Pass** is a small [passage](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") through the mountains between [Whiterun Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Hold "Skyrim:Whiterun Hold") and [Falkreath Hold](/wiki/Skyrim:Falkreath_Hold "Skyrim:Falkreath Hold") containing a [necromancer](/wiki/Skyrim:Necromancer "Skyrim:Necromancer") and [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton"). It contains only one zone, *[Brittleshin Pass](#Brittleshin_Pass)*.

Although the interior of the ruin is named "Brittleshin Pass", the map markers for the two entrances are named "North Brittleshin Pass" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=North+Brittleshin+Pass&zoom=14&legacy=true) and "South Brittleshin Pass" [(map)](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=South+Brittleshin+Pass&zoom=14&legacy=true), counting as two separate locations for the "Locations Discovered" statistic. The northern entrance is southwest of [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun"), and the southern entrance is west of [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood").

## Related Quests

- **[The Staff of Hasedoki](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Hasedoki "Skyrim:The Staff of Hasedoki")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Hasedoki "Skyrim:Staff of Hasedoki"): Locate a legendary staff that's been smuggled into Skyrim.

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Arniel's Endeavor (part 2)](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret.
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave.
- **[Onmund's Request](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund%27s_Request "Skyrim:Onmund's Request")**: Help [Onmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Onmund "Skyrim:Onmund") negotiate the return of a family amulet from [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir").

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior: North Brittleshin Pass

North Brittleshin Pass

The path to the northern entrance leads south from the road between [Whiterun](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun "Skyrim:Whiterun") and [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") east of [Bloated Man's Grotto](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloated_Man%27s_Grotto "Skyrim:Bloated Man's Grotto"). Just past a rock cairn on your right is a large fallen tree; inside the hollow trunk is an apprentice-locked [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"). Pass some mammoth bones and a pile of rocks on the right with a flag attached, a rock on the left with three [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") plants nearby, and a mammoth ribcage on the right with a [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower"). A second blue mountain flower grows on the other side of the entrance.

### Exterior: South Brittleshin Pass

South Brittleshin Pass

The path to the southern entrance leads north from a jetty on the shore of [Lake Ilinalta](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Ilinalta "Skyrim:Lake Ilinalta") east of [Ilinalta's Deep](/wiki/Skyrim:Ilinalta%27s_Deep "Skyrim:Ilinalta's Deep"). Shortly before the entrance is a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush on the right of the path. Opposite the entrance is a stack of rocks with a flag attached.

### Brittleshin Pass

Garnet eyes

From the southern entrance, you enter a narrow tunnel full of vegetation leading down to the north. The lit brazier ahead marks the transition into a ruined room with rubble on one side. A [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus is behind the fern on the right as you enter the room. Opposite is a double iron door with a [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing over it and a second growing from a ledge with a lit brazier to the left. There are sideboards on either side of the door, but the one to the left is broken.

Through the iron doors is a large room on multiple levels, you are on a ledge with two rock pillars opposite you, with a stone face carved high on the wall with [flawless garnets](/wiki/Skyrim:Flawless_Garnet "Skyrim:Flawless Garnet") for eyes that can be dislodged with a ranged shot or the Flames spell. On your right is a lit brazier and past this is the path down. Be aware there are two skeletons at the bottom. Following the path down you pass an open sarcophagus on your right and a second fly amanita on your left and another by the first pillar. There is yet another fly amanita to the right at a dead end with [iron ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") on both side walls. The path continues between the ledge you've just descended from and the pillars. Behind the second pillar are a flight of stairs up to an area with a fly amanita fungus and an apprentice-trapped chest that activates a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap. To the northwest is a tunnel exiting this room, there is a fly amanita fungus on each side of the tunnel mouth.

The tunnel heads down a flight of stairs to another lit brazier at the bottom. In this tunnel overhead, there is a very hard to reach [web sac](/wiki/Skyrim:Web_Sac "Skyrim:Web Sac"). You can hear another skeleton and the tunnel turns to the southwest and opens into another room. You can see a leveled necromancer in front of you up a flight of stairs, facing away from you. The skeleton is just out of sight to the left. Taking out the necromancer with a [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow") will draw the skeleton out into view.

At the altar

In the room, on your left is a stone table. On the table is a wooden bowl containing a [human heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart"). There is blood all over the table and floor of this room. To the right are a couple of nearly completely buried sideboards. To the south is the flight of stairs leading up to where the necromancer stood. At the top, on your left against the south wall is an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"). In front of you is an altar with a skeleton that can be looted, a random vigorous potion, a random filled [soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems"), a random enchanted [dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Dagger "Skyrim:Dagger") and copies of *[Ancestors and the Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestors_and_the_Dunmer "Skyrim:Ancestors and the Dunmer")*, *[The Book of Daedra](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Daedra "Skyrim:The Book of Daedra")*, *[The Arcturian Heresy](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Arcturian_Heresy "Skyrim:The Arcturian Heresy")* and a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Warrior's Charge](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrior%27s_Charge "Skyrim:The Warrior's Charge")*. There are lit braziers at either end of the altar. On your right against the north wall is an upright opened sarcophagus. At the bottom of the stairs to the left is a fly amanita fungus.

On your right as you enter this room are two cages, the first is adept-locked and empty, the second has two [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") on the floor and the door is open. Against the west wall is a slightly raised area with a hay pile on the left and various crates and a barrel to the right. On top of the barrel is a quiver of iron arrows, an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel"), and two [weak lingering poisons](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Lingering_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Lingering Poison"). Between these and the cages is an exit to the northwest. There is a lit brazier on your left and behind this is an unlocked boss chest (if you have been sent here to retrieve an item this is where it will be).

To the northwest is a stone bridge to a pillar with a wooden ramp spiraling down around it. At the bottom of the spiraling ramp is a botched up straight ramp to the cave floor. At the top of the straight ramp is the top of a hanging moss plant. There is another at the bottom on the other side of a lit brazier. There are two skeletons patrolling in this area and also quite a bit of vegetation and several pillars. To the northeast is a [spellcaster trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Spellcaster_Trap "Skyrim:Spellcaster Trap") that uses a filled [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") and casts [Icy Spear](/wiki/Skyrim:Icy_Spear "Skyrim:Icy Spear") even at low levels which makes it extremely dangerous to injured or weak characters. It is in a clear area with five pillars around it. There are stairs leading up to the northeast behind it. At the top of the stairs is the tunnel to the northern entrance.

## Notes

- The marker for North Brittleshin Pass can be placed on your map by overhearing a [Whiterun guard](/wiki/Skyrim:Whiterun_Guard "Skyrim:Whiterun Guard") mention it in their random dialogue. However, they claim Brittleshin Pass is "southeast of here", when it is in fact southwest of Whiterun.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, addresses this issue. An audio splice has been done to correct this error.
- Though the pass has entrances in two different holds (Whiterun and Falkreath), it is considered to be within Falkreath Hold for radiant quests.
- Two [corundum ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") are outside the south entrance: one is to the west by the lake, and the other is to the east near the mountain. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is outside the north entrance.

## Bugs

- NPCs and creatures are unable to properly navigate throughout the dungeon due to a poor navmesh.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Brittleshin Pass

Brodir Grove

**Brodir Grove** is a small circle of stones northeast of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [reavers](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

## Walkthrough

The center of the camp

Three of the reavers will confront you as you approach; the unique greatsword [Stormfang](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormfang "Skyrim:Stormfang") is in the hands of a [reaver lord](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver_Lord "Skyrim:Reaver Lord"). The grove is centered around five large standing stones, with the reaver camp within the perimeter of the stones. There are ropes strung between four of the stones, with [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") hanging from the ropes. To the right of the stone to the south is a lean-to shelter with a bedroll underneath. Two large crates and two [trama root](/wiki/Skyrim:Trama_Root "Skyrim:Trama Root") plants are behind the lean-to, and a [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plant is beside it. To the left of the lean-to are three barrels, three crates, and four sacks stacked together. Following the perimeter counterclockwise, there are more crates and barrels stacked between the first and second stones, with bone chimes between the stones, and stacks of even more barrels and crates around the second stone, with an adept-locked chest beside the stone. Continuing around, another stack of barrels and crates and more bone chimes are between the second and third stones, with two [bear traps](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") on the ground between the stack and the third stone.

The bone chimes at the grove

A post by the third stone has two [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids and two [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") hanging from it. There are two crates, two barrels, and a pile of firewood around the third stone as well, with an expert-locked [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") on one of the crates. More bone chimes hang between the third and fourth stones, and another crate and two barrels are by the fourth stone. In front of the fourth stone is an unlocked chest, and to the left of the stone is a [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") deposit. No rope or bone chimes are between the fourth and fifth stones. There are two scathecraw plants near the fifth stone, and just outside the perimeter are two more heart stone deposits. By the fifth stone is yet another crate with three sacks stacked on top, a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), and an unlocked boss chest with another bear trap in front of it. There is also no rope or bone chimes between the fifth and first stones; only a couple [ash yam](/wiki/Skyrim:Ash_Yam "Skyrim:Ash Yam") plants are found here. On the back of the fifth stone is a set of three weapon racks, one of which holds a leveled battle axe. In the center of the camp is a large split log acting as a bench, with a firepit in front with a spit and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") hanging over it.

## Notes

- The name "Brodir Grove" probably comes from the Old Norse and Icelandic word *bróðir*, meaning *brother*. The letter *ð* is often anglicized as *d*.
- Two [gold ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") and two [emerald geodes](/wiki/Skyrim:Emerald_Geode "Skyrim:Emerald Geode") can be found west of the camp.
- Brodir Grove also [appears](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Brodir_Grove "Bloodmoon:Brodir Grove") in *[Bloodmoon](/wiki/Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon "Bloodmoon:Bloodmoon")*.

## Bugs

- Since the reaver lord respawns, you can obtain Stormfang multiple times.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.5, fixes this bug.

Broken Fang Cave

**Broken Fang Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southeast of [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") containing [skeletons](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton") and [vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). It contains only one zone, *[Broken Fang Cave](#Broken_Fang_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

**[Bloodthirst](/wiki/Skyrim:Bloodthirst_(quest) "Skyrim:Bloodthirst (quest)")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnfang_%26_Duskfang "Skyrim:Dawnfang & Duskfang"): Find a cursed blood-drinking sword.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There is evidence of recent slaughter outside the cave, with bloody human and horse remains and an abandoned cart hinting at things to come. There is a sack next to the cart. [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") and [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") grow close to the entrance. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is also nearby.

### Broken Fang Cave

The cave consists of two rooms inhabited by strong vampires; approach with caution. The first room is the largest and has the first of the two vampires. There is a skeleton in each corner of the room as well. Once the skirmish is finished, locate the adept-locked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") in the southeastern corner. The rest of the room contains only empty decorated coffins, empty wine bottles, and skeletal remains. There are five additional sets of stairs, each leading up to a small landing. The stairs themselves lead to nothing in particular, with the exception of the second staircase on the west wall. This leads to the second room where you can expect a boss vampire.

The second room acts as the vampires' lair. The first item of note is an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") with a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [weak magicka poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Magicka_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Magicka Poison"), and a bottle of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom"). These can be found either on the table, or on the floor after the altercation with the vampire. Near to the alchemy lab will be a copy of the [Lockpicking](/wiki/Skyrim:Lockpicking "Skyrim:Lockpicking") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Wolf Queen, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Wolf_Queen,_v1 "Skyrim:The Wolf Queen, v1")*. Going around the periphery of the room, next is a large cage containing bloody rags, then an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanters "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanters") with an enchanted sword lying atop it. A small bookcase next to the enchanter holds a copy of the [Illusion](/wiki/Skyrim:Illusion "Skyrim:Illusion") skill book *[Mystery of Talara, Part 4](/wiki/Skyrim:Mystery_of_Talara,_Part_4 "Skyrim:Mystery of Talara, Part 4")*, a [black soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Black Soul Gem"), and two additional soul gems. Next come to a bookcase with samples of [frost salt](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts") and [vampire dust](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire_Dust "Skyrim:Vampire Dust"). On the left-hand end table, by the double bed, is a leveled potion. The boss chest is also close to the double bed. On a raised platform are two single beds with a dresser between them. On the dresser is one of two samples of [Jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"); the second can be found on the corner of the table next to the bed platform. Both of the tables in this room are set with grisly meals; the table in the center of the room serves a [human heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart"). A [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") is on the floor by this table.

## Notes

- North of Broken Fang Cave is an unmarked ruin with a [shrine of Zenithar](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Zenithar "Skyrim:Shrine of Zenithar"). It contains a copy of the [Speech](/wiki/Skyrim:Speech "Skyrim:Speech") skill book *[2920, Second Seed, v5](/wiki/Skyrim:2920,_Second_Seed,_v5 "Skyrim:2920, Second Seed, v5")* and a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"). A locked chest is on top of the ruin.
- East of the shrine of Zenithar is a [shrine of Stendarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Stendarr "Skyrim:Shrine of Stendarr"). On the base of the shrine is a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") skill book *[Twin Secrets](/wiki/Skyrim:Twin_Secrets "Skyrim:Twin Secrets")* and a strongbox.

## Maps

- 

  Broken Fang Cave

# Skyrim:Broken Helm Hollow

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

Broken Helm Hollow

**Broken Helm Hollow** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") in the southeast corner of [The Rift](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Rift "Skyrim:The Rift") containing [bandits](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit"). It contains only one zone, *[Broken Helm Hollow](#Broken_Helm_Hollow)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Arniel's Endeavor](/wiki/Skyrim:Arniel%27s_Endeavor "Skyrim:Arniel's Endeavor")**: Uncover an ancient Dwemer secret. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Flight or Fight](/wiki/Skyrim:Flight_or_Fight "Skyrim:Flight or Fight")**: Help [Grosta](/wiki/Skyrim:Grosta "Skyrim:Grosta") at [Heartwood Mill](/wiki/Skyrim:Heartwood_Mill "Skyrim:Heartwood Mill") locate her missing husband.
- **[Retrieval](/wiki/Skyrim:Retrieval "Skyrim:Retrieval")**: Journey to a random location to retrieve a fragment of [Wuuthrad](/wiki/Skyrim:Wuuthrad "Skyrim:Wuuthrad"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Striking the Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Striking_the_Heart "Skyrim:Striking the Heart")**: Assassinate a leader of the Silver Hand. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The cave entrance is on the eastern face of the small peak southeast of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften"), near the large waterfall. Two low-level bandits stand guard outside the entrance. The treasure chest for *[Treasure Map IX](/wiki/Skyrim:Treasure_Map_IX "Skyrim:Treasure Map IX")* is found partway down the waterfall, assuming you have obtained the map.

### Broken Helm Hollow

A murdered husband

Alchemical samples found throughout the cave include [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita"), [glowing mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom"), [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool"), [Namira's Rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot"), and [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") fungi (see table below). The cave contains three sleeping bandits, two in the main campsite and a chief bandit on a raised area overlooking the camp. It is possible to take all three bandits by surprise if sneak mode is employed, so take care to avoid the [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes") when entering the main chamber. Ahead you will see the two sleeping bandits and the bandit camp. It is advisable to first take out the chief bandit sleeping on the ledge overlooking the camp, as you have the opportunity for the first strike. Provided this leveled bandit has not been roused, a variety of sneak attacks, poisons, or a shout can be used to weaken him before he gets his bearings. The two bandits below will sleep through the altercation. Once the chief bandit is disposed of, the remaining two bandits can also be removed by sneak attack. An alternate strategy is to climb onto the table at the back wall of the camp and then jump up onto a large rock outcropping. This will give you an elevated position with a view of the entire chamber below and allow protected range attacks on the chief bandit.

The boss-level chest is on the raised area by the chief bandit. It is protected by a [swinging mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Swinging_Mace "Skyrim:Swinging Mace") trap with a novice-locked [tension cable](/wiki/Skyrim:Tension_Cable "Skyrim:Tension Cable") trigger on the right side of the chest. Next to the chest is an end table holding a copy of the [Two-handed](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-handed "Skyrim:Two-handed") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Battle of Sancre Tor](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_of_Sancre_Tor "Skyrim:Battle of Sancre Tor")* and a random potion. Next to the end table is a bookcase with a copy of *[Darkest Darkness](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkest_Darkness "Skyrim:Darkest Darkness")*. There is little in the way of treasure in the campsite, but it does feature a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). A pull chain can be found next to a torch sconce at the bottom of the slope leading up to the raised area. Activating the pull chain will reveal a hidden room. Inside is an end table containing a [spell tome](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes"), a poison, and a weapons rack holding a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") and a [steel sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Sword "Skyrim:Steel Sword"). However, most notably, the room also contains the body of a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_(dead) "Skyrim:Nord (dead)"). The corpse will be anonymous unless the miscellaneous quest [Flight or Fight](/wiki/Skyrim:Flight_or_Fight "Skyrim:Flight or Fight") has been initiated. Because of a [bug](/wiki/Skyrim:Flight_or_Fight#Bugs "Skyrim:Flight or Fight"), it is recommended not to activate/search the body until you start the quest by talking to [Grosta](/wiki/Skyrim:Grosta "Skyrim:Grosta"). The dead Nord turns out to be her husband, [Leifnarr](/wiki/Skyrim:Leifnarr "Skyrim:Leifnarr").

| Fungi |
| --- |
| 6 [Bleeding Crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown")  1 [Blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort")  2 [Fly Amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita")  1 [Glowing Mushroom](/wiki/Skyrim:Glowing_Mushroom "Skyrim:Glowing Mushroom")  4 [Imp Stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool")  3 [Namira's Rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot")  2 [White Cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") |

## Notes

- Three [corundum ore](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore "Skyrim:Corundum Ore") veins can be found here: one next to the stream inside the cave, one inside the secret room, and one outside at the bottom of the waterfall.
- At the base of the waterfall, near one of the corundum ore veins, is the body of a dead Khajiit with a coin purse and 4 loose gold coins next to him. Three levels higher on the waterfall cascade, there are 5 more gold coins and an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword").
- Broken Helm Hollow also [appears](/wiki/Online:Broken_Helm_Hollow "Online:Broken Helm Hollow") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").

## Bugs

- Broken Helm Hollow isn't marked as a cave, so cave-based radiant quests won't target it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- The corpse in the hidden room is revealed to be Grosta's missing husband Leifnarr during the quest Flight or Fight. Leifnarr's body is unnamed, identified only by the generic title "Nord". If you find this corpse first without talking to Grosta, the quest will activate stage 15, "Report Leifnarr's Death to his family", but no dialogue option will be added to Grosta making the quest unable to be completed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.

## Maps

- 

  Broken Helm Hollow

# Skyrim:Broken Limb Camp

## Overview

Broken Limb Camp

**Broken Limb Camp** is a [giant camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant_Camps "Skyrim:Giant Camps") north-northwest of [Darkwater Crossing](/wiki/Skyrim:Darkwater_Crossing "Skyrim:Darkwater Crossing").

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Giant "Skyrim:Bounty: Giant")**: Kill a problematic [giant](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Walkthrough

A giant at the camp

The camp is on the edge of the hot springs in [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") near the bank of the [White River](/wiki/Skyrim:White_River "Skyrim:White River"). Two [giants](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant "Skyrim:Giant") occupy the camp, which is surrounded by the typical painted stones, [bone chimes](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Chimes "Skyrim:Bone Chimes"), and bones. The central campfire has been extinguished, with a [dragon's tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue") plant growing among the burnt remnants. An unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and two [mammoth cheese bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl") are south of the campfire. More dragon's tongue, [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), [creep cluster](/wiki/Skyrim:Creep_Cluster "Skyrim:Creep Cluster") plants, and a birds' nest are in the vicinity.

Broken Oar Grotto

**Broken Oar Grotto** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") north of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") containing [Blackblood Marauders](/wiki/Skyrim:Blackblood_Marauder "Skyrim:Blackblood Marauder") and their leader [Captain Hargar](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Hargar "Skyrim:Captain Hargar"). It contains only one zone, *[Broken Oar Grotto](#Broken_Oar_Grotto)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Lights Out!](/wiki/Skyrim:Lights_Out! "Skyrim:Lights Out!")**: Help run a [cargo ship](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Icerunner "Skyrim:The Icerunner") aground.

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon")**: Find the [Moon Amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Moon_Amulet "Skyrim:Moon Amulet") for [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- **[Bounty: Bandit Boss](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Bandit_Boss "Skyrim:Bounty: Bandit Boss")**: Eliminate a bandit leader for a bounty reward.
- **[Dungeon Delving](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeon_Delving_(Caves) "Skyrim:Dungeon Delving (Caves)")**: Do a favor by retrieving an item from a cave.
- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader.
- **[Protecting the Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Protecting_the_Bloodline "Skyrim:Protecting the Bloodline")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Destroy the [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire") before it turns its allies.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

Located at the northern tip of the coastline of Solitude, the entrance to Broken Oar Grotto resembles a landslide next to a small cave entrance. A crushed longboat can be seen among the rubble, rock, and broken trees. Two rowboats are beached in front of the entrance. A small lit campfire is nearby along with two [spiky grass](/wiki/Skyrim:Spiky_Grass "Skyrim:Spiky Grass") plants and a couple barrels, one of which contains [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"). A number of small islets nearby can be explored for ore veins.

### Broken Oar Grotto

Grotto interior

Broken Oar Grotto is a huge flooded cavern where a group of raiders, the Blackblood Marauders, have built facilities for housing and launching the vessels they use to raid along the coast. The main cavern entrance for their ships has been blocked by a cave-in, preventing any large vessels from being launched in the last year, leading to most of them being sunk or repurposed. Recently, one of the crew has thought to find someone gullible enough to aid them in causing a ship to run aground and using rowboats to capture and strip it of its valuables. The other half of the longboat seen outside can be found inside, crushed under the cave-in.

Upon entering the cavern, there is a wooden platform in front of you, with a rowboat tied up to the platform and a stack of crates beside it. A flight of steps leads down into the water, which can be used to find the first of four underwater [chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") lying next to a lootable skeleton (see [notes](#Notes)). There are three [bear pelts](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt") resting on the stacked crates, and a fourth pelt and a lootable barrel and sack on the rowboat. Beyond this is a suspended wooden bridge crossing to another wooden platform with shelves of sacks, barrels, and various goods, including alchemical [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). There is also a novice-locked chest with a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") beside it on a set of boards above and to the left, which can be reached from the top of the first ramp. Against the south wall is an open crate containing many bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), with more on the shelves to the left. There is an [oil lantern](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Lanterns "Skyrim:Oil Lanterns") hanging from a beam above, and a couple ramps leading up to a higher platform to the left. Two marauders are standing at the top, talking about a chest they've found hidden on the deck of a sunken ship. At the top is an open crate containing three haunches of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison") beside more barrels, and a path leading to the northeast. The path soon splits, with one path climbing a steep natural stone bridge to the northwest, while the other path continues at the same level to the east.

Climbing the bridge brings you to a much higher platform with three fillets of [horker meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Meat "Skyrim:Horker Meat") and several pieces of cheese by the edge on a small set of shelves. The path follows the west wall and descends to an area guarded by a marauder, with a lever that operates a raised drawbridge across to the east side of the cavern. To the left of the lever is another wooden ramp that descends to another platform, with an open crate containing more bottles of wine and a second ramp descending to a platform at water level, with a rowboat on the platform containing an unlocked chest. With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found here; fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be caught here. There is also stairs that descends into the water, which can be used to find the second underwater chest.

Continuing to the east from the initial junction, there are crates on either side of the path with a couple bear pelts, an unlocked chest, a bucket of [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), and a cart containing more bear pelts and a couple cheese wheels. Just behind the cart is an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") on the south wall. Beyond the ore vein, the path follows the east wall of the cavern, passing another ladder into the water on the left, before climbing back up to meet with the eastern side of the drawbridge. At this point, there is a tunnel to the east, and a table beside the bridge with a small coin purse on top. There is also a path continuing to the northeast following the eastern wall of the cavern.

The tunnel to the east turns to the north then back to the east, before opening into a small cave with a wooden plank wall on the right shielding a raised area with a long wooden table surrounded by an [oil slick](/wiki/Skyrim:Oil_Slicks "Skyrim:Oil Slicks"), with an oil lantern above and a marauder sitting at the table. There is a second marauder sleeping on a bedroll to the east. Once these are dealt with, you are free to explore. On the table is a bowl of [tomato soup](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato_Soup "Skyrim:Tomato Soup"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), and a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), with an unlocked chest and a set of shelves to the west, against the wall. The shelves hold a random [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"), two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), two [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), a bowl of bread, and a haunch of raw venison on top. An alcove to the west beside the entrance holds a bucket in a hole in the floor, and a convenient table and lantern. There are a total of four bedrolls against the walls to the north and east, and an exit to the southeast into another small cave.

This cave holds two healing potions and a poison on a barrel against the north wall, and more crates and an unlocked chest against the south wall. A flight of wooden stairs against the southeast wall leads up to a loft, with a medium coin purse and two loose [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") coins on a crate. Under the stairs is a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein"). A tunnel to the northeast leads back to the main chamber of the grotto, where to the left, against the southwestern wall, is a pile of barrels and crates with two [goat hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Hide "Skyrim:Goat Hide") on top.

After emerging back into the main chamber, you will see to the north a partially sunken boat beneath a large wooden structure built out over the water, composed of wooden scaffolding incorporating pieces of what was once a large ship, with the cabin forming a wooden building on top. To the northwest, the path continues and forks, with the left-hand path leading up an earthen ramp to another natural stone bridge across the water, and the right-hand path continuing along the edge of the water. This right-hand path comes to a second lever-operated raised drawbridge that gives access to the lower level of the wooden structure, before continuing around to the southwest, past another iron ore vein, and back to the first drawbridge.

The ramp and stone bridge leading up to the northwest is guarded at the top by a marauder. From the top of the bridge, it is possible to see several marauders below you on the wooden structure on different levels, thus serving as an excellent location to start picking them off (possibly with the [long bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Long_Bow "Skyrim:Long Bow") and quiver of [iron arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Arrow "Skyrim:Iron Arrow") by a railing at the rear of the ledge), due to the distance they need to travel to engage you. This path continues northwest across the cavern to the west wall, before descending and following the wall around to the north end of the wooden structure. Near a rock column on the right is a [wood chopping block](/wiki/Skyrim:Wood_Chopping_Block "Skyrim:Wood Chopping Block"), with a [silver ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Silver Ore Vein") opposite this against the northeast wall, and a flight of stairs leading down to the left of the chopping block.

The path continues to the east, passing an entrance on the right into the wooden building seen from the far side, while to the northeast is a [forge](/wiki/Skyrim:Forge "Skyrim:Forge"), along with a [workbench](/wiki/Skyrim:Workbench "Skyrim:Workbench") which has a [steel greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Greatsword "Skyrim:Steel Greatsword"), a random [stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Stamina "Skyrim:Stamina") potion, and a copy of the [Smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Cherim's Heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Cherim%27s_Heart "Skyrim:Cherim's Heart")* on top. A [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone") sits against the north wall, to the left of which is a [smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") with a square wooden table beside it. On the table is an [iron sword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer"), and a pair of [iron gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Iron Gauntlets"). On the far side of the smelter is a row of three weapon racks holding an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword") and [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), with a round table holding an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") beside them and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack") to the left. To the southeast is the prow of a ship, with three more weapon racks in front holding a couple more random [bows](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"). Near these weapon racks is a leveled [potion of true shot](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_True_Shot "Skyrim:Potion of True Shot"), while on the prow are a couple archery targets with a few iron arrows lying on the deck.

View of the sunken ship

Entering the building leads into a room with an unlocked chest on top of a table in the western corner. A set of shelves behind the door against the northeast wall holds a bowl of [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"), [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a couple bottles of wine, an iron helmet, and a few common books. Beyond an internal wall is a small square wooden table with three medium coin purses, an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a random healing potion, eight gold coins, and *[Hargar's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Hargar%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Hargar's Journal")*, which describes where Captain Hargar keeps his loot hidden from these lowlifes and also provides a bit more of an explanation regarding the job planned by [Jaree-Ra](/wiki/Skyrim:Jaree-Ra "Skyrim:Jaree-Ra") and his sister [Deeja](/wiki/Skyrim:Deeja "Skyrim:Deeja"). Against the northwest wall is a long wooden table with a set of random [armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Armor "Skyrim:Armor") and two bottles of wine on top, and a weapon plaque above holding a random [two-handed weapon](/wiki/Skyrim:Two-Handed_Weapons "Skyrim:Two-Handed Weapons").

To the left of this table is the Icerunner's main chest. To the southwest is a ramp up to a small bedroom area with a single bed in the western corner, and a round wooden table beside it with a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), a bottle of wine, an easily missed [silver amethyst ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Amethyst_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Amethyst Ring"), and a common book on top. A large coin purse sitting on top of a yardarm is visible through a gap in the wall behind the bed; the purse can be knocked off with an arrow or the [Unrelenting Force](/wiki/Skyrim:Unrelenting_Force "Skyrim:Unrelenting Force") [shout](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Shouts "Skyrim:Dragon Shouts"), or reached by jumping onto the end of the yardarm from a higher rock ledge and acrobatically balancing along it while avoiding a hazardous misstep. Above the table is a shield plaque with a [banded iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Banded_Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Banded Iron Shield") and an unlootable iron sword (see [bugs](#Bugs)). By the head of the bed is a bowl of red apples, and against the southeast wall is a set of shelves holding four bottles of wine, a red apple, and seven common books, with a [mammoth tusk](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Tusk "Skyrim:Mammoth Tusk") on top. There is a ramp leading down beneath the bedroom area, past a lookout post, to another storage area among the scaffolding with an oil slick on the ground and an oil lantern above it.

There are many sacks and barrels in this area along the rear wall, with a wooden table holding a bottle of alto wine, a honey nut treat, and a cooked [horse haunch](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Haunch "Skyrim:Horse Haunch"), and a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks") on a lit brazier to the left. Farther to the left is the flight of wooden stairs seen previously beside the wood chopping block. In front of the stairs is another wooden ramp down to another part of the ship that was used to build the structure. There is an oil slick on the deck along with an oil lantern above and a long wooden table with chairs around it, with a [mammoth steak](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Steak "Skyrim:Mammoth Steak"), a bowl of [horker stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Horker_Stew "Skyrim:Horker Stew"), and several common books on top. There is a second table with a mead barrel on top, with a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") underneath. There is a rowboat below that can be reached via another ramp, with a ladder down into the water to the left. The ladder can be used to dive down and board the partially sunken boat beside the structure. On the deck of this boat is a master-locked chest that can be opened using a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Hargar%27s_Chest_Key "Skyrim:Hargar's Chest Key") in Captain Hargar's possession. There is also a large coin purse and an expert-locked chest among the pilings that are supporting the wooden structure (see notes).

## Notes

- It is advisable to complete Ahtar's quest before any other quests in Broken Oar Grotto, as killing Captain Hargar will render that quest inaccessible, thus making it difficult to ever use Ahtar as a follower.
- There are four underwater chests hidden inside:
  1. Immediately after entering the grotto, head left down the stairs leading into the water. The first chest will be on your right next to a rock and a skeleton.
  2. Continue along the wooden scaffolding, take the stone arched path up to the ceiling of the cavern, then continue down past the first wooden drawbridge to a dock with a boat pulled up onto it. Take the ladder at the end of the dock down into the water, and the second chest will be directly in front of you a short distance away, next to a large rock and a skeleton.
  3. The third, master-locked chest is on the deck of a partially sunken boat, next to the captain's quarters, as noted in *Hargar's Journal*.
  4. The fourth is an expert-locked chest on an underwater platform among the pilings that support the captain's quarters. From the bottom platform of the structure containing the captain's quarters, there are two ladders into the water. Walk off the southeast one toward the partially sunken boat. Turn left, and go between the scaffolding and the partially sunken boat. Swim to the bottom, and look left for the only space between pilings that isn't blocked by cross-bracing, then swim northwest until you're blocked by more cross-bracing. Turn right, and you'll see the chest on a platform above you next to a large coin purse.
- Two [gold ore veins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Gold Ore Vein") are due west of the grotto on a large islet with a flag, with one at the east base of the rock ledge that forms the peak of the islet and the other at the base of the ledge on the west.
- [DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") If the quest [Protecting the Bloodline](/wiki/Skyrim:Protecting_the_Bloodline "Skyrim:Protecting the Bloodline") sends you to Broken Oar Grotto, the Vampire will be found inside fighting with the Blackblood Marauders due to their factions not having any kind of positive modifiers towards the other.

## Bugs

- If the quest [Amulet of the Moon](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_the_Moon "Skyrim:Amulet of the Moon") directs you here, check to see whether you have already visited this location. This location does not respawn, so if you have been here before, the Moon Amulet cannot spawn here and you cannot complete the quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.1.0, fixes this bug.
  - You will need to reload a previous save to get a different location from [Kharjo](/wiki/Skyrim:Kharjo "Skyrim:Kharjo").
- When in the water, you may randomly fall to the bottom as if there is no water and may or may not be allowed a breath. Swimming will continue to work normally afterward.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.7, fixes this bug.
- The control quest here may become stuck due to an engine issue with scenes that have AI packages covering their final phases.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.4, fixes this bug.
- You may not be able to interact with the iron sword on the wall plate above the captain's bed.
- The searchable barrel outside the dungeon respawns despite it being classed as a "no-reset zone". **?**
