Broken Tower Redoubt

**Broken Tower Redoubt** is a medium-sized [fort](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Forts "Skyrim:Military Forts") east of [Karthwasten](/wiki/Skyrim:Karthwasten "Skyrim:Karthwasten") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). It contains two zones, both named *Broken Tower Redoubt*: the [ground level](#Broken_Tower_Redoubt:_Ground_Level) and the [upper tower](#Broken_Tower_Redoubt:_Upper_Tower).

It is a dangerous place, making travel between Karthwasten and [Rorikstead](/wiki/Skyrim:Rorikstead "Skyrim:Rorikstead") hazardous. The guards of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") will warn you of the danger, stating, *"Beware the region northeast, across the river. Forsworn have taken refuge in Broken Tower Redoubt and Red Eagle Redoubt."*

## Related Quests

- **[The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella")**: Find a new [Sybil](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") for the [Temple of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Temple of Dibella").

#### Radiant Quests

- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward.
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest.
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah").
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader.
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store.

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior: Ground Level

The fort lies along the road between Karthwasten and Rorikstead. One [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") patrols the road, and another two Forsworn on the middle level exterior will attack with bows. If they lose sight of you, they will descend through the ground floor and try to find you. A [blue mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower") grows by the door, and two [purple mountain flowers](/wiki/Skyrim:Purple_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Purple Mountain Flower") grow near the western end of the fort. Just past the western edge of the fort, two blue mountain flowers, a purple mountain flower, and two [juniper](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries") trees grow by a dirt path leading to [Liar's Retreat](/wiki/Skyrim:Liar%27s_Retreat "Skyrim:Liar's Retreat").

### Broken Tower Redoubt: Ground Level

The main room of the fort

The ground floor door opens to a short twisting tunnel. After two turns it opens to a large room, with two Forsworn, one on the lower level and one on the higher level. There is a table to the left with two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), and straight ahead is a small room with a random [potion of magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") on a barrel and fifteen bottles of Nord mead on a set of shelves. Opposite the first table is another with a lute on it. To the right of that table, in the darkness, is an adept-locked door leading to a storage room with thirteen bottles of Nord mead and a random [potion of stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") on some shelves, another two bottles of Nord mead on a barrel, and a chest. Above the chest are seven hanging [rabbits](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"), with another two pheasants on the floor behind the chest.

From the main part of the room there are two sets of stairs. The one to the north has collapsed, but the one to the south is still intact. At the far end of the left-hand side on some fallen masonry are two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), and hiding between two barrels is a [Dibella statue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dibella_Statue "Skyrim:Dibella Statue"), while to the right-hand side is a door leading deeper into the fort. In the next corridor, there is a [spiked wall](/wiki/Skyrim:Spike_Wall "Skyrim:Spike Wall") trap with two [pressure plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Pressure_Plate "Skyrim:Pressure Plate"), one on either side of the trap. The first is hidden in some hay by two barrels on the approach and has a table next to it holding a bottle of Alto wine, a wooden plate with a salmon steak and raw salmon meat on it, and a large [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"). The second is beside another two barrels around the corner, just before the end of the spiked wall located to the right.

After this is a corridor running in a semi-circle around a circular room. There is a Forsworn patrolling the corridor, which has two doors; one to the north that leads outside to the exterior middle level, and one to the east leading back to the main room. There are two single beds and four bedrolls, all unowned, in the circular room. On the shelves to the left from the first entry are a copy of the [Block](/wiki/Skyrim:Block "Skyrim:Block") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Mirror](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Mirror "Skyrim:The Mirror")*, a [frenzy poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Frenzy_Poison "Skyrim:Frenzy Poison"), a [satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Satchel "Skyrim:Satchel"), an open [strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:Strongbox "Skyrim:Strongbox"), and bottles of alto wine and wine. On the cupboard shelf after that are a [solution of enhanced stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Enhanced_Stamina "Skyrim:Solution of Enhanced Stamina") (worth over 1,000 gold), several bottles of alto wine and wine, and a bowl on top. By the end of the bed beside the cupboard is a crate with three loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"), a large coin purse, a [silver ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring"), and sometimes a random potion on top, and by the other bed are a novice-locked chest and a table with a mead barrel and a bowl containing bread. There are also a wardrobe and a second table in the room.

The corridor to the east leads back to main room, above the collapsed staircase. There is a table with a random [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and a bottle of alto wine. The corridor leads to the base of the east tower, passing another exit to the middle exterior level on the left which has a barrel with a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile") on top next to it. By the base of the stairs are a table with a salt pile and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") on top, as well as some shelves with three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), three loose septims, other food, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"), and another drum. Halfway up the stairs is a [tripwire](/wiki/Skyrim:Tripwire "Skyrim:Tripwire") that activates some [falling boulders](/wiki/Skyrim:Falling_Boulders "Skyrim:Falling Boulders"). A Forsworn patrols this part of the stairs, and can be killed by triggering the tripwire at the appropriate point. This may alert two other Forsworn in the area at the top of the stairs.

At the top of stairs is a room where another Forsworn waits. There are two unowned single beds in the room, and a table with a random potion, a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), a haunch of [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), a bowl of [tomato soup](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato_Soup "Skyrim:Tomato Soup"), and a [honey nut treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat"). There are another bowl of tomato soup and a fillet of salmon meat on some cupboard shelves, a set of shelves holding two flutes and drums, and an unlocked chest by one of the beds. There are more stairs on the other side of the room, with a pickaxe on the ground by their base, leading up to a third exit, past a final Forsworn.

The camp on the middle level

### Exterior: Middle Level

The middle level of the exterior is guarded by two Forsworn, one to the east and one to the west. On the eastern side are an empty table and a simple tent with a bedroll. On the western side is a small camp, with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot"), a [grindstone](/wiki/Skyrim:Grindstone "Skyrim:Grindstone"), two hay piles, and a table with three [iron swords](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Sword "Skyrim:Iron Sword"), an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), and a random [war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:War_Axe "Skyrim:War Axe") on top and a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") underneath. There are two entrances to the interior from this level, one at each end.

### Exterior: Top Level

The top level exterior is the only way to get to the top of the western tower. It is guarded by a single leveled Forsworn, and there are two tables: one with a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow") and [forsworn arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Arrow "Skyrim:Forsworn Arrow") (which may have fallen through the table and be underneath), and the other with a random leveled potion.

### Broken Tower Redoubt: Upper Tower

The Briarheart and the statue covered in blood in the sacrificial chamber

The top level of the tower contains a statue and shrine to [Dibella](/wiki/Lore:Dibella "Lore:Dibella"), guarded by a [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart"); there is also a [lightning rune](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Rune "Skyrim:Lightning Rune") in the middle of the room. The top level is split into the main chamber and a side bedroom. There is an expert-locked cell off the main room that is empty (unless you are here to rescue someone for a quest, in which case they will occupy this cell); the Briarheart carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Broken_Tower_Prison_Key "Skyrim:Broken Tower Prison Key") that unlocks the cell.

There is a table to the left of the entrance that holds a decapitated skeever, a copy of the [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Liminal Bridges](/wiki/Skyrim:Liminal_Bridges "Skyrim:Liminal Bridges")*, a random healing potion, two pieces of [canis root](/wiki/Skyrim:Canis_Root "Skyrim:Canis Root"), and a copy of *[Ancestors and the Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancestors_and_the_Dunmer "Skyrim:Ancestors and the Dunmer")*. There are two random frost weakness poisons, a bottle of wine, and two bottles of alto wine on the shelves beside that. On the floor there are seven sprigs of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberry "Skyrim:Snowberry") and a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes") leading to the statue and [shrine of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:Shrine_of_Dibella "Skyrim:Shrine of Dibella"). Beside the entrance to the bedroom is another set of shelves containing three flutes and two drums, with a lute next to it.

The bedroom to the north has an unowned double bed, an unlocked chest, a table, a cupboard, and an end table with some cheese on top. On the table are a bowl of [beef stew](/wiki/Skyrim:Beef_Stew "Skyrim:Beef Stew"), a [silver emerald necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Emerald_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Emerald Necklace"), two bottles of alto wine, a copy of *[The Firmament](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Firmament "Skyrim:The Firmament")*, a bowl of [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), a plate holding a [grilled chicken breast](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Chicken_Breast "Skyrim:Grilled Chicken Breast"), and a [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull"). On the cupboard shelves are a random magicka potion, two [leather strips](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"), a canis root, a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll"), and some [horse meat](/wiki/Skyrim:Horse_Meat "Skyrim:Horse Meat").

## Notes

- It is possible to gain access to the highest level of Broken Tower Redoubt without going through all the levels by climbing down the mountain behind the fort.
- If you have started both [The Heart of Dibella](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Heart_of_Dibella "Skyrim:The Heart of Dibella") and [The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors"), and the [Radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant") system has chosen Broken Tower Redoubt as the location for [Logrolf the Willful](/wiki/Skyrim:Logrolf_the_Willful "Skyrim:Logrolf the Willful"), both he and [Fjotra](/wiki/Skyrim:Fjotra "Skyrim:Fjotra") will occupy the same cell in the tower.
- Despite being occupied by Forsworn, there is a large amount of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") to be found in the lower interior, 34 in total.
- There are a couple ore veins nearby: an [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") on the road to the east, and a [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") to the northeast with a skeleton and pickaxe. There is another corundum vein outside Liar's Retreat to the northwest.
- Aside from the Briarheart, all Forsworn enemies encountered here are female.

## Maps

- 

  Ground Level
- 

  Upper Tower

# Skyrim:Broken Tusk Mine

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Mine.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Mine.png) | Mine: Broken Tusk Mine ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Broken+Tusk+Mine)) | | |

| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 6 |
| Occupants | |

| Location | |
| North of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") Southeast of [Bristleback Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Bristleback_Cave "Skyrim:Bristleback Cave") | |

| # of [Heart Stone Deposits](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") | 2 |

Broken Tusk Mine

**Broken Tusk Mine** is a small [heart stone](/wiki/Skyrim:Heart_Stone "Skyrim:Heart Stone") [mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Mines "Skyrim:Mines") north of [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") containing [rieklings](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling "Skyrim:Riekling"). It contains only one zone, *[Broken Tusk Mine](#Broken_Tusk_Mine)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

### Exterior

The mine can be reached from the north or by descending the mountain from the [Stalhrim Source](/wiki/Skyrim:Stalhrim_Source "Skyrim:Stalhrim Source") to the east. Above the mine entrance is a multi-tiered riekling camp built upon the mountain. The camp features a pair of bridges, the second of which spans the gap leading to the mine entrance. At the far end of the bridges is a tent, with a [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") sack inside and two food sacks outside. The path continues northeast to the uppermost level, where a second tent contains an unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") and another unlocked chest is under a lookout platform to the right. Also under the platform is an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") on top of a crate. Four rieklings, including a mounted riekling charger, guard the camp and mine entrance.

### Broken Tusk Mine

Mine interior

The entrance descends to a wooden platform with a ramp leading down to the cavern floor. The interior of the mine consists of a single large cavern with several riekling tents. The right section of the platform appears newer than the rest, and seems to have been built by the rieklings. Just below this section of the platform, you will find some collapsed and broken timbers, with a lootable skeleton lying on top. There is a riekling on the platform to the left of the ramp, in front of an empty tent. Another riekling is by a campfire next to the south wall, and the third riekling is next to a [riekling hut](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Hut "Skyrim:Riekling Hut") to the west.

Under the wooden platform, to the right as you descend the ramps, is a crate with two [gold ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ingot "Skyrim:Gold Ingot"), two small [coin purses](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), two [gold necklaces](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Necklace "Skyrim:Gold Necklace"), two [silver necklaces](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Necklace "Skyrim:Silver Necklace"), a [gold ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold_Ring "Skyrim:Gold Ring"), two [silver rings](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Ring"), a [silver garnet ring](/wiki/Skyrim:Silver_Garnet_Ring "Skyrim:Silver Garnet Ring"), two [garnets](/wiki/Skyrim:Garnet "Skyrim:Garnet"), and six loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") all on top, and two more gold ingots on the ground in front of it. To the north is a heart stone deposit, with an unlocked wooden chest to the left flanked by two barrels containing [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients"). Farther to the left is a pen containing a second heart stone deposit and a campfire. To the west is the riekling hut, with a [riekling barrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Riekling_Barrel "Skyrim:Riekling Barrel") to the left that will burst open to reveal another riekling. Behind the barrel is another unlocked chest, with a short tunnel to the left heading southwest containing a dead [reaver](/wiki/Skyrim:Reaver "Skyrim:Reaver") and a lootable [skeleton](/wiki/Skyrim:Skeleton "Skyrim:Skeleton").

## Notes

- To the left of the empty tent on the platform inside the mine is a patch on the wall that looks like a depleted [ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Ores_and_Ingots "Skyrim:Ores and Ingots").

# Skyrim:Bromjunaar Sanctuary

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Nordic Ruin: Bromjunaar Sanctuary | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Important Treasure | |
| [Konahrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Konahrik "Skyrim:Konahrik") [Wooden Mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Wooden_Mask "Skyrim:Wooden Mask") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| LabyrinthianPriestSanctuary | |
| Region | |
| [Hjaalmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjaalmarch "Skyrim:Hjaalmarch") | |

Bromjunaar Sanctuary

**Bromjunaar Sanctuary** is a hidden location reached by equipping the [wooden mask](/wiki/Skyrim:Wooden_Mask "Skyrim:Wooden Mask") while inside a building in [Labyrinthian](/wiki/Skyrim:Labyrinthian "Skyrim:Labyrinthian").

## Walkthrough

Ruined dragon priest mask holders

All nine dragon priest masks including the final one, [Konahrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Konahrik "Skyrim:Konahrik")

While scouring Labyrinthian, you might find a skeleton, some [notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hired_Thug%27s_Missive "Skyrim:Hired Thug's Missive"), and a wooden mask in one of the snowbound buildings in the area. The notes reveal that equipping the wooden mask while inside the central room of the building will transport you back in time, before the destruction and subsequent burial of the structure.

Bromjunaar Sanctuary is an alternate version of the room with no conventional exit, representing its state in the distant past. It contains several empty [chests](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), [urns](/wiki/Skyrim:Urn "Skyrim:Urn"), and sets of shelves, as well as eight [dragon priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest "Skyrim:Dragon Priest") busts upon which all eight [dragon priest masks](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Priest_Mask "Skyrim:Dragon Priest Mask") found in the base game can be placed. The eight masks needed are: [Hevnoraak](/wiki/Skyrim:Hevnoraak_(item) "Skyrim:Hevnoraak (item)"), [Krosis](/wiki/Skyrim:Krosis_(item) "Skyrim:Krosis (item)"), [Morokei](/wiki/Skyrim:Morokei_(item) "Skyrim:Morokei (item)"), [Nahkriin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahkriin_(item) "Skyrim:Nahkriin (item)"), [Otar](/wiki/Skyrim:Otar "Skyrim:Otar"), [Rahgot](/wiki/Skyrim:Rahgot_(item) "Skyrim:Rahgot (item)"), [Vokun](/wiki/Skyrim:Vokun_(item) "Skyrim:Vokun (item)"), and [Volsung](/wiki/Skyrim:Volsung_(item) "Skyrim:Volsung (item)"). Placing all eight masks on the statues at the same time will unlock [Konahrik](/wiki/Skyrim:Konahrik "Skyrim:Konahrik"), the powerful ninth mask. The other masks can be retrieved after being placed, but any improvements made to them through [smithing](/wiki/Skyrim:Smithing "Skyrim:Smithing") will have been removed once they were placed on the busts.

To leave the sanctuary, simply unequip the wooden mask.

## Notes

- Equipping the wooden mask outside the central room of the building and then entering the room will not transport you to the sanctuary; you must equip the mask while inside the room.
- If the wooden mask is dropped while in the sanctuary, it will be restored to your inventory when you return to Labyrinthian.
- Items placed in the sanctuary don't reset, nor do most of the containers. The two urns by the static door, however, are not safe for storage.
- If any of the other masks from the base game are sold to a merchant, it will become impossible to obtain Konahrik. However, PC players can use [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") commands to obtain the mask.
- [Nahkriin](/wiki/Skyrim:Nahkriin_(item) "Skyrim:Nahkriin (item)") can only be obtained when in [Skuldafn](/wiki/Skyrim:Skuldafn_Temple "Skyrim:Skuldafn Temple") as part of the main quest. If you fail to retrieve it at that time, you will not get a second chance to obtain it. However, PC players can use console commands to acquire Nahkriin, and thus, Konahrik, while all players can use the ["dead loading" glitch](/wiki/Skyrim:Glitches#Dead_Loading "Skyrim:Glitches") to load/warp back to Skuldafn.
- [Morokei](/wiki/Skyrim:Morokei_(item) "Skyrim:Morokei (item)") can only be obtained from a sealed area of Labyrinthian. Without glitches, it is not possible to unseal the area containing Morokei without joining the College of Winterhold and completing much of its questline. Normally it is obtained during the College of Winterhold quest [The Staff of Magnus](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Staff_of_Magnus "Skyrim:The Staff of Magnus"), but it is possible to return later to Labyrinthian if the mask was left behind during the quest.
- The sanctuary was originally intended to be a player home, but due to time restraints, this was not implemented by the developers. However, at least one of the game's designers hoped modders would add this feature.[[UOL 1]](#cite_note-JoelBurgess-1)
- Bromjunaar means either "Light of the Northern Servants" or "North Kingdom" in the [dragon language](/wiki/Lore:Dragon_Language "Lore:Dragon Language").
- The books *[Holdings of Jarl Gjalund](/wiki/Skyrim:Holdings_of_Jarl_Gjalund "Skyrim:Holdings of Jarl Gjalund")* and *[A Minor Maze](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Minor_Maze "Skyrim:A Minor Maze")* refer to Bromjunaar as an important settlement in the past.

## Bugs

- It is possible to get a horse into the room from which the sanctuary can be accessed, but equipping the wooden mask while on horseback causes the game to crash.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Bronze Water Cave

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Bronze Water Cave ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bronze+Water+Cave)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Clearable](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons#Clearing "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Dungeon](/wiki/Skyrim:Dungeons "Skyrim:Dungeons") | Yes |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days or 30 days |
| [Level](/wiki/Skyrim:Encounter_Zone_Level "Skyrim:Encounter Zone Level") | Min: 2 |
| Occupants | |
| [Animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") | |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| BronzeWaterCaveExterior, BronzeWaterCave | |
| Region | |
| [The Pale](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Pale "Skyrim:The Pale") | |
| Location | |
| West of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") East-southeast of [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") | |

Bronze Water Cave

**Bronze Water Cave** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") west of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). It contains only one zone, *[Bronze Water Cave](#Bronze_Water_Cave)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Blindsighted](/wiki/Skyrim:Blindsighted "Skyrim:Blindsighted")**: Stop [Mercer Frey](/wiki/Skyrim:Mercer_Frey "Skyrim:Mercer Frey").
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Beneath Bronze Waters](/wiki/Skyrim:Beneath_Bronze_Waters "Skyrim:Beneath Bronze Waters")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Investigate the waters outside Bronze Water Cave.

### Exterior

Fishing supplies

Fishing supplies

The entrance to the cave is on the north shore of the semi-frozen [Lake Yorgrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Lake_Yorgrim "Skyrim:Lake Yorgrim"). Several Dwemer bronze pipes on either side and in front of the entrance seem to be distributing hot water or steam into the lake.

### Bronze Water Cave

Bronze Water Cave interior

Upon entering, there is a short tunnel that opens into a small chamber containing more pipes along the walls. Two leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals") have made this cave their home. On the ground are various bones, both human and animal, as well as blood and gore. Among the debris is a random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions"). Against the east wall is an unlocked Dwemer [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), and farther to the south (toward the exit), beside the same pipe, is an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel").

The cave's main purpose is to serve as an escape route from the flooded *[Irkngthand Sanctuary](/wiki/Skyrim:Irkngthand#Irkngthand_Sanctuary "Skyrim:Irkngthand")* near the end of the [Thieves Guild](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction) "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") quest [Blindsighted](/wiki/Skyrim:Blindsighted "Skyrim:Blindsighted"), with the exit from *Irkngthand Sanctuary* in the back of the cave. During the quest, this cave will not contain any animals. After completion of the quest, Bronze Water Cave can be used to access *Irkngthand Sanctuary*.

## Bugs

- The [Dwarven spider](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Spider "Skyrim:Dwarven Spider") ambush outside Bronze Water Cave can be triggered prematurely due to the spiders not being disabled before the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") quest [Beneath Bronze Waters](/wiki/Skyrim:Beneath_Bronze_Waters "Skyrim:Beneath Bronze Waters"). If the ambush is triggered prematurely, the quest will then be impossible to start, as the spiders are required for the quest.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.2.9a, fixes this bug.
- The trigger box for Kinthal's Saints bandit camp at Bronze Water Cave may attempt to disable itself even though it's controlled by an enable parent.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.3.2, addresses this issue. The DisableWhenDone flag has been removed as it's also flagged DoOnce and won't trigger again anyway.

## Maps

- 

  Bronze Water Cave

# Skyrim:Brood Cavern

## Overview

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [SR-mapicon-Cave.png](/wiki/File:SR-mapicon-Cave.png) | Cave: Brood Cavern ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Brood+Cavern)) | | |

Brood Cavern

**Brood Cavern** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal") containing leveled [animals](/wiki/Skyrim:Animals "Skyrim:Animals"). It contains only one zone, *[Brood Cavern](#Brood_Cavern)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Animal Extermination](/wiki/Skyrim:Animal_Extermination_(B) "Skyrim:Animal Extermination (B)")**: Fulfill a contract given to the [Companions](/wiki/Skyrim:Companions "Skyrim:Companions") to clear out a beast den. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Salty Sea-Dogs](/wiki/Skyrim:Salty_Sea-Dogs "Skyrim:Salty Sea-Dogs")**: Find some [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine-Cut_Void_Salts "Skyrim:Fine-Cut Void Salts") for an inexperienced [sea captain](/wiki/Skyrim:Captain_Wayfinder "Skyrim:Captain Wayfinder"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant")) The target of this quest will be found in the first chest by the dead hunter.
- **[A New Order](/wiki/Skyrim:A_New_Order "Skyrim:A New Order")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Recruit [Isran](/wiki/Skyrim:Isran "Skyrim:Isran")'s old allies for the [Dawnguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard_(faction) "Skyrim:Dawnguard (faction)"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

### Exterior

A stream flows out of the cave, forming a waterfall over a small cliff in front of the entrance. A [dead Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit_(dead) "Skyrim:Khajiit (dead)") can be found at the base of the waterfall, with a troll skull and a humanoid skull nearby. An [iron ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Iron Ore Vein") is just east of the entrance.

### Brood Cavern

Fishing supplies

The partially flooded cavern features two waterfalls flowing down the cave walls, with a stream leading back out the entrance. Many scenic plants grow in the cavern, but only three [fly amanita](/wiki/Skyrim:Fly_Amanita "Skyrim:Fly Amanita") fungus and a few [hanging moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") are harvestable. The cavern contains three leveled animals or other creatures, which may include [cave bears](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear "Skyrim:Cave Bear") or [trolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll "Skyrim:Troll"). As you enter, on the left is the corpse of a female [Redguard](/wiki/Skyrim:Redguard "Skyrim:Redguard") [hunter](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunter "Skyrim:Hunter") near a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), with a random [poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Poison "Skyrim:Poison"), a random [bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Bow "Skyrim:Bow"), and some random [arrows](/wiki/Skyrim:Arrows "Skyrim:Arrows") next to them. A copy of the [Archery](/wiki/Skyrim:Archery "Skyrim:Archery") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[The Black Arrow, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Black_Arrow,_v2 "Skyrim:The Black Arrow, v2")* can be found on the corpse. A dead [deer](/wiki/Skyrim:Deer "Skyrim:Deer") is on one of the islands of dry land. A novice-locked chest is in one of the short side tunnels off the main cavern, behind the waterfall on the right wall. A [corundum ore vein](/wiki/Skyrim:Corundum_Ore_Vein "Skyrim:Corundum Ore Vein") is just to the left of the waterfall at the rear of the room, and an iron ore vein is on the south wall.

With the [Fishing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing") [Creation](/wiki/Skyrim:Creation_Club "Skyrim:Creation Club") installed, some [Fishing Supplies](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_Supplies "Skyrim:Fishing Supplies") can be found here; fish from [Underground](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing_(activity)#Biomes "Skyrim:Fishing (activity)") waters can be found here.

## Notes

- If you return to the cave after initially clearing it, the dead hunter, poison, bow, and arrows may not respawn. Technically the dead hunter does respawn, if enter console command `prid 2ffec` then enter `inv`, you will notice her inventory updates as usual, but the body doesn't show.
- According to the [Creation Kit](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Creation_Kit "Skyrim Mod:Creation Kit"), the dead hunter is named **Urwa**.

## Maps

- 

  Brood Cavern

# Skyrim:Brother Verulus

## Overview

| Brother Verulus (RefID: 0001BB8F) | | | |

| Race | [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") | Gender | Male |
| Level | 6 | Class | [Priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") |
| [RefID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001BB8F | [BaseID](/wiki/Skyrim:NPCs#Console_IDs "Skyrim:NPCs") | 0001338C |

Brother Verulus

**Brother Verulus** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [priest](/wiki/Skyrim:Priest "Skyrim:Priest") residing in the [Hall of the Dead](/wiki/Skyrim:Hall_of_the_Dead_(Markarth) "Skyrim:Hall of the Dead (Markarth)") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). He can initially be found outside of the hall in [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"), having an argument with [Thongvor Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thongvor_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thongvor Silver-Blood").

He wears a set of [hooded monk robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Hooded_Monk_Robes "Skyrim:Hooded Monk Robes") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#000bacd7 "Skyrim:Clothing"). He carries the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth_Hall_of_the_Dead_Key "Skyrim:Markarth Hall of the Dead Key") to the Hall of the Dead along with a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). In combat, he relies on an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") or a [staff of frostbite](/wiki/Skyrim:Staff_of_Frostbite "Skyrim:Staff of Frostbite"). Being a priest he knows a decent set of spells. From the school of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), he knows [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh") and [Stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Stoneflesh"). From the school of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), he knows [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt") and [Sparks](/wiki/Skyrim:Sparks "Skyrim:Sparks"). From the school of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), he knows [Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing"), [Grand Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Grand_Healing "Skyrim:Grand Healing"), [Lesser Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Ward "Skyrim:Lesser Ward"), [Turn Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Turn_Undead_(spell) "Skyrim:Turn Undead (spell)"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing"), and [Turn Lesser Undead](/wiki/Skyrim:Turn_Lesser_Undead "Skyrim:Turn Lesser Undead").

He starts his day within Understone Keep at 8am, and will wander around the Keep for the entire day, eating at noon and at 6pm, before going to sleep at midnight.

## Related Quests

- **[The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death")**: Prepare a feast for the [Lady of Decay](/wiki/Lore:Namira "Lore:Namira").

## Quest Related Events

Upon entering Understone Keep for the first time, you will witness a heated argument between Brother Verulus and [Thongvor Silver-Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Thongvor_Silver-Blood "Skyrim:Thongvor Silver-Blood"):

:   **Thongvor**: *"What are you hiding, priest?"*
:   **Verulus**: *"I'm not hiding anything. It's closed for a reason."*
:   **Thongvor**: *"Typical Imperial lies. First you take away Talos, now you're keeping us from seeing our honored dead? You and [the Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") will answer for any desecration of my ancestors' bodies."*
:   **Verulus**: *"That's enough, Thongvor. We're done."*

You can ask him some questions if you talk to him:

:   **What's the Hall of the Dead?**

    :   *"New to Skyrim? I was confused at first, too. The Nords call their mausoleums the Hall of the Dead. It's where people in the city are buried. Fathers. Forefathers. Mothers. Foremothers."*
:   **Who's Arkay?**

    :   *"Arkay. One of the Eight Divines. God of the Cycle of Birth and Death. It is his shrine people pray to when they visit the Hall. That his divinity will watch over their ancestors on the way to the next life."*

After the conversation with Thongvor, walking up to Verulus and engaging him in conversation will make him immediately say:

:   *"If it's about the Hall of the Dead, no, you can't go in there."*
:   **Why not?**

    :   *"I can't talk about it. Rest assured, the Jarl hears everyone's concerns. You will be able to visit the dead again soon."*

Then, you have several options:

| Option | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| I could help if you tell me. **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"All right. I was going to suggest the Jarl hire someone to sort this mess out, anyway."* | | | |
| Would some coin help? **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: *"Well, the Priesthood of Arkay always accepts generous donations."* **Failed**: *"That's not going to work."* | | | |
| I don't like being ignored. **(Intimidate)** | **Failed**: *"Then my answer is the Hall of the Dead is closed. By order of the Jarl. Understand?"* | | | |
| I'll come back later, then. | *"Arkay keep you and protect you."* | | | |

Succeeding in convincing him to tell you will trigger the quest [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death"). He will explain further what is going on:

:   *"We've discovered that some of the dead have been... eaten. Flesh has been chewed off, bones were snapped to get at the marrow inside. We haven't caught anyone or anything yet. It's like it knows when I'm there. If you can get to the bottom of this, the Priesthood of Arkay will reward you. Take my key, and be careful."*

Once you have returned to him, tasked from [Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola") to lure him into her trap, he will anxiously say:

:   *"You've returned. What happened in the Hall of the Dead?"*
:   **The Hall of the Dead is safe now.**

    :   *"Divines preserve you, you're a hero. We'll re-open the Hall right away. Here. Take my amulet as a reward."*

If you chose to kill Eola, you have an option to say:

:   **Your cannibal has been taken care of.**

    :   *"I don't need to know the details. Blessings of Arkay to you for your help. Here. Take my amulet as a reward."*

If instead you chose to spare Eola, you will need to speak to Brother Verulus again:

:   **I have need of a priest in my travels.**

    :   *"You are looking for Arkay's protection while you delve some dank tomb, I take it? My duties keep me busy in Markarth. I don't know if I can help you."*

At this point, you have several options:

| Option | Dialogue |
| --- | --- |
| There would be treasure to share... **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"Treasure, you say? I suppose the Jarl won't mind if I'm gone for a little while. Lead on. **Failed**: You know, in the Priesthood of Arkay, we have a joke about an empty pocket being better than a full grave."* | | | |
| I'm willing to pay. **(Bribe)** | **Passed**: *"That's no small amount of coin, friend. I suppose I can come with you for a short venture. Lead on. **Failed**: I'm just not up for it, sorry. I'd rather stay here, have a glass of wine, and perform my rites to Arkay in peace."* | | | |
| You're coming with me. Now. **(Intimidate)** | **Failed**: *"I think you need to calm down before I summon the guards."* | | | |
| Never mind, then. | *"Arkay watch over you."* | | | |

The perfect feast

While following you during the quest, he may occasionally say one of the following:

:   *"Don't worry, Arkay's protection is absolute."*

:   *"Don't worry, the Eight are watching over us. I hope."*

Upon successfully luring him to the chamber where he is to be sacrificed, he will be hypnotized by Eola:

:   **Verulus**: *"Who... who are you? What's going on?"*
:   **Eola**: *"Priest of Arkay. I'm your friend."*
:   **Verulus**: *"You're my... friend...."*
:   **Eola**: *"Yes. I'm your friend, and I've invited you to dinner."*
:   **Verulus**: *"I've been invited to dinner.... I'm so hungry...."*
:   **Eola**: *"Why don't you lay down and rest, while we get the meal ready?"*
:   **Verulus**: *"I need to lay down. I'll just be a minute...."*

If you make Brother Verulus sleep and then decide to kill everyone in the room, he will wake up in a daze.

:   *"What... what happened?"*
:   **It doesn't matter. You're safe.**

    :   *"Thank you. I don't know what's going on, but I think I owe you my life."*
:   **You were this close to being food.**

    :   *"Sweet Breath of Arkay, were these the cannibals that were plaguing the Hall of the Dead?"*

Regardless of your choice, he will then say:

:   *"I need to get back to Markarth. Here, take this. It's the least I can do for saving my life."*

Or, simply:

:   *"I must return to Markarth."*

If you see him later after the quest, he will occasionally say:

:   *"Thanks again for saving my life. I think I'm done with venturing outside of Markarth, though."*

## Notes

- While on the quest [The Taste of Death](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Taste_of_Death "Skyrim:The Taste of Death"), once having asked him to accompany you to [Reachcliff Cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Reachcliff_Cave "Skyrim:Reachcliff Cave"), Brother Verulus will follow you everywhere until he is brought to [Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola"). Thus, he may be used as a powerful follower in addition to any [follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") you may already have if you postpone returning to Reachcliff Cave, although it might be important to note that you can only add items to his inventory (Via follower commands(Hold the Talk button on him)) but there is no way of dismissing him or getting your items back from him other than eating him.

## Bugs

- If you kill [Eola](/wiki/Skyrim:Eola "Skyrim:Eola") in the Hall of the Dead and report back to Verulus, he will approach and speak to you every time you are near him at [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep").
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.7, fixes this bug.
- Several coffins and other graves for NPCs in the Markarth Hall of the Dead were not initially disabled like they should be, resulting in them showing up as all belonging to Brother Verulus until the assigned NPC actually dies.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.2, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12200))
- If Thongvor Silver-Blood is exiled and you enter Understone Keep for the first time, Brother Verulus will not be standing around waiting for him in order to run the scene about the Hall of the Dead being closed.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- Verulus cannot be persuaded to follow you to Reachcliff Cave without a bribe (or the [Amulet of Articulation](/wiki/Skyrim:Amulet_of_Articulation "Skyrim:Amulet of Articulation")), because the Speech check is done on Verulus instead of yourself.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 2.0.9, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=18667))
- Brother Verulus may still stand around waiting on Thongvor after the Stormcloaks take Markarth because his AI package wasn't checking Thongvor's government faction status.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Brothers in Irons

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Investigate a wanted criminal.** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | *[Nightgate Inn Patron's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn_Patron%27s_Note "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn Patron's Note")*, [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn") |
| Location(s): | [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"), [Clam Digger's Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Haafingar#Clam_Digger.27s_Camp "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Haafingar") |
| Reward: | Full set of enchanted [iron plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron#Iron_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Iron") armor |
| ID: | ccBGSSSE052\_Quest |
| Added by: | [Alternative Armors - Iron](/wiki/Skyrim:Alternative_Armors_-_Iron "Skyrim:Alternative Armors - Iron") |

Brothers in Irons

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Nightgate Inn Patron's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn_Patron%27s_Note "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn Patron's Note")* in [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn").
2. Investigate the barrel behind the inn.
3. Read the *[Undercover Guard's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Undercover_Guard%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Undercover Guard's Journal")*.
4. Investigate the [camp site](/wiki/Skyrim:Unmarked_Places_Haafingar#Clam_Digger.27s_Camp "Skyrim:Unmarked Places Haafingar").
5. Inspect Pale-Eyes' body.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The barrel behind the inn

To start this quest, read the *[Nightgate Inn Patron's Note](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn_Patron%27s_Note "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn Patron's Note")* in [Nightgate Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightgate_Inn "Skyrim:Nightgate Inn"). The note mentions the barrel behind the Inn, investigate the barrel and you will find *[Undercover Guard's Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Undercover_Guard%27s_Journal "Skyrim:Undercover Guard's Journal")*. The journal mentions that a wanted criminal, [Pale-Eyes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale-Eyes "Skyrim:Pale-Eyes") is camping out west of Northwatch Keep.

As you arrive at the camp, you will find a Thalmor wizard and two Thalmor soldiers, once you have dealt with them you can search the corpse of Pale-Eyes to find a full set of enchanted [iron plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron#Iron_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Iron") armor. Once you take [his journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Pale-Eyes%27_Journal "Skyrim:Pale-Eyes' Journal"), the quest will finish.

## Notes

- The camp is actually at a secondary location known as the "Clamdigger's Camp" not far from the Icewater Jetty.
- The Undercover Guard's Journal can remain as a quest item.

## Quest Stages

| Brothers in Irons (ccBGSSSE052\_Quest) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 1 |  | At Nightgate Inn, I found a journal written by an undercover guard that indicated a wanted criminal was camping out west of Northwatch Keep. By the time I arrived, he had already been killed by the Thalmor agents. After dealing with the Thalmor, I retrieved the journal from his body. |
| 10 |  | I've heard rumors about mysterious patrons passing through Nightgate Inn. Perhaps I should pay the inn a visit and see what I can uncover. *Objective 10:* Look for a note at the Nightgate Inn |
| 11 |  | I've heard rumors about mysterious patrons passing through Nightgate Inn. I found a note written by someone who stayed at the lodge. *Objective 11:* Search the barrel behind Nightgate Inn |
| 12 |  | I've heard rumors about mysterious patrons passing through Nightgate Inn. Once I arrived, I found a note on the counter that implied an Elf patron left something in a barrel behind the inn. *Objective 12:* Read the Undercover Guard's Journal |
| 20 |  | At Nightgate Inn, I found a journal written by an undercover guard that indicated a wanted criminal was camping out west of Northwatch Keep. I should head out there and see what I can find. *Objective 20:* Investigate the camp site near the northern coast |
| 30 |  | At Nightgate Inn, I found a journal written by an undercover guard that indicated a wanted criminal was camping out west of Northwatch Keep. At the camp, I encountered three Justiciars. *Objective 30:* Inspect the body |
| 1000 | ☑ | At Nightgate Inn, I found a journal written by an undercover guard that indicated a wanted criminal was camping out west of Northwatch Keep. By the time I arrived, he had already been killed by the Thalmor agents. After dealing with the Thalmor, I retrieved the journal from his body. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 40, 50, 60, 70, 80, 90, 100.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccBGSSSE052_Quest stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccBGSSSE052_Quest`.

Bruca's Leap Redoubt

**Bruca's Leap Redoubt** is a small [cave](/wiki/Skyrim:Caves "Skyrim:Caves") southwest of [Dragon Bridge](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon_Bridge "Skyrim:Dragon Bridge") containing [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn"). It contains only one zone, *[Bruca's Leap Redoubt](#Bruca.27s_Leap_Redoubt)*.

## Related Quests

- **[Bounty: Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Bounty:_Forsworn "Skyrim:Bounty: Forsworn")**: Kill a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader for a bounty reward. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The Ghost of Old Hroldan](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:The Ghost of Old Hroldan")**: Put an [ancient ghost](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghost_of_Old_Hroldan "Skyrim:Ghost of Old Hroldan") to rest. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[The House of Horrors](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Horrors "Skyrim:The House of Horrors")**: Help [Molag Bal](/wiki/Lore:Molag_Bal "Lore:Molag Bal") take revenge upon a servant of [Boethiah](/wiki/Lore:Boethiah "Lore:Boethiah"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Kill the Forsworn Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Forsworn_Leader_(Jarl) "Skyrim:Kill the Forsworn Leader (Jarl)")**: Do a favor for [Jarl Igmund](/wiki/Skyrim:Igmund "Skyrim:Igmund") by killing a [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Lisbet's Missing Shipment](/wiki/Skyrim:Lisbet%27s_Missing_Shipment "Skyrim:Lisbet's Missing Shipment")**: Retrieve a missing Dibella Statue for a struggling store. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

The exterior campsite

Two Forsworn, one a melee fighter and the other an archer, have made camp outside the cave entrance. The campsite features a [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest"), five bedrolls, and a [tanning rack](/wiki/Skyrim:Tanning_Rack "Skyrim:Tanning Rack"). Also in the area are two [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") fungi, a [chickens' nest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken%27s_Egg "Skyrim:Chicken's Egg"), and a [chicken](/wiki/Skyrim:Chicken "Skyrim:Chicken").

### Bruca's Leap Redoubt

The main chamber

The cave interior is quite small, consisting of a curving passage leading down to a chamber with wooden scaffolding. The [Forsworn Briarheart](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn_Briarheart "Skyrim:Forsworn Briarheart") shaman and its melee fighter bodyguard will likely be immediately alerted to your presence. However, by sneaking, you may snipe at them from the window-like opening straight down from the entrance. An [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") is on the ledge nearby. At the bottom of the passage is a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a [Dwarven arrow](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Arrow "Skyrim:Dwarven Arrow").

Lying on a table in the chamber is the corpse of a Forsworn fighter who was in the process of being transformed into a Briarheart, with his [heart](/wiki/Skyrim:Human_Heart "Skyrim:Human Heart") and an iron dagger placed nearby. A [bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Bear Pelt"), a [cave bear pelt](/wiki/Skyrim:Cave_Bear_Pelt "Skyrim:Cave Bear Pelt"), and two [cow hides](/wiki/Skyrim:Cow_Hide "Skyrim:Cow Hide") are scattered around, and an [ingredient barrel](/wiki/Skyrim:Barrel "Skyrim:Barrel") of uncommon quality is near the table. A bookshelf holds a copy of the [Enchanting](/wiki/Skyrim:Enchanting "Skyrim:Enchanting") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[A Tragedy in Black](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Tragedy_in_Black "Skyrim:A Tragedy in Black")*, a few ingredients (including one sample each of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), [sabre cat tooth](/wiki/Skyrim:Sabre_Cat_Tooth "Skyrim:Sabre Cat Tooth"), [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), and [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap")), and an [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") of uncommon quality. A random [potion](/wiki/Skyrim:Potions "Skyrim:Potions") is in a bucket nearby. The boss chest is behind the bookshelf, but beware the [bear trap](/wiki/Skyrim:Bear_Trap "Skyrim:Bear Trap") in front of it.

A few fungi grow in the cave, including one [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort"), three Namira's rot, and one white cap.

## Bugs

- Bruca's Leap Redoubt isn't marked as a cave, so cave-based radiant quests won't target it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, fixes this bug.
- The Forsworn members here may attack their own chickens.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.1.1, addresses this issue. Both factions have been set to be friendly towards one another to prevent this from happening.
- The cave contains a goat hide you cannot interact with.

## Maps

- 

  Bruca's Leap Redoubt

# Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House

## Overview

Brunwulf Free-Winter's House

**Brunwulf Free-Winter's House** is the home of [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter") in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

It is a one story house, with a partial loft area located in Windhelm near the main entrance. Next door to [Aretino Residence](/wiki/Skyrim:Aretino_Residence "Skyrim:Aretino Residence"), almost directly opposite [Calixto's House of Curiosities](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto%27s_House_of_Curiosities "Skyrim:Calixto's House of Curiosities"). It consists of only one zone, *[Brunwulf Free-Winter's House](#Brunwulf_Free-Winter.27s_House)*.

## Residents

| Name |
| --- |
| [Brunwulf Free-Winter](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter")  [Korir](/wiki/Skyrim:Korir "Skyrim:Korir")\*  [Thaena](/wiki/Skyrim:Thaena "Skyrim:Thaena")\*  [Assur](/wiki/Skyrim:Assur "Skyrim:Assur")\* |

\* These people will only move here if Winterhold is under Imperial control.

## Brunwulf Free-Winter's House

The interior of the Free-Winter household

The entrance has a novice level lock. The entry leads straight into the main living area, with a practice dummy and a pile of firewood against the south wall. There are quite a few sacks of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") around the whole house. To the west of the entrance is a flight of wooden stairs up to a small loft area and behind the stairs is a small square wooden table with a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), two [salmon steaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Salmon_Steak "Skyrim:Salmon Steak"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a couple of wedges of cheese on top. Against the west wall is a small set of shelves holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine") and a bottle of Nord mead. Against the north wall is a dresser containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") with two [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot") and a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") on top. Further to the right still against the north wall is a long wooden table holding a [mammoth snout](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Snout "Skyrim:Mammoth Snout"), three [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato"), three bulbs of [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic"), a bunch of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a salt pile, a loaf of bread, a [sweet roll](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and three [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"). Right of this is a fire pit with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") over it and a chair in front. By the chair is a copy of *[Immortal Blood](/wiki/Skyrim:Immortal_Blood "Skyrim:Immortal Blood")*. Beside the fire pit is a narrow wooden table holding a haunch of raw [venison](/wiki/Skyrim:Venison "Skyrim:Venison"), a [potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato") and a loaf of bread, with three wall shelves holding various skulls beside the table and hanging from the wall beside the shelves is a [hunting bow](/wiki/Skyrim:Hunting_Bow "Skyrim:Hunting Bow"). There is a doorway through into a bedroom to the east, with a bookcase to the left holding four common books. To the right of the doorway is a wall shelf holding a set of [hide armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Armor "Skyrim:Hide Armor"), [bracers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Bracers "Skyrim:Hide Bracers"), [shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Shield "Skyrim:Hide Shield") and [helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Helmet "Skyrim:Helmet"), a [potion of the berserker](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_the_Berserker "Skyrim:Potion of the Berserker") and an [iron greatsword](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Greatsword "Skyrim:Iron Greatsword") leaning against the wall beside it. Under the shelf is a long unlocked [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing gold. To the right, in an alcove on the south wall is a large round wooden table holding an [iron battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Battleaxe "Skyrim:Iron Battleaxe") and [troll skull](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Skull "Skyrim:Troll Skull").

The bedroom is very small consisting of a single owned bed opposite the doorway in the northeastern corner, with a respawning [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") on the floor by the head of the bed, which contains leveled items. Against the east wall is a small unit holding a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a [leather strip](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Strips "Skyrim:Leather Strips"). In the southeast corner is a corner shelf holding a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health"), with a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum") on the floor beside it. To the right, against the south wall is a small cupboard with an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace") and eight loose [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") on top. The loft area is very small and only contains a couple of barrels, one of which contains food.

## Notes

- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") to the bottom right of the entrance door.
- All containers; with the exception of most barrels, sacks, and the knapsack; are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.
