Brunwulf Free-Winter

*"It's not that simple. Ulfric wants a Skyrim for the Nords."*

**Brunwulf Free-Winter** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") who lives on the east side of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He is known for standing up for the [Dunmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Dark_Elf "Skyrim:Dark Elf") and [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian") in the city and thus openly goes against the opinions of his fellow Nords [Rolff Stone-Fist](/wiki/Skyrim:Rolff_Stone-Fist "Skyrim:Rolff Stone-Fist") and [Angrenor Once-Honored](/wiki/Skyrim:Angrenor_Once-Honored "Skyrim:Angrenor Once-Honored"). He'd be happy to reward you for [clearing a bandit hideout](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader"). Brunwulf is made [jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Windhelm if [Ulfric Stormcloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulfric_Stormcloak "Skyrim:Ulfric Stormcloak") is deposed by the [Imperial Legion](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial_Legion "Skyrim:Imperial Legion"), and he enacts a more tolerant administration of the hold.

According to townsfolk and Brunwulf himself, he is a veteran of the [Great War](/wiki/Lore:Great_War "Lore:Great War") against the Aldmeri Dominion's invasion of the empire of Tamriel. However, despite being recognized a war hero by many, Brunwulf explains he is not proud of this title and claims that the war had not given any glory to anyone.

Brunwulf wakes at 7am to eat breakfast for one hour, then heads to the local marketplace at 8am, browsing the stands for four hours. At noon, where he goes to depends on the day: on [Morndas](/wiki/Lore:Calendar#Days_of_the_Week "Lore:Calendar"), Middas, and Fredas, he heads to the [Palace of the Kings](/wiki/Skyrim:Palace_of_the_Kings "Skyrim:Palace of the Kings"), staying there for four hours. On Tirdas and Turdas, he goes back [home](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf_Free-Winter%27s_House "Skyrim:Brunwulf Free-Winter's House") for a four-hour nap. On Loredas and Sundas, he goes to the [Temple of Talos](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Talos "Skyrim:Temple of Talos") for a four-hour visit. Either way, at 4pm he enters [Candlehearth Hall](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlehearth_Hall "Skyrim:Candlehearth Hall"). After four hours, he exits the Hall to patrol the city until midnight, when he returns home to sleep.

When he becomes the jarl of Windhelm, he'll move in to the Palace of the Kings. His schedule will also change: he will sleep from 10pm to 8am, waking up to perform his duties as jarl, sitting in the throne and holding court.

He wears [scaled horn armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Horn_Armor "Skyrim:Scaled Horn Armor") with matching [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Scaled_Boots "Skyrim:Scaled Boots"), and carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic"), his [house key](/wiki/Skyrim:Brunwulf%27s_House_Key "Skyrim:Brunwulf's House Key"), and some [upper-class items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader")**: Do a favor by slaying a bandit leader. ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Thane of Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Eastmarch "Skyrim:Thane of Eastmarch")**: Gain the title of [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

- This NPC is one of many potential quest givers or quest targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_NPCs "Skyrim:Radiant").

## Dialogue

Upon arriving to the Gray Quarter for the first time, [Malthyr Elenil](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") can be seen convincing Brunwulf to speak with Ulfric Stormcloak, leader of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks") and the current jarl of Windhelm.

:   **Malthyr:** *"You're a war hero, Brunwulf. Ulfric will listen to you."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"It's not that simple. Ulfric wants a Skyrim for the Nords. He doesn't trust what he calls outsiders."*
:   **Malthyr:** *"You've seen how we live -- cramped alleys, run-down buildings, few guard patrols. Even the name "Gray Quarter" is an insult."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"I'll speak to Ulfric soon, but I make no promises that I can change his mind."*
:   **Malthyr:** *"That's all I ask. With your help, we have a chance to make a better life for ourselves here. For that, I thank you."*

After the conversation above, Brunwulf will resume his normal schedule.

Should you approach him, he'll have a few comments on the reality of war:

:   *"There's no glory in war. It's just something they tell soldiers so they'll risk their lives."*

:   *"They call me a war hero. I'm no hero, I'm just a soldier who didn't want to die."*

He may also comment on the [civil war](/wiki/Skyrim:Civil_War "Skyrim:Civil War"):

:   *"The sooner this war ends, the sooner we can all get on with our lives."*

He can also be heard remarking about Ulfric's prejudiced views:

:   *"If Ulfric had his way, anyone who wasn't a Nord would be shipped right out of Skyrim."*

He will usually end conversations by saying *"Farewell, then."*

Upon your first time speaking to him when he is not jarl, he'll ask you,

:   *"You one of those "Skyrim for the Nords" types?"*

If you are a Nord, you can reply in two ways:

:   **Yes. Anyone who's not a Nord is a trespasser.**

    :   *"Is that so? You ought to join the Stormcloaks, if you haven't already. Seems to me they're a bunch of narrow-minded bigots, just like you. Meantime, you best steer clear of me."*
:   **No. Skyrim's big enough for everyone.**

    :   *"Good. Too many Nords in this town have been listening to Ulfric's narrow-minded words. He's tough, loyal to his men and a good leader, but if you're not a Nord, Ulfric will never trust you."*

If you are not a Nord, your dialogue options will instead be:

:   **Yes. Outsiders like me have no place here.**

    :   *"That's just what Ulfric wants you to think. If that's what you really believe, then you're a fool. Never had much patience for fools, myself."*
:   **I think all folk should be welcome here.**

    :   *"And you're right, at least as far as I'm concerned. Don't let Ulfric or some of these other short-sighted Nords bother you. Most of us are happy to welcome newcomers."*

If you say that you think Skyrim is for everyone, he will start to [like](/wiki/Skyrim:Disposition "Skyrim:Disposition") you. To reflect this increase in disposition, he may wish you well with the following statement, regardless of your character's gender:

:   *"Safe journeys, sword-brother."*

On the other hand, answering that Skyrim should only be inhabited by Nords will cause him to start to dislike you. Instead of greeting you, he can be found trying to ignore you. He says either of these lines regardless of your character's actual race and gender.

:   *"I told you, I've got no patience for fools. Keep walking."*

:   *"Got no time for a Nord who thinks he's better than everyone else. Keep walking."*

You can ask him about the Dark Elves, and he'll explain what the conversation between him and Malthyr was about.

:   **Why help the dark elves?**
:   *"Help the Dark Elves? Oh, you must have heard me talking to Malthyr.
    The Dark Elves live in a run-down slum called the Gray Quarter. Ulfric's content to keep it that way.
    I guess they think I can open Ulfric's eyes to their plight, and get him to lift a finger on their behalf.
    I'm trying, but Ulfric is set in his ways. For him, there's two kinds of people in this world -- Nords, and the folk beneath them."*

You can also mention that Malthyr called him a war hero, and Brunwulf will explain why. It turns out that he has a rather bleak opinion about the Great War.

:   **That dark elf called you a war hero.**
:   *"I killed a lot of High Elves in the Great War, and I didn't die. I guess that makes me a war hero.
    The "Great War"- there was nothing great about it. Thousands died on both sides and where did we end up?
    Did we really save the Empire or did we just plant the seeds for Ulfric's uprising and another war?"*

*"Being a Jarl isn't something I ever wanted, but if I can help these people, then I will."*

After the victory of the [siege of Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm"), [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") will give a speech, mentioning why Brunwulf will be appointed to rule the city: *"We are turning the city over to Brunwulf Free-Winter, an honorable and faithful man. Many of you will be staying in Windhelm to aid the Jarl in restoring order and stamping out any embers of rebellion that may still smolder here."*

When he becomes the jarl of Windhelm, he'll have new greetings, mostly on working to rebuild the city.

:   *"It'll take time to rebuild, but the Nords are no strangers to hard work."*

:   *"The dark elves and Argonians won't soon forget Ulfric's prejudice, but I'm doing what I can to repair that rift."*

:   *"Being a Jarl isn't something I ever wanted, but if I can help these people, then I will."*

:   *"My time is limited, so speak quickly."*

His other dialogue will also be replaced with a new set to better suit his position as jarl. You can ask him how he is settling into his new role, and he'll answer, elaborating on the difficulties of repairing Windhelm. You can also ask about any potential plans to renovate the Gray Quarter, and whether or not the Argonians will ever be allowed into the city.

:   **How are you settling into your new role?**
:   *"Every day is a struggle, but a Nord doesn't back down from a fight when the cause is honorable.
    I just wish things were simpler. In my days as a soldier, I knew who the enemy was, and how to defeat him.
    Unfortunately, a sword can't repair damaged buildings, feed hungry people or undo years of prejudice."*
:   **Any plans to renovate the Gray Quarter?**
:   *"I've taken the first steps toward doing so already.
    I met with several of the Dark Elves to discuss improvements in the Gray Quarter, but we have no real plans as of yet.
    First we'll need to refill our coffers and stockpile stone and wood. The war took a heavy toll on Windhelm's resources.
    But I swore an oath to our Dunmer friends that, for as long as I sit on the throne of Windhelm, their needs will not be ignored."*
:   **Will you let the Argonians into the city?**
:   *"I'd like to, but it's not as simple as that.
    Most of the folk in the city believe as Ulfric did, that outsiders should not be trusted.
    Until those people learn to accept the Argonians, they must remain outside, for their own safety.
    Old habits don't die easily, and we Nords can be as stubborn as stone."*

It turns out that many of Windhelm's non-Nord citizens are optimistic about the city's conditions improving now that Ulfric is gone. Should you ask [Aval Atheron](/wiki/Skyrim:Aval_Atheron "Skyrim:Aval Atheron"), a Dunmer merchant, if things have changed much with the Empire in charge, he'll first tell you, *"Well, not yet. The Empire hasn't been in charge for that long, and real change takes time."* He'll continue, expressing his hopes, *"Still, having a just and honorable man like Brunwulf in charge can only be an improvement. Unlike Ulfric, Brunwulf has shown a great willingness to work with the other races and make us feel more at home here."* He'll end with a mix of relief and optimism, *"For the first time in a long while, I truly believe that there are brighter days ahead."*

### Quest-Related Events

To start his version of the quest [Kill the Bandit Leader](/wiki/Skyrim:Kill_the_Bandit_Leader "Skyrim:Kill the Bandit Leader"), ask him if Ulfric doesn't care about outsiders. He'll explain the situation. If you refuse the quest, the rest of the conversation is very simple:

:   **That's too bad.**
:   *"Yes. It is."*

If you accept the quest, Brunwulf will commend you for offering to take care of the bandits.

:   **Ulfric doesn't care about outsiders?**
:   *"Whenever a group of marauders attack a Nord village, Ulfric is the first to sound the horn and send the men.
    But a group of Dark Elf refugees gets ambushed? A group of [Argonians](/wiki/Skyrim:Argonian "Skyrim:Argonian"), or a [Khajiit](/wiki/Skyrim:Khajiit "Skyrim:Khajiit") caravan? No troops. No investigation. Nothing.
    There's a group of cutthroats out there right now that Ulfric doesn't lift a finger to bring to justice, as long as they don't threaten Nord land."*
:   *"That's a brave offer. I'd be happy to throw in my coin behind that.
    You deal with them, I'll make sure you get paid. Maybe this old soldier will throw in some lessons as well."*

You'll be given a random dungeon in [Eastmarch](/wiki/Skyrim:Eastmarch "Skyrim:Eastmarch") to clear. If you have accepted the quest, Brunwulf will say the following after you exit the conversation:

:   *"Show those marauders what Windhelm justice tastes like."*

Once you've cleared your assigned dungeon of bandits, mention this to Brunwulf. He'll be grateful, and will reward you with leveled gold and a lesson in [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor").

:   **<Dungeon Name> is free of bandits.**
:   *"Now that's good work. Everyone will be a lot safer with them gone, Dark Elf and Nord alike.
    Here, some gold as promised, and let me show you a bit about wearing heavy armor. Save you some aches on a long march."*

### Conversations

While shopping, Aval Atheron may offer a discount to him for his efforts to help the Dunmer, though Brunwulf will politely refuse:

:   **Aval:** *"Friend Brunwulf, how good to see you! If you see anything you like, just let me know and I'll glad offer you a discount."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"That's not necessary. I'll pay the same price as anyone else."*
:   **Aval:** *"But I insist. and with good reason. [Malthyr](/wiki/Skyrim:Malthyr_Elenil "Skyrim:Malthyr Elenil") told me that you've been speaking to Ulfric about our situation. He said you're going to help us. So few Nords have ever offered to help us, a discount is the least I can do."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"I'm not looking for special treatment, Aval. All I did was talk to Ulfric. For all I know, he's already forgotten the conversation. I wouldn't get your hopes up."*
:   **Aval:** *"Oh, I see. Well, I'm sorry to have troubled you about it. Just... know that your efforts are appreciated."*

At Candlehearth Hall, he may chat with his lover, [Elda Early-Dawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Elda_Early-Dawn "Skyrim:Elda Early-Dawn"). She'll mockingly scold him for flirting with her:

:   **Elda:** *"Tell me about the Great War. I hear you were in the battle of..."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"Elda, honey, let's not talk about the war. It's in the past."*
:   **Elda:** *"I'm sorry. What would you like to talk about?"*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"Hows*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")] *about we figure out some way to keep warm tonight?"*
:   **Elda:** *"Oh! You behave, now!"*

Brunwulf may also ask about the inn, and Elda will explain why she is still running the establishment instead of retiring.

:   **Brunwulf:** *"How long have you run this place, again?"*
:   **Elda:** *"Nearly thirty years, now."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"Just wondering when you'll be ready to give it up and settle down. Seems like you're always working."*
:   **Elda:** *"I just feel like if I'm not here, then something could go wrong. [Nils](/wiki/Skyrim:Nils "Skyrim:Nils") is a hard worker, but I wouldn't trust him to run things."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"One of these days he'll have to learn."*
:   **Elda:** *"Perhaps. But not today."*

Brunwulf and Elda may also discuss building a cabin near Riften.

:   **Brunwulf:** *"I've been thinking about building that cabin we talked about."*
:   **Elda:** *"Oh? Where?"*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"There's a clear spot just west of Riften. You know the area?"*
:   **Elda:** *"I've been there before, but I don't know it well."*
:   **Brunwulf:** *"Well that's where I want to build. In the fall forest. Give it an easterly view. The sunrise is almost as pretty as you are."*
:   **Elda:** *"That sounds lovely. You're very sweet."*

## Notes

- *[A Dream of Sovngarde](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Dream_of_Sovngarde "Skyrim:A Dream of Sovngarde")* is written by a "Skardan Free-Winter". There is no known connection besides a shared surname.
- Despite his seemingly kind disposition towards non-Nords, he will occasionally use the racial slur "lizard" to Argonians or "cat" to Khajiit when you exhaust his normal dialogue as either race. However, this is purely inherent to his voice type.
- If Brunwulf becomes Jarl, no housecarl will be assigned to him.

## Bugs

- After finishing the quest [Battle for Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Battle_for_Windhelm "Skyrim:Battle for Windhelm") for the Imperials, Brunwulf sometimes won't appear in the Palace of the Kings. Without him, you are unable to purchase Hjerim or become thane of Eastmarch if you have not already.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.
  - To fix this, travel out of Windhelm and return.
  -  Using the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console"), type `prid 0001B117` and enter to target Brunwulf. Then move him to your location (preferably the Palace of The Kings) with the command `moveto player`.
  - Finishing [Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice") appears to fix this as well. Brunwulf doesn't seem to pick up his jarl duties before this quest is completed.
- After becoming Jarl, Brunwulf may not get the "Jarl" prefix to his name when other new Jarls do.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
  -  This can be fixed if you select Ulfric and Galmar's corpses with the console immediately after killing them and type `addfac 0003662a -1` and `addfac 00036629 1`, and/or by disabling them.
- If Brunwulf becomes Jarl, his Kill The Bandit Leader quest may no longer be available to start, but still may be available to complete. If that is the case, he may lack the "Jarl" prefix to his name until the aforementioned quest is finished.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.4, fixes this bug.
- If the Empire wins the war, Brunwulf may still play his scene with Malthyr in the Gray Quarter if you had never been there. Likewise, Brunwulf may also play his scene with Aval in the marketplace even if the Empire had won the war. Since both scenes talk about Brunwulf speaking to Ulfric, they are no longer relevant once Ulfric is dead.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. Both scenes will now be disabled if the Empire wins the war.

Brutius

**Brutius** is an old man hosting a fishing contest. He will invite you to join him, but this is all a ruse.

His spells and perks depend on his level, see [this page](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit#Mages "Skyrim:Bandit") for details.

## Related Quests

- **[No Contest](/wiki/Skyrim:No_Contest "Skyrim:No Contest")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Fishing "Skyrim:Fishing"): Take part in a fishing contest.

### No Contest

Brutius reveals the ruse

When you first approach him:

:   **I'm here for the fishing contest. Are you ready to begin?**
:   *"Yeah."*
:   **You're Brutius? I expected someone younger. You're just a feeble old man.**
:   *"I don't have to take that from you!"*
:   **Shall we make a wager, then?**
:   *"How much?"*

:   :   **100 gold.**
    :   **500 gold.**
    :   **1000 gold!**

:   **Where shall we hold the contest?**
:   *"Here's where you need to go."*

When you meet at the specified location, he will attack you with his fellow accomplices.

## Bugs

- If you travel to Morthal during this quest causing Brutius to spawn, fail to talk to him, then visit your player home, when you return to town Brutius may have wandered away over the mountains past Labyrinthian toward Whiterun. A trigger box is not configured to be player-only activated, passing NPCs and animals may accidentally advance quest stages, so Brutius's travel packages stop working. **?**
- There may be two copies of Brutius' Journal in his inventory. Taking both of them will break the quest.[How?](/wiki/Category:Pages_Missing_Data "Category:Pages Missing Data") **?**

# Skyrim:Bryling's House

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Bryling's House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Bryling%27s+House)) | | |

Bryling's House

**Bryling's House** is a small house in [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), the home of [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling"), a [Thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude").

It is located just outside the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace") on the left-hand side, next door to the [Bards College](/wiki/Skyrim:Bards_College "Skyrim:Bards College"). Bryling spends most of her day in the palace, and her house contains lots of valuable items, making it an easy target if you are asked to steal from Solitude for [The Bedlam Job](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bedlam_Job "Skyrim:The Bedlam Job").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Bryling](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling "Skyrim:Bryling")  [Irnskar Ironhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irnskar_Ironhand "Skyrim:Irnskar Ironhand") |

## Related Quests

- This location is one of many potential targets for [one or more of the Radiant quests](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant#Quest_Locations "Skyrim:Radiant").

### Exterior

There are a flight of stairs up to the main entrance. The front door is apprentice-locked most of the time. There is a second entrance at the side of the house via a small garden which has various harvestable [plants](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") growing in it. There are also a couple of [hanging mosses](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss") growing from the walls by the stairs and around to the side of the building where there are quite a few [food](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food") barrels stacked up. An accessible horizontal ledge outside contains a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing").

| Plants |
| --- |
| 1 [Blue Mountain Flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Blue Mountain Flower")  4 [Dragon's Tongue](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragon%27s_Tongue "Skyrim:Dragon's Tongue")  2 [Hanging Moss](/wiki/Skyrim:Hanging_Moss "Skyrim:Hanging Moss")  1 [Lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender") |

#### First Floor

First floor main room

There are a number of food sacks and barrels throughout the house and the crockery is of the finest quality including [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), [goblets](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet") etc. Entering through the main entrance, the room has a narrow wooden table against the southwest wall with a [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") holding two [sweet rolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Sweet_Roll "Skyrim:Sweet Roll") and two [honey nut treats](/wiki/Skyrim:Honey_Nut_Treat "Skyrim:Honey Nut Treat") and a plate of [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") on top and a low table and chair in front. On the table is a plate of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and cheese. Along the northwest wall is an open crate containing bunch of [tundra cotton](/wiki/Skyrim:Tundra_Cotton "Skyrim:Tundra Cotton") and a [red mountain flower](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Mountain_Flower "Skyrim:Red Mountain Flower"). To the right is a small wardrobe containing [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") and with a copy of *[Uncommon Taste](/wiki/Skyrim:Uncommon_Taste "Skyrim:Uncommon Taste")* on top. In the northern corner is a round wooden table with a [candlestick](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick") on top. Opposite against the southeast wall is a cupboard containing clutter with a vase with a [snowberry](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries") bush to the left.

To the northeast is an opening that leads into a kitchen and dining area with a small reading area to the left, where there are a pair of bookcases against the southwest wall holding eleven common books, a [potion of extreme stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Extreme_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Extreme Stamina") and a [solution of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Solution_of_Strength "Skyrim:Solution of Strength"). There is a second vase containing a snowberry bush against the northwest wall and against the northeast wall is a set of shelves holding a common book, a bunch of tundra cotton, [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), a [potion of health](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Health "Skyrim:Potion of Health") and a [potion of regeneration](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Regeneration "Skyrim:Potion of Regeneration"). In the middle of this area is a low table and chair, with three common books and a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine") on the table. This part of the room is separated from the kitchen an dining area by a pair of sets of shelves and an open crate, which contains a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a bunch of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), a [potion of plentiful magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Magicka"), a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing") and two empty [lesser soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"). On the shelves are a [weak poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Poison"), a [weak stamina poison](/wiki/Skyrim:Weak_Stamina_Poison "Skyrim:Weak Stamina Poison"), two common books, a [potion of vigorous stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Vigorous_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Vigorous Stamina"), a [potion of ultimate magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Ultimate_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Ultimate Magicka") and an empty lesser soul gem, with an empty [petty soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem") on a stand beside the shelves.

In the kitchen and dining area is a long wooden table set for two with two [seared slaughterfish](/wiki/Skyrim:Seared_Slaughterfish "Skyrim:Seared Slaughterfish"), a portion of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), a potion of regeneration and a bunch of tundra cotton with a round wooden table beside the table is small round table with a loaf of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread") and a couple of cheese wheels on top. At the other end of the table is a small unit holding a bottle of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"). Against the northeast wall is a bookcase holding six common books, a potion of health, a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute") and a [drum](/wiki/Skyrim:Drum "Skyrim:Drum"). To the right in the eastern corner is a small set of shelves holding a few goblets and having an open crate in front of it containing a potion of regeneration, two [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). Against the southeast wall is a small cupboard containing more clutter, while to the right is a fireplace with a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") in front on a stand, a piece of [raw beef](/wiki/Skyrim:Raw_Beef "Skyrim:Raw Beef") underneath and a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage") in a cast iron pot on the hearth. On the mantelpiece is a bottle of [frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom").

To the southwest is an alcove with a small cupboard with an open crate on top containing two [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek") and five [tomatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Tomato "Skyrim:Tomato") against the southeast wall. Against the southwest wall is a set of shelves holding a common book, a bunch of tundra cotton, a [draught of strength](/wiki/Skyrim:Draught_of_Strength "Skyrim:Draught of Strength"), a potion of health, a potion of regeneration and a basket containing two bunches of lavender. Against the northwest wall is a narrow table with a bowl of bread and a plate holding a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"). To the northeast there is a stairwell with a flight of stairs leading up and down.

#### Second Floor

Main bedroom

At the top of the stairs is another large vase containing a snowberry bush. There is a door opposite the stairs on the southwest wall, with two single owned beds coming out from the southwest wall with end tables on the outside of both and an open crate at the foot of the left-hand bed containing a bunch of tundra cotton and a red mountain flower. Against the southwest wall is a small cupboard with a [thistle branch](/wiki/Skyrim:Thistle_Branch "Skyrim:Thistle Branch") on top. In front of the cupboard is a low table and chair with a plate of bread and cheese and a common book on top. Against the northeast wall is a narrow table with a bowl of bread, a plate holding a sliced eidar cheese and an iron dagger on top, with a wall shelf above it holding another thistle branch, while against the northwest wall is a wooden bench with a round wooden table to the left of it and two common books on top and a third underneath.

The hallway continues to the southeast where there is an alcove just past another door to the northeast. In the alcove is another low table and chair with a plate of bread and cheese and a common book on top. Against the northeast wall is a narrow wooden table with a wall shelf above, while against the southeast wall is a small cupboard holding a potion of health, a flute and a drum on top. Against the southwest wall are a pair of wall shelves holding a bunch of lavender and a [potion of plentiful healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Plentiful_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Plentiful Healing").

The bedroom to the northeast has a large owned double bed coming out from the northeast wall, with an end table on either side and a long unlocked respawning [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") at the foot of the bed containing random items. In the northern corner is a small wardrobe containing fine clothes, while in the eastern corner is a small round table with a [pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Pot "Skyrim:Pot") on top and an unlocked wooden chest containing gold beside it against the southeast wall. Against the southwest wall is a narrow wooden table holding a bowl of bread and a plate holding a sliced eidar cheese and an iron dagger. Behind the door to the northwest is a small wardrobe containing fine clothes and with a basket to the right of it containing a small [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a wash basin on a stand to the right of that.

#### Cellar

Cellar

Descending the stairs leads to a storage area with a cupboard on the right at the bottom of the stairs holding a few [empty wine bottle](/wiki/Skyrim:Empty_Wine_Bottle "Skyrim:Empty Wine Bottle"). To the northwest is a large stack of food barrels with more behind a large vat. In front of this against the southwest wall is a cupboard holding two loaves of bread and several cheese wheels. There are more sacks of foodstuffs to the left and a set of shelves holding several mead barrels. To the left of this is a rack hanging from the wall with a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid, two bunches of [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam") all hanging from it. In the southern corner is the back entrance to the house. There is a small square wooden table in the middle of the room with a common book on top, while against the northeast wall is a cupboard holding an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), a respawning [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") containing leveled items, and a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe"). To the right is a second cupboard holding a bunch of tundra cotton, a [gourd](/wiki/Skyrim:Gourd "Skyrim:Gourd"), three garlic bulbs, a set of fine clothes and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots "Skyrim:Boots"). To the right against the southeast wall is another cupboard. Above these cupboards are three garlic braids hanging from the ceiling.

## Notes

- Bryling's House appears as the [The Antiquarian Circle's headquarters](/wiki/Online:The_Antiquarian_Circle "Online:The Antiquarian Circle") in [ESO](/wiki/Online:Online "Online:Online").
- The [key to the house](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Bryling's House") is carried by Bryling and [Irnskar Ironhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irnskar_Ironhand "Skyrim:Irnskar Ironhand").
- There is a  "Loot") Loot [shadowmark](/wiki/Skyrim:Thieves_Guild_(faction)#Shadowmarks "Skyrim:Thieves Guild (faction)") on the top of the stairs wall.
- With the exception of most barrels, sacks, and other respawning items mentioned above, all containers in the house are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- Some of the items are marked as owned by the MarkarthHagsCureFaction, making them free to take if you help [Bothela](/wiki/Skyrim:Bothela "Skyrim:Bothela"). **?**

# Skyrim:Bryling

## Overview

| Bryling (RefID: 000198BF) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Home City | [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude") | | |

Thane Bryling

**Bryling** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H"), a thane of [Solitude](/wiki/Skyrim:Solitude "Skyrim:Solitude"), and the owner of [Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine"). She has a [house](/wiki/Skyrim:Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Bryling's House") in the city but spends most of her day in the [Blue Palace](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Palace "Skyrim:Blue Palace"). Very rarely, she can be found browsing the marketplace in Solitude. She is evidently having a secret tryst with [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard"), the steward of Solitude.

Bryling wears an upper-class outfit consisting of a [fur-trimmed cloak](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes#Fur-Trimmed_Cloak "Skyrim:Clothes"), [fine armguards](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Armguards "Skyrim:Fine Armguards"), [pleated shoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Pleated_Shoes "Skyrim:Pleated Shoes"), and a [copper and moonstone circlet](/wiki/Skyrim:Copper_and_Moonstone_Circlet "Skyrim:Copper and Moonstone Circlet"). She wields a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger") and carries her house [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Bryling%27s_House "Skyrim:Key to Bryling's House") and a selection of [upper-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

She can be found in the Blue Palace for most of the day, from 8am to 8pm; eating lunch at 1pm and going to sleep at midnight.

## Related Quests

- **[Payment Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Payment_Delivery "Skyrim:Payment Delivery")**: Tell Thane Bryling that the late shipment from [Rockwallow Mine](/wiki/Skyrim:Rockwallow_Mine "Skyrim:Rockwallow Mine") will be arriving soon.

## Dialogue

Bryling may greet you by saying one of the following:

:   *"Thane Bryling, at your service."*

:   *"I can always find time to share a word with a warrior."*

Despite supporting the Empire, she respects the determination of the [Stormcloaks](/wiki/Skyrim:Stormcloaks "Skyrim:Stormcloaks").

:   *"Many condemn the Stormcloaks, but I refuse. There is honor in fighting for what you believe."*

She also comments on the war.

:   *"This godsforsaken war is dividing our people and destroying our land."*

When closing conversation, she may use one of the following lines:

:   *"It's been an honor."*

:   *"I'll get back to court business, then."*

## Quest-Related Events

During the quest [Payment Delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Payment_Delivery "Skyrim:Payment Delivery"), you can tell Bryling that you have a message from [Pactur](/wiki/Skyrim:Pactur "Skyrim:Pactur"). She expresses concern, and upon hearing that they're fine, she thanks you for delivering the message.

:   **Pactur asked me to deliver a message.**
:   *"Is everything all right? I've not heard from [Sorli](/wiki/Skyrim:Sorli_the_Builder "Skyrim:Sorli the Builder") or Pactur in some time."*

    :   **Everything is fine. The shipment will be here soon.**
    :   *"That's good news. I was starting to fear something had happened.
        You have my thanks."*

## Conversations

Bryling can be found having conversations with members of the Court, including [Falk Firebeard](/wiki/Skyrim:Falk_Firebeard "Skyrim:Falk Firebeard").

:   **Bryling:** *"Falk, you shouldn't have come. You know what'd happen if people found out about us."*
:   **Falk:** *"I know, my lady. I just needed to see you outside of court, away from all of the politics."*
:   **Bryling:** *"I'm serious. If [Erikur](/wiki/Skyrim:Erikur "Skyrim:Erikur") knew about us, he'd force you to resign from your position. And without you, he'd have the Jarl bent around his little finger."*
:   **Falk:** *"You're right, of course. But when this war is over, I'll gladly resign and we can stop sneaking around like this."*
:   **Bryling:** *"One more reason to pray for the fighting to end then, my love."*

:   **Bryling:** *"There's something that's been troubling me, Falk. I am hesitant to share it, but I feel that I must."*
:   **Falk:** *"Speak your mind, Bryling. You're among friends here."*
:   **Bryling:** *"You know that I support the Empire, as we all do. However, I fear [General Tullius](/wiki/Skyrim:General_Tullius "Skyrim:General Tullius") is underestimating the Stormcloaks. Too often the general has lost good soldiers because he did not take Ulfric and his men seriously. If this continues, and the worst comes to pass, Solitude will pay the price. The Empire is headquartered here, after all."*
:   **Falk:** *"We don't have the luxury of hanging back to see who wins before choosing our friends, Bryling. You know this. And besides, no Nord with a shred of honor would consider it. We're no cowards. Have faith, Bryling. When this war is over and Ulfric is dead, you'll see that you were jumping at shadows, and nothing more."*

During one of her conversations with Falk, [Sybille Stentor](/wiki/Skyrim:Sybille_Stentor "Skyrim:Sybille Stentor") gets involved:

:   **Falk:** *"It's nearly time to collect taxes on your properties here in the city, Bryling. We'll need to visit each home for an assessment."*
:   **Bryling:** *"Is it that time again already? Very well, let's meet this evening and make the arrangements."*
:   **Sybille:** *"Oh, well done. Very subtle."*
:   **Bryling:** *"I beg your pardon?"*
:   **Sybille:** *"Oh, I'm sorry, did I imply that you'd be meeting for purposes other than court business? You must forgive me."*
:   **Falk:** *"Hold your tongue, Wizard, or you're likely to lose it."*
:   **Sybille:** *"I should very much like to see you try it, my dear steward."*
:   **Bryling:** *"Stop it, both of you. You're acting like children."*

She may also be overheard having some conversations with [Irnskar Ironhand](/wiki/Skyrim:Irnskar_Ironhand "Skyrim:Irnskar Ironhand"):

:   **Bryling:** *"What news have you heard from the war, Irnskar?"*
:   **Irnskar:** *"You won't like it, my lady."*
:   **Bryling:** *"I'm well aware that I won't like it. But it's my duty to keep my people safe. Tell me."*
:   **Irnskar:** *"Possession of the holds change on an almost daily basis, but I can report that Haafingar is still secure. Your people are safe."*
:   **Bryling:** *"I'm not just talking about my subjects. I'm talking about my people: the proud Nords of Skyrim."*
:   **Irnskar:** *"I told you you wouldn't like the news."*

:   **Irnskar:** *"My lady, I'm pleased to inform you that you have a new gown for court, specially tailored by madame [Endarie](/wiki/Skyrim:Endarie "Skyrim:Endarie")."*
:   **Bryling:** *"Really? How did we afford that? Besides, I like the gown I already have."*
:   **Irnskar:** *"Madame Endarie insisted. She made it free of charge, in honor of your lenience about last month's rent discrepancies."*
:   **Bryling:** *"That was suspiciously nice of her. I thought she hated everyone."*
:   **Irnskar:** *"She does, my lady. But apparently, she hates you just a little less than the others."*

## Unused Dialogue

Bryling was also meant to play a role in [Boethiah's Bidding](/wiki/Skyrim:Boethiah%27s_Bidding "Skyrim:Boethiah's Bidding"). Like many of the other palace regulars, she could've helped lead you to jarl Elisif in her chambers if you were on friendly terms with her.

:   **What's wrong with the Jarl?**
:   *"She's telling everyone she's sick. But she's really locked herself in her room because she fears an assassin is out to get her."*

:   :   **Assassins? Really? That's ridiculous. Who would want to kill her?**
    :   *"I know. The poor girl's fright has left her bereft of reason. But there's no talking her out of it. I fear she'll be locked in there for days."*

:   :   :   **Maybe she'd feel safer with a personal bodyguard? I could do that.**
        :   *"I bet she would feel safer. And hopefully you wouldn't have to baby sit her for long. Once she calms down, she might start thinking straight again. Let's go talk with her. Stay close. Talk of assassins has the guards jumpy. They might attack you if you're not standing near me."*

Upon arriving to Elisif's chambers, she would speak to the shaken jarl:

:   **Bryling:** *"Elisif..."*
:   **Elisif:** *"Go. Away. Please!"*
:   **Bryling:** *"I've brought a friend. Someone who can help. A bodyguard. To protect you."*
:   **Elisif:** *"I thought you didn't believe I was in danger!"*
:   **Bryling:** *"It doesn't really matter what I believe, now does it? I've brought you someone who can protect you. That's what you want, isn't it?"*
:   **Elisif:** *"Well, what are you waiting for?!"*

Elisif would then let you enter her chambers, with Bryling returning to her other duties.

Upon quest completion, one of the scenes she has with Falk would get one different line, but there are no other known changes meant for her.

:   **Bryling:** *"Falk, you shouldn't have come. You know what'd happen if people found out about us."*
:   **Falk:** *"I know, my lady. I just needed to see you outside of court, away from all of the politics."*
:   **Bryling:** *"I'm serious. If Erikur knew about us, he'd force you to resign from your position. And without you helping the Jarl, Solitude would be weaker."*
:   **Falk:** *"You're right, of course. But when this war is over, I'll gladly resign and we can stop sneaking around like this."*
:   **Bryling:** *"One more reason to pray for the fighting to end then, my love."*

## Notes

- Bryling is a potential member of the `JobJarlFaction`, yet will never at any point become a jarl. She's also a member of the `Favor252QuestGiverFaction`, which is tied to the quest [Thane of Haafingar](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane_of_Haafingar "Skyrim:Thane of Haafingar"). Since the only other person in this faction is [Jarl Elisif the Fair](/wiki/Skyrim:Elisif_the_Fair "Skyrim:Elisif the Fair"), it can be reasoned that Bryling was once meant to replace Elisif. The thane quest for other holds is also set up to work with both an Imperial-aligned and a Stormcloak-aligned jarl. It's unknown under which circumstances this was meant to happen.
  - The scenes Bryling has with Irnskar, or at the very least the scene concerning the status of the war, seems to have been written with Bryling as jarl in mind, as she explicitly refers to the citizens of Haafingar as "her subjects".
  - The outfit Bryling wears is known as `JarlClothesBryling`, which fits the naming scheme of the outfits of all other initially incumbent jarls. Notably, the only jarl that starts out *without* this distinction is jarl [Idgrod Ravencrone](/wiki/Skyrim:Idgrod_Ravencrone "Skyrim:Idgrod Ravencrone") of [Morthal](/wiki/Skyrim:Morthal "Skyrim:Morthal"). Dialogue attached to Sorli the Builder in the final game was written before Idgrod's, and might have once belonged to Bryling serving as incumbent jarl for Morthal, as both women share the same voice type.
- A scene Bryling has with Irnskar implies that she owns the building in which Radiant Raiment is located, and that the sisters pay her rent. However, a scene that Erikur has with his sister [Gisli](/wiki/Skyrim:Gisli "Skyrim:Gisli") implies that *he* owns the building and the sisters pay *him* rent instead.

## Bugs

- Her secret conversation with Falk Firebeard may occasionally happen right in the Solitude Court, in front of everyone else.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.0, fixes this bug.

# Skyrim:Brynjolf

## Overview

| Brynjolf (RefID: 00020545) ([lore page](/wiki/Lore:Brynjolf "Lore:Brynjolf")) | | | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
