| # of [Alchemy Labs](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs") | 1 |

[Burguk](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Burguk "Skyrim:Chief Burguk")'s Longhouse

**Burguk's Longhouse** is the longhouse of [Chief Burguk](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Burguk "Skyrim:Chief Burguk"), located in the Orc stronghold of [Dushnikh Yal](/wiki/Skyrim:Dushnikh_Yal "Skyrim:Dushnikh Yal").

The longhouse contains two zones: *[Burguk's Longhouse](#Burguk.27s_Longhouse)* and *[Burguk's Longhouse Cellar](#Burguk.27s_Longhouse_Cellar)*.

The quality of the items in the longhouse suggests Dushnik Yal is the most prosperous Orc stronghold in Skyrim.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Chief Burguk](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Burguk "Skyrim:Chief Burguk")[Trainer (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Master)")[One-handed (Master)](/wiki/Skyrim:One-handed "One-handed (Master)")  [Arob](/wiki/Skyrim:Arob "Skyrim:Arob")  [Gharol](/wiki/Skyrim:Gharol "Skyrim:Gharol")[Blacksmith](/wiki/Skyrim:Blacksmith "Blacksmith")[Trainer (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Expert)")[Heavy Armor (Expert)](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Heavy Armor (Expert)")  [Ghorbash the Iron Hand](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorbash_the_Iron_Hand "Skyrim:Ghorbash the Iron Hand")[Follower](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Follower")  [Murbul](/wiki/Skyrim:Murbul "Skyrim:Murbul")[Apothecary](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchants "Apothecary")  [Nagrub](/wiki/Skyrim:Nagrub "Skyrim:Nagrub")  [Shel](/wiki/Skyrim:Shel "Skyrim:Shel") |

### Burguk's Longhouse

The entrance is normally novice-locked, however if you have received [Ghorbash the Iron Hand's](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorbash_the_Iron_Hand "Skyrim:Ghorbash the Iron Hand") [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Burguk%27s_Longhouse "Skyrim:Key to Burguk's Longhouse") to the longhouse, you will be able to enter without it being considered trespassing. Upon entry there is a dresser to your right holding a copy of *[The Code of Malacath](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Code_of_Malacath "Skyrim:The Code of Malacath")*, with a firepit against the west wall opposite the entrance. There is a searchable pot hanging over it. To the right, against the north wall is a sideboard with a [leg of goat](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat "Skyrim:Leg of Goat"), three [leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Leek "Skyrim:Leek"), a [cabbage](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), a [rabbit](/wiki/Skyrim:Rabbit_(dead) "Skyrim:Rabbit (dead)") and an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") on top and a metal pot concealing a random [ingredient](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") underneath. Hanging above the sideboard are two racks holding two rabbits and a [pheasant](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant"). between the sideboard and firepit is a trapdoor to the cellar. To the left of the firepit, still against the west wall is a very long wooden table set with fancy [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Plate "Skyrim:Plate"), [goblet](/wiki/Skyrim:Goblet "Skyrim:Goblet"), a [jug](/wiki/Skyrim:Jug "Skyrim:Jug") and [platter](/wiki/Skyrim:Platter "Skyrim:Platter") along with four portions of [grilled leeks](/wiki/Skyrim:Grilled_Leeks "Skyrim:Grilled Leeks"), two [legs of goat roast](/wiki/Skyrim:Leg_of_Goat_Roast "Skyrim:Leg of Goat Roast"), a [baked potato](/wiki/Skyrim:Baked_Potatoes "Skyrim:Baked Potatoes") and a couple of [goat cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wedge"). In the southwest corner is a square wooden table holding a [flute](/wiki/Skyrim:Flute "Skyrim:Flute"). To the left of the entrance as you enter are a couple of sets of shelves holding a whole range of fancy cookware include [bowls](/wiki/Skyrim:Bowl "Skyrim:Bowl"), plates, goblets, jugs and [candlesticks](/wiki/Skyrim:Candlestick "Skyrim:Candlestick") as well as two [red](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple") and [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple") and two cabbages. There are doorways into bedrooms to the southeast and northeast.

The doorway to the southeast leads to [Chief Burguk's](/wiki/Skyrim:Chief_Burguk "Skyrim:Chief Burguk") bedroom and contains a double bed coming out from the east wall with a weapon plaque over it holding a leveled [battleaxe](/wiki/Skyrim:Battleaxe "Skyrim:Battleaxe"), an end table to the left of the bed, a chair to the right and an unlocked respawning [chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Chest "Skyrim:Chest") containing random items at the foot of the bed. To the left, against the wall is a wooden bench and to the left a dresser with an iron dagger, a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse") and a copy of *[The Bear of Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bear_of_Markarth "Skyrim:The Bear of Markarth")* on top. To the right of the bed is a set of shelves holding a set of [iron armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Armor "Skyrim:Iron Armor"), an [iron helmet](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Helmet "Skyrim:Iron Helmet") and a couple of [ruined books](/wiki/Skyrim:Ruined_Book "Skyrim:Ruined Book"). To the right of the doorway as you enter the bedroom is another dresser, this one holding a pair of leveled gauntlets, a fancy platter, jug and bowl.

The bedroom to the northeast is very cluttered and contains six single beds. In the southwest corner is a set of shelves holding seven common books and a couple of sacks of [foodstuffs](/wiki/Skyrim:Food "Skyrim:Food"), with an end table against the west wall beside it, next along are two of the single beds coming out from the wall, but they have been pushed together, with a dresser holding two more common books on the other side of them. There is another bed coming out from the wall next to the dresser, with an unlocked chest containing leveled items at the foot of the bed and a final bed along the wall, not coming out from it, with a pair of [hide boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Hide_Boots "Skyrim:Hide Boots") beside it. On the other side of the room, starting with a bed along the east wall with an end table with a small coin purse on top at the foot of the bed. Next to this is a bed coming out from the wall with a pair of [leather boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Leather_Boots "Skyrim:Leather Boots") beside it. At the end of the room is a doorway into a tiny bedroom containing a single bed against the northwest wall, a round wooden table at the foot of the bed, right in the northern corner, with two common books and a copy of *[The True Nature of Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:The_True_Nature_of_Orcs "Skyrim:The True Nature of Orcs")* on top and more food sacks on the floor. Opposite the bed against the east wall is a dresser containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes") with a respawning [apothecary's satchel](/wiki/Skyrim:Apothecary%27s_Satchel "Skyrim:Apothecary's Satchel") containing common ingredients, a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina") and a leveled [healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Healing "Skyrim:Healing") potion and a copy of *[Lost Legends](/wiki/Skyrim:Lost_Legends "Skyrim:Lost Legends")* all on top.

### Burguk's Longhouse Cellar

The same key that opens the longhouse also open the trapdoor to the cellar. When entering the cellar you descend the ladder to find a stack of crates and a couple of food barrels beside it. You are on a raised wooden platform with a couple of sets of shelves and cupboards around a round wooden table and two chairs in the middle of the platform. The shelves hold a bottle of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two bottles of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"), an iron dagger and a couple of wheels of cheese. While one of the cupboards hold only clutter, the other holds two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), two bottles of wine and a few [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"). To the right of this one are two more chairs and to the right is a dresser holding a mixture of clothes and [fine clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Fine_Clothes "Skyrim:Fine Clothes") with an iron dagger laying on top.

To the northwest there is a ramp down off the platform to a cave area with a variety of different fungi including [bleeding crown](/wiki/Skyrim:Bleeding_Crown "Skyrim:Bleeding Crown"), [blisterwort](/wiki/Skyrim:Blisterwort "Skyrim:Blisterwort") and [imp stool](/wiki/Skyrim:Imp_Stool "Skyrim:Imp Stool") all growing together next to a rock pillar at the bottom of the ramp, elsewhere in the cellar are [white cap](/wiki/Skyrim:White_Cap "Skyrim:White Cap") and [Namira's rot](/wiki/Skyrim:Namira%27s_Rot "Skyrim:Namira's Rot") fungi. Next to the ramp is a sideboard holding an [iron war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_War_Axe "Skyrim:Iron War Axe"), a leveled sword and copies of two common books and a copy of the [Heavy Armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Heavy_Armor "Skyrim:Heavy Armor") [skill book](/wiki/Skyrim:Skill_Books "Skyrim:Skill Books") *[Orsinium and the Orcs](/wiki/Skyrim:Orsinium_and_the_Orcs "Skyrim:Orsinium and the Orcs")*. There is also an [iron shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Shield "Skyrim:Iron Shield") leaning against the sideboard on the ground. Under the platform is an apprentice-locked respawning chest containing random items and further back there is a cupboard with a leveled healing potion and a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of minor magicka](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Magicka "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Magicka") and potion of minor stamina as well as a leveled helmet and the unique [dragonfly in a jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonfly_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Dragonfly in a Jar"), one of the five [bugs in a jar](/wiki/Skyrim:Miscellaneous_Items#Bugs_in_a_Jar "Skyrim:Miscellaneous Items"). There are a pair of [iron boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Boots "Skyrim:Iron Boots") and an [iron warhammer](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Warhammer "Skyrim:Iron Warhammer") in front and leaning against the cupboard.

There is a path that continues to the north before twisting and turning until you reach another room which contains a few food barrels, one of which has a pile of potatoes on top, a total of six racks hanging from the ceiling in two groups of three, holding two pheasants and four rabbits. Next to a frame for stretching pelts is a medium coin purse on the ground. The path leaves this room to the northwest and takes you to a room with an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Lab "Skyrim:Alchemy Lab") with a potion of minor healing and a potion of minor magicka on top and various ingredients laying on rocks and hanging from the ceiling all around. There is a bunch of [jazbay grapes](/wiki/Skyrim:Jazbay_Grapes "Skyrim:Jazbay Grapes"), a total of seven [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") bulbs and braids, two bowls of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), a total of eight bunches of dried [elves ear](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear"), a bunch of [frost mirriam](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Mirriam "Skyrim:Frost Mirriam"), a sprig of [snowberries](/wiki/Skyrim:Snowberries "Skyrim:Snowberries"), two bunches of [juniper berries](/wiki/Skyrim:Juniper_Berries "Skyrim:Juniper Berries"), a [taproot](/wiki/Skyrim:Taproot "Skyrim:Taproot") and a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"). There is also a respawning apothecary's satchel containing uncommon [ingredients](/wiki/Skyrim:Ingredients "Skyrim:Ingredients") on one of the rocks. The path continues to the west, passing under a naturally lit section before rejoining where you started, opposite the sideboard. The path also has several varieties of fungi growing in them.

## Notes

- The main building [respawns](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") but the cellar does not.
- A permanently disabled copy of [Ghorbash's Ancestral Axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghorbash%27s_Ancestral_Axe "Skyrim:Ghorbash's Ancestral Axe") is placed in the building.
- Other than most barrels, sacks, and containers specified to be respawning above, all containers in the house are [non-respawning](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") and safe to store items in.

## Bugs

- Sometimes the alchemy lab in the longhouse basement is invisible. It still functions like an alchemy lab, it just cannot be seen.

# Skyrim:Butcher

## Overview

This article is about the bandit in Cragslane Cavern. For the Butcher of Windhelm, see [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium").

| [Faction(s)](/wiki/Skyrim:Factions "Skyrim:Factions") | [BanditFaction](/wiki/Skyrim:BanditFaction "Skyrim:BanditFaction") | | |

The Butcher

The **Butcher** is the [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Bandit "Skyrim:Bandit") leader of [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern").

He wears a full set of heavy armor, excluding the helmet, which can be up to [steel plate](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Plate_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Plate Armor") ([Nordic](/wiki/Skyrim:Nordic "Skyrim:Nordic") if the [Dragonborn add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dragonborn "Skyrim:Dragonborn") is installed) in quality. He also carries a shield, which can be up to [ebony](/wiki/Skyrim:Ebony "Skyrim:Ebony") in quality, but doesn't use it unless you disarm him. The Butcher wields a two handed weapon which can be up to ebony quality, and carries a leveled amount of [gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold").

## Related Quests

- **[Supply and Demand](/wiki/Skyrim:Supply_and_Demand "Skyrim:Supply and Demand")**: Clear [Cragslane Cavern](/wiki/Skyrim:Cragslane_Cavern "Skyrim:Cragslane Cavern") for the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of [Riften](/wiki/Skyrim:Riften "Skyrim:Riften").

## Notes

- Before version 1.9 of the [official Skyrim patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch#Version_1.9 "Skyrim:Patch"), the Butcher was simply named 'Bandit'.

# Skyrim:Buy Dwarven artifact

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **Bring your newly-obtained [Dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven "Skyrim:Dwarven") artifact to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth").** | |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") |
| Location(s): | Any [City](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities"), [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth") |
| Reward: | Varying Amount of Gold |
| ID: | WIAddItem07 |

Calcelmo wants to buy a Dwarven item from you.

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Buy a [Dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven "Skyrim:Dwarven") item from a shop in a [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities").
2. Receive the message from a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier").
3. Sell it to [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo").

## Detailed Walkthrough

After purchasing a [Dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven "Skyrim:Dwarven") item of any kind inside a [city](/wiki/Skyrim:Cities "Skyrim:Cities"), a [courier](/wiki/Skyrim:Courier "Skyrim:Courier") may come to you shortly afterward with a [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Calcemo "Skyrim:Letter from Calcemo") from [Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Calcelmo "Skyrim:Calcelmo") in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), saying that he wants to buy the item from you. Reading the letter triggers this quest.

When you take the item to Calcelmo, you can sell it to him for twice the item's base value. If you succeed at a persuade (Speech 50+) or intimidate check, Calcelmo will offer two and a half times the item's base value.

| Option | Dialogue | | | | Reaction |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Sounds fair. Here you go. | Wonderful. You've just made an important contribution to the advancement of a Dwemer scholarship. | | | | Make the deal |
| I think you can do better than that.  **(Persuade)** | **Passed**: Well... I suppose important research is worth every coin. All right. You have yourself a deal. How's double and a half its value in trade? **Failed**: With this the world could have a better understanding of the Dwemer! Come now, where's your sense of propriety? Extorting an old man like this. | | | | **Passed**: Make a decision on the new deal **Failed**: Nothing |
| Not good enough. I'll shake the extra coin out of you if I must.  **(Intimidate)** | **Passed**: Hold on, there. I suppose, in the uh, interest of research... I can spare a few more coins. Double and a half its value. That's all I can muster. **Failed**: Ha! I'll see to it the Jarl hears of your abuse of a court scholar. Shame on you. | | | | **Passed**: Make a decision on the new deal **Failed**: Nothing |
| Not good enough. I'll hold onto this. You'll need to find another one. | Oh... well... I can see you have no appreciation for scholarship. | | | | Cancel the deal |

## Value Ratio

You can use these tables to find out how much gold Calcelmo will pay you for each item:

### Dwarven Armor

| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Dwarven Armor | 400 | 800 | 1000 |
| Dwarven Boots | 85 | 170 | 212 |
| Dwarven Gauntlets | 85 | 170 | 212 |
| Dwarven Helmet | 200 | 400 | 500 |
| Dwarven Shield | 225 | 450 | 562 |

| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Dwarven Arrow | 4 | 8 | 10 |
| Dwarven Battleaxe | 300 | 600 | 750 |
| Dwarven Bolt[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | 3 | 6 | 7 |
| Dwarven Bow | 270 | 540 | 675 |
| Dwarven Crossbow[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | 350 | 700 | 875 |
| Dwarven Dagger | 55 | 110 | 137 |
| Dwarven Greatsword | 270 | 540 | 675 |

| Dwarven Sword | 135 | 270 | 337 |

| Dwarven Warhammer | 325 | 650 | 812 |
| Enhanced Dwarven Crossbow[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | 550 | 1100 | 1375 |
| Exploding Dwarven Bolt of Fire[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | 15 | 30 | 37 |

| Exploding Dwarven Bolt of Shock[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard") | 15 | 30 | 37 |

## Notes

- Enchanted and non-enchanted Dwarven apparel and weapons (including arrows/bolts) can trigger this quest.
- You can keep the item and complete the quest by agreeing to sell, immediately exiting dialogue, and then dropping your item before it is removed.
  - Be mindful of your positioning if using this trick, as it's possible for the item in question to be tossed into the flowing water below and end up out of reach.
- If the item is dropped, sold, tempered, or enchanted the quest cannot be completed unless you find another, identical item (as stated in his message).
- This quest may be triggered multiple times.
- Calcelmo may ask for the same item more than once.
- If you have two of the requested item and want to keep a specific one, trade the one you want to your follower then finish the quest as Calcelmo might end up taking the one you want to keep.
- As the price Calcelmo offers is calculated from the **base value** of the item (e.g., [Dwarven gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Dwarven Gauntlets") have a base value of 85 septims), selling an enchanted item through this quest can be a horribly bad deal.
- With the addition of [Dawnguard add-on](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), Calcelmo may ask for Dwarven Crossbows, Enhanced Dwarven Crossbows, and Dwarven Bolts, including any of the three explosive bolts discovered during the [Ancient Technology](/wiki/Skyrim:Ancient_Technology "Skyrim:Ancient Technology") radiant quests.
- It doesn't matter where you buy it (be it [Volkihar Castle](/wiki/Skyrim:Castle_Volkihar "Skyrim:Castle Volkihar") or [the Riverwood Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader")) or from which merchant (even the [Dremora Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Dremora_Merchant "Skyrim:Dremora Merchant") via the [Black Market](/wiki/Skyrim:Black_Market "Skyrim:Black Market") power), you can still get the letter via courier to start the quest.
- If the requested item you bought is enchanted, it is strongly recommended that you don't disenchant it at an [Arcane Enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter"), or you may need to tell Calcelmo you lost it.
- If the requested item was bought from a [military camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Military_Camps "Skyrim:Military Camps"), the note will say "military camp", rather than the camp's actual name. For example, [Reach Stormcloak Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Reach_Stormcloak_Camp "Skyrim:Reach Stormcloak Camp") and [Winterhold Imperial Camp](/wiki/Skyrim:Winterhold_Imperial_Camp "Skyrim:Winterhold Imperial Camp") will simply be recognized as "Stormcloak military camp" and "Imperial military camp", respectively.
- Crafting, enchanting, looting, and stealing Dwarven weapons and armor doesn't initiate the quest; they must be purchased from a valid merchant. However, if one you made, enchanted, looted, or stole is sold to a merchant and purchased back, then that may be taken into account.
- You may or may not get his letter after you buy a Dwarven item from a blacksmith or merchant. If you want to keep the item and not start the quest (as it will remain stuck in your quest log until you finally sell the item to him), don't read the letter he sends to you and drop it or put it into a container (one belonging to you or even something in the depths of a dungeon). He'll still have the dialogue option to sell (as if you'd read the note, even though you didn't), but as long as you don't pick it, you can avoid starting the quest and keep what you paid for.

## Bugs

- Calcelmo may not acknowledge that an item is in your inventory.
  - Removing the item and getting it back again, such as dropping it and picking it up or trading it to a follower temporarily, may fix this. You may have to be in third-person view or the item could disappear when you drop it.
  - If you have sold/lost the item, you can add it to your inventory through the console commands and it may be accepted by Calcelmo.
  - If you have sold/lost the item, a forged/enchanted replacement may not be accepted by Calcelmo.
- Items that have been marked for the quest, but the courier has not delivered the note regarding, can be enchanted but cannot be named. **?**
- The item Calcelmo requests may not be removed from your inventory when you are rewarded.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, fixes this bug.
- The [Execution Hood](/wiki/Skyrim:Execution_Hood "Skyrim:Execution Hood") from [With Friends Like These...](/wiki/Skyrim:With_Friends_Like_These... "Skyrim:With Friends Like These...") is counted as a Dwarven artifact for this quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.1, fixes this bug.
- It is possible to sell an item to Calcelmo without having been given the note from the courier. This would then result in the courier attempting to make a delivery for the quest even though it was already complete.
  - The [Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Special_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Special Edition Patch"), version 4.0.8, fixes this bug.
- Unique items like the [Dwarven Black Bow of Fate](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Black_Bow_of_Fate "Skyrim:Dwarven Black Bow of Fate") can be targeted by this quest. If you're not willing to part with the item, your only choices are to drop the item, as detailed in Notes, or leave the quest active. **?**
- You can escape the dialogue right after Persuade/Intimidate speech check before advancing quest stage. Therefore it can be repeated for leveling Speech up.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

## Quest Stages

| Buy Dwarven artifact (WIAddItem07) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | *Objective 10:* Bring a <Alias=Item> to Calcelmo |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 0, 100, 200, 255.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage WIAddItem07 stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest WIAddItem07`.

# Skyrim:Buyer Beware

## Overview

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| [SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png](/wiki/File:SR-qico-Miscellaneous.png) | **Ambush a meeting to retrieve the [Mask of Vivec](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Vivec "Skyrim:Mask of Vivec").** |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Quest Giver: | [Matriarch Drevlan](/wiki/Skyrim:Matriarch_Drevlan "Skyrim:Matriarch Drevlan") |
| Location(s): | [Ashfall's Tear](/wiki/Skyrim:Ashfall%27s_Tear "Skyrim:Ashfall's Tear"), [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock"), [Old Attius Farm Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm_Cellar "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm Cellar") |

Buyer Beware

## Quick Walkthrough

1. Read *[Masks of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Masks_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Masks of the Tribunal")*.
2. Shoot down the bird outside the Bulwark's south gate.
3. Read the [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_on_the_Target "Skyrim:Note on the Target").
4. Follow the Redoran Guard to Old Attius Farm Cellar.
5. Kill the guard and the [Buyer](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer "Skyrim:Buyer").
6. Retrieve the Mask of Vivec.

## Detailed Walkthrough

The Felsaad Tern

After reading *[Masks of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Masks_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Masks of the Tribunal")*, you will need to travel to Raven Rock, and head up the stairs near the front of the Temple to the top of the Bulwark. Face south towards [Old Attius Farm](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm") to see a lone [Felsaad Tern](/wiki/Skyrim:Felsaad_Tern "Skyrim:Felsaad Tern") circling close by. As long as it's not too close to midnight (any time up to 11) this bird will appear and continuously circle around. If it's knocked out of the sky an objective prompt to "retrieve the note" will appear. Find the bird's body and loot it to find a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Note_on_the_Target "Skyrim:Note on the Target").

Locate the Redoran Guard marked with a quest objective. Follow him south to the Old Attius Farm site, and from there down through the trapdoor into the [Old Attius Farm Cellar](/wiki/Skyrim:Old_Attius_Farm_Cellar "Skyrim:Old Attius Farm Cellar"). Kill the guard and the [Buyer](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer "Skyrim:Buyer"), and retrieve the [Mask of Vivec](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Vivec "Skyrim:Mask of Vivec") and a Fahlbtharz Forge Gem. Optionally loot the Redoran Guard for a [note](/wiki/Skyrim:Redoran_Guard%27s_Note "Skyrim:Redoran Guard's Note") describing his motivations.

Finishing this quest completes one of the three tasks of the goddess in the [Ghosts of the Tribunal](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal_(quest) "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal (quest)") quest. It also provides one of the four forge gems required to complete the [Trueflame](/wiki/Skyrim:Trueflame_(quest) "Skyrim:Trueflame (quest)") quest.

## Notes

- The Redoran Guard needn't be followed or watched. Just head over near the Old Attius Farm Cellar trap door and wait past midnight, during 12AM~4AM. It'll be unlocked and the Buyer will be down there with the guard. They'll attack on sight so kill them.

## Quest Stages

| Buyer Beware (ccASVSSE001\_QuestA) | | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Stage | Finishes Quest | Journal Entry |
| 10 |  | I've discovered a temple near Raven Rock where worshipers of Almalexia gather. It seems the temple Matriarch is searching for the lost Masks of Vivec and Sotha Sil. *Objective 11:* Read Masks of the Tribunal |
| 40 |  | I've discovered a temple near Raven Rock where worshipers of Almalexia gather. It seems the temple Matriarch is searching for the lost Masks of Vivec and Sotha Sil. Rumor has it that the Mask of Vivec is being transported back to Morrowind, but an enterprising guard is looking to sell to another buyer. I should watch the Bulwark for any guards leaving their post near midnight. *Objective 21:* Shoot down the bird outside the Bulwark's south gate  *Objective 30:* Retrieve the note  *Objective 40:* Read the Note on the Target  *Objective 50:* Track the Redoran Guard's movements after midnight |
| 50 |  | I've discovered a temple near Raven Rock where worshipers of Almalexia gather. It seems the temple Matriarch is searching for the lost Masks of Vivec and Sotha Sil. Rumor has it that the Mask of Vivec is being transported back to Morrowind, but an enterprising guard is looking to sell to another buyer. I followed a guard to a secret cellar where he intends to make the sale. *Objective 60:* Look for clues in the cellar |
| 60 |  | I've discovered a temple near Raven Rock where worshipers of Almalexia gather. It seems the temple Matriarch is searching for the lost Masks of Vivec and Sotha Sil. Rumor has it that the Mask of Vivec is being transported back to Morrowind, but an enterprising guard is looking to sell to another buyer. I followed the guard to a secret cellar where he intends to make the sale. *Objective 70:* Kill the Buyer |
| 70 |  | I've discovered a temple near Raven Rock where worshipers of Almalexia gather. It seems the temple Matriarch is searching for the lost Masks of Vivec and Sotha Sil. Rumor has it that the Mask of Vivec is being transported back to Morrowind, but an enterprising guard is looking to sell to another buyer. I followed the guard to a secret cellar where he planned to make the sale, and killed the buyer. *Objective 70:* Retrieve the Mask of Vivec |
| 1000 | ☑ | I've discovered a temple near Raven Rock where worshipers of Almalexia gather. It seems the temple Matriarch is searching for the lost Masks of Vivec and Sotha Sil. Rumor has it that the Mask of Vivec is being transported back to Morrowind, but an enterprising guard is looking to sell to another buyer. I followed the guard to a secret cellar where he planned to make the sale, killed the buyer, and picked up the Mask of Vivec. |

- The following empty quest stages were omitted from the table: 1, 2, 20, 30, 35, 80, 2000, 3000.

Notes

- Any text displayed in angle brackets (e.g., `<Alias=LocationHold>`) is dynamically set by the Radiant Quest system, and will be filled in with the appropriate word(s) when seen in game.
- Not all Journal Entries may appear in your journal; which entries appear and which entries do not depends on the manner in which the quest is done.
- Stages are not always in order of progress. This is usually the case with quests that have multiple possible outcomes or quests where certain tasks may be done in any order. Some stages may therefore repeat objectives seen in other stages.
- If an entry is marked as "Finishes Quest" it means the quest disappears from the Active Quest list, but you may still receive new entries for that quest.
- On the PC, it is possible to use the [console](/wiki/Skyrim:Console "Skyrim:Console") to advance through the quest by entering `setstage ccASVSSE001_QuestA stage`, where `stage` is the number of the stage you wish to complete. It is not possible to un-complete (i.e. go back) quest stages, but it is possible to clear all stages of the quest using `resetquest ccASVSSE001_QuestA`.

The **Buyer** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") who is encountered during [Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware"). He must be killed to complete the quest.

## Related Quests

- **[Buyer Beware](/wiki/Skyrim:Buyer_Beware "Skyrim:Buyer Beware")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Ghosts_of_the_Tribunal "Skyrim:Ghosts of the Tribunal"): Ambush a meeting to retrieve the [Mask of Vivec](/wiki/Skyrim:Mask_of_Vivec "Skyrim:Mask of Vivec").

# Skyrim:Caerellius House

## Overview

|  |
| --- |
| **This article is being developed as part of the Skyrim Houses Redesign Project. If you see this tag it means the article can still be improved. Please see the [project page](/wiki/UESPWiki:SHRP "UESPWiki:SHRP") for guidelines.** |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Caerellius House ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=solstheim&centeron=Caerellius+House)) | | |
| # of Zones | 1 |
| [Respawn Time](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawn "Skyrim:Respawn") | 10 days |
| Console Location Code(s) | |
| DLC2RRCresciusHouse | |
| Region | |
| [Solstheim](/wiki/Skyrim:Solstheim "Skyrim:Solstheim") | |
| Location | |
| [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock") | |
| Special Features | |
| # of [Cooking Pots/Spits](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking "Skyrim:Cooking") | 1 |

Caerellius House

**Caerellius House** is the home of [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius") and [Aphia Velothi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aphia_Velothi "Skyrim:Aphia Velothi") in [Raven Rock](/wiki/Skyrim:Raven_Rock "Skyrim:Raven Rock").

It is on the waterfront between [the Bulwark](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bulwark "Skyrim:The Bulwark") to the southeast and [Morvayn Manor](/wiki/Skyrim:Morvayn_Manor "Skyrim:Morvayn Manor") to the northwest, opposite the entrance to the [Ulen Ancestral Tomb](/wiki/Skyrim:Ulen_Ancestral_Tomb "Skyrim:Ulen Ancestral Tomb").

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Aphia Velothi](/wiki/Skyrim:Aphia_Velothi "Skyrim:Aphia Velothi") [Trainer (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Trainers "Trainer (Common)")[Restoration (Common)](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Restoration (Common)")  [Crescius Caerellius](/wiki/Skyrim:Crescius_Caerellius "Skyrim:Crescius Caerellius") |

## Related Quests

- **[Pain in the Necklace](/wiki/Skyrim:Pain_in_the_Necklace "Skyrim:Pain in the Necklace")**: Find [East Empire pendants](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Pendant "Skyrim:East Empire Pendant") for [Fethis Alor](/wiki/Skyrim:Fethis_Alor "Skyrim:Fethis Alor").

### Exterior

To the left of the entrance are three unusable barrels and an empty cart. To the right of the entrance are three crates, four unusable barrels, and three [scathecraw](/wiki/Skyrim:Scathecraw "Skyrim:Scathecraw") plants. Along the back of the building on the waterfront is an ash yam urn among more crates. The entrance has an apprentice-level lock.

### Caerellius House

The entrance leads into a cooking and living area on the lower floor of the house. Along the south wall is a table holding four [carrots](/wiki/Skyrim:Carrot "Skyrim:Carrot"), three [potatoes](/wiki/Skyrim:Potato "Skyrim:Potato"), four [red apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple"), two [green apples](/wiki/Skyrim:Green_Apple "Skyrim:Green Apple"), three bottles of [wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Wine "Skyrim:Wine"), two [cabbages](/wiki/Skyrim:Cabbage "Skyrim:Cabbage"), two [goat cheese wheels](/wiki/Skyrim:Goat_Cheese_Wheel "Skyrim:Goat Cheese Wheel"), two [eidar cheese wedges](/wiki/Skyrim:Eidar_Cheese_Wedge "Skyrim:Eidar Cheese Wedge"), and a [sliced eidar cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Sliced_Eidar_Cheese "Skyrim:Sliced Eidar Cheese"), with copies of *[History of Raven Rock, Vol. I](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock,_Vol._I "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock, Vol. I")*, *[Vol. II](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock,_Vol._II "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock, Vol. II")*, and *[Vol. III](/wiki/Skyrim:History_of_Raven_Rock,_Vol._III "Skyrim:History of Raven Rock, Vol. III")* on the wall ledge behind the table. In the southwest corner is a chair and two meat barrels, one of which has a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead") on top. Along the west wall are three [pheasants](/wiki/Skyrim:Pheasant "Skyrim:Pheasant") hanging from a rack, a chair, four bottles of Nord mead on the wall ledge, three [elves ears](/wiki/Skyrim:Elves_Ear "Skyrim:Elves Ear") and a [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braid hanging from the ceiling, and a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand over a fire. In the northwest corner is an [East Empire Company strongbox](/wiki/Skyrim:East_Empire_Company_Strongbox "Skyrim:East Empire Company Strongbox") on the wall ledge. Along the north wall is a copy of *[The Reclamations](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Reclamations "Skyrim:The Reclamations")* on the wall ledge and a doorway to the next room. In the northeast corner is a meat barrel and copies of *[Confessions of a Dunmer Skooma Eater](/wiki/Skyrim:Confessions_of_a_Dunmer_Skooma_Eater "Skyrim:Confessions of a Dunmer Skooma Eater")* and *[The House of Troubles](/wiki/Skyrim:The_House_of_Troubles "Skyrim:The House of Troubles")* on the wall ledge.

The next room is circular, and features the stairs leading up to the upper floor. Along the curved west wall are three sacks, two meat barrels, and a set of shelves holding a [boiled creme treat](/wiki/Skyrim:Boiled_Creme_Treat "Skyrim:Boiled Creme Treat"), three loaves of [bread](/wiki/Skyrim:Bread "Skyrim:Bread"), four bottles of Nord mead, two bottles of wine, two bottles of [alto wine](/wiki/Skyrim:Alto_Wine "Skyrim:Alto Wine"), a sample of [Felsaad tern feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Felsaad_Tern_Feathers "Skyrim:Felsaad Tern Feathers"), and a cast iron pot containing three red apples. Along the north wall beneath the stairs are two chairs and a small round table holding two loaves of bread, and a wood pile.

The small circular room on the upper floor is the sleeping area. To the northwest at the top of the stairs is a sack and an end table holding two filled [lesser soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), a large and a medium [coin purse](/wiki/Skyrim:Coin_Purse "Skyrim:Coin Purse"), and three loose [coins](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold"). To the southwest is an owned double bed. To the southeast is a chest, a sack, and a set of shelves holding a [potion of minor healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Healing"), a [potion of healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Healing "Skyrim:Potion of Healing"), and copies of *[Dunmer of Skyrim](/wiki/Skyrim:Dunmer_of_Skyrim "Skyrim:Dunmer of Skyrim")*, *[Pirate King of the Abecean](/wiki/Skyrim:Pirate_King_of_the_Abecean "Skyrim:Pirate King of the Abecean")*, and *[The True Noble's Code](/wiki/Skyrim:The_True_Noble%27s_Code "Skyrim:The True Noble's Code")*.

## Bugs

- Several buildings in Raven Rock, including the Caerellius house, were incorrectly assigned the [music](/wiki/Skyrim:Music "Skyrim:Music") heard in [Apocrypha](/wiki/Skyrim:Apocrypha "Skyrim:Apocrypha") rather than the default Solstheim music heard in other houses.
  -  The [Unofficial Dragonborn Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Dragonborn_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Dragonborn Patch"), version 1.0.2, fixes this bug. ([details](https://afktrack.afkmods.com/index.php?a=issues&i=12062))

# Skyrim:Cairine

## Overview

Cairine

**Cairine** is a [Breton](/wiki/Skyrim:Breton "Skyrim:Breton") [citizen](/wiki/Skyrim:Citizen_(class) "Skyrim:Citizen (class)") living in [The Warrens](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Warrens "Skyrim:The Warrens"), the hub for all the poor and sick of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). She used to work at the [Smelter](/wiki/Skyrim:Smelter "Skyrim:Smelter") in Markarth, but is now too sick to do so. Instead, she spends her whole day sitting on the ground of the Warrens holding her stomach in pain.

She wears a set of [ragged robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Robes "Skyrim:Ragged Robes") and a matching pair of [ragged boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Ragged_Boots "Skyrim:Ragged Boots"). She only carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

## Related Quests

- **[New Allegiances](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Allegiances "Skyrim:New Allegiances")**[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"): Turn the target into a [vampire](/wiki/Skyrim:Vampire "Skyrim:Vampire"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))

## Dialogue

When approached she can say:

:   *"You don't want to be here. No one wants to."*
:   *"Don't know anyone here doesn't have [Rattles](/wiki/Skyrim:Rattles "Skyrim:Rattles") or [Ataxia](/wiki/Skyrim:Ataxia "Skyrim:Ataxia")."*

### New Allegiances

If you are part of the [Volkihar vampires](/wiki/Skyrim:Volkihar_Vampire_Clan "Skyrim:Volkihar Vampire Clan")[DG](/wiki/Skyrim:Dawnguard "Skyrim:Dawnguard"), you will eventually get [tasked](/wiki/Skyrim:New_Allegiances "Skyrim:New Allegiances") by [Vingalmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Vingalmo "Skyrim:Vingalmo") to turn a citizen into a vampire. Cairine is one of these possible victims. He will describe her as:

:   *"A pathetic creature in her present condition, but the gift will embolden her. And her lowly state suits her to being our eyes and ears in Markarth."*

You can transform her:

:   *"Something's happened, I can't quite remember... I don't feel... right... I'm going to lay down... for awhile..."*

Once you have turned her, she will be very grateful and greet you with:

:   *"Great gift of blood you've given me. Blood that boils in my veins. Gives me strength. You can use my coffin whenever you like."*
:   *"Blood of the sick. Blood of the weak. Blood of the unsuspecting noble lord. Savor each flavor. Unsuspecting, delicious prey."*
:   *"I keep an eye on their comings and goings. No one suspects poor Cairine. Poor, poor Cairine. Ha!"*
:   *"The darkness hums and we sing its praises. Sweet melodies. Sweet like the water that flows through their veins."*

## Rumors

Smelter worker [Omluag](/wiki/Skyrim:Omluag "Skyrim:Omluag") will mention her when asked who works alongside him:

:   *"A few people in the Warrens used to work here. [Degaine](/wiki/Skyrim:Degaine "Skyrim:Degaine") broke some bones a while back. [Eltrys](/wiki/Skyrim:Eltrys "Skyrim:Eltrys") quit. Cairine is too sick."*

## Notes

- Despite what Cairine says, no one in the Warrens has Rattles or Ataxia. These diseases are only present on wild animals in *Skyrim*, unlike *[Oblivion](/wiki/Oblivion:Oblivion "Oblivion:Oblivion")*, where beggars also carried such diseases.
- Cairine herself does not have any kind of disease you can catch either. Her behavior is caused by her AI package `MarkarthCairineWarrenIdlePackage` which is linked to a marker, resulting in her sitting on the ground with the "wounded" animation. She does this around the clock because her package has no set duration, despite the fact she has other packages set up in her schedule, which all get overridden.

## Bugs

- When "killed" for the first time, Cairine will lie still on the floor, yet she is still able to blink, detect you and engage in conversation.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- You might not be able to turn Cairine into a vampire, due to her never standing and her sitting animation preventing you from feeding on her. **?**
  -  If you select her in the console and type `moveto player`, she will be standing and you can proceed normally.

Calcelmo

**Calcelmo**, Scholar of [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"), is a [High Elf](/wiki/Skyrim:High_Elf "Skyrim:High Elf") [conjurer](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer "Skyrim:CombatMageConjurer") of great renown who dedicates himself to researching the [Dwemer](/wiki/Lore:Dwemer "Lore:Dwemer"). He and his nephew [Aicantar](/wiki/Skyrim:Aicantar "Skyrim:Aicantar") study the [Dwemer ruins beneath Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel"). He is the author of the series of books known simply as *[Dwarves](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarves_(book) "Skyrim:Dwarves (book)")*. His next expected work is a book on the translation of the [Falmer](/wiki/Skyrim:Falmer "Skyrim:Falmer") language which is tentatively titled *Calcelmo's Guide to the Falmer Tongue*. For other historical information, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Calcelmo_of_Markarth "Lore:Calcelmo of Markarth").

He is the [court mage](/wiki/Skyrim:Court_Wizard "Skyrim:Court Wizard") of the [Jarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Jarl "Skyrim:Jarl") of Markarth, and he and Aicantar oversee the excavation of the ruins beneath [Understone Keep](/wiki/Skyrim:Understone_Keep "Skyrim:Understone Keep"). To find him at his workplace, enter the keep and turn left (south), and proceed a short distance through the "tunnel" (as others in the keep refer to the area) until you come to a short flight of steps. Turn and look west. His area is near an [arcane enchanter](/wiki/Skyrim:Arcane_Enchanter "Skyrim:Arcane Enchanter") and an [alchemy lab](/wiki/Skyrim:Alchemy_Labs "Skyrim:Alchemy Labs").

There are a number of pieces of scrap metal around his workshop that respawn periodically that yield a total of 21 [Dwarven metal ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Metal_Ingot "Skyrim:Dwarven Metal Ingot") when smelted. They are flagged as owned by Calcelmo, so taking them is considering stealing until you increase his disposition towards you.

Calcelmo wears [blue mage robes](/wiki/Skyrim:Blue_Mage_Robes "Skyrim:Blue Mage Robes") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0006b46c "Skyrim:Clothing"). He carries an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), a [key to Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Key to Nchuand-Zel"), a [Dwemer Museum key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum_Key "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum Key"), and a selection of [common loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). Being a wizard, he knows a large amount of spells. From the school of [Alteration](/wiki/Skyrim:Alteration "Skyrim:Alteration"), he knows [Oakflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Oakflesh "Skyrim:Oakflesh") and [Stoneflesh](/wiki/Skyrim:Stoneflesh "Skyrim:Stoneflesh"). From the school of [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration"), he knows [Conjure Flame Atronach](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjure_Flame_Atronach "Skyrim:Conjure Flame Atronach"), [Raise Zombie](/wiki/Skyrim:Raise_Zombie "Skyrim:Raise Zombie"), and [Reanimate Corpse](/wiki/Skyrim:Reanimate_Corpse "Skyrim:Reanimate Corpse"). From the school of [Destruction](/wiki/Skyrim:Destruction "Skyrim:Destruction"), he knows [Chain Lightning](/wiki/Skyrim:Chain_Lightning "Skyrim:Chain Lightning"), [Fireball](/wiki/Skyrim:Fireball "Skyrim:Fireball"), [Firebolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Firebolt "Skyrim:Firebolt"), [Lightning Bolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Lightning_Bolt "Skyrim:Lightning Bolt"), [Incinerate](/wiki/Skyrim:Incinerate "Skyrim:Incinerate"), and [Thunderbolt](/wiki/Skyrim:Thunderbolt "Skyrim:Thunderbolt"). Lastly, from the school of [Restoration](/wiki/Skyrim:Restoration "Skyrim:Restoration"), he knows [Close Wounds](/wiki/Skyrim:Close_Wounds "Skyrim:Close Wounds"), [Fast Healing](/wiki/Skyrim:Fast_Healing "Skyrim:Fast Healing"), and [Steadfast Ward](/wiki/Skyrim:Steadfast_Ward "Skyrim:Steadfast Ward").

Being a very dedicated wizard, he devotes all his time to study, never stopping to eat or sleep. The only exception to this routine is after you set him up with [Faleen](/wiki/Skyrim:Faleen "Skyrim:Faleen") (see [this section](#The_Book_of_Love)); he'll then eat with her between 6am and 8am, and 8pm and 10pm.

## Related Quests

- **[The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love")**: Help the [Temple of Mara](/wiki/Skyrim:Temple_of_Mara "Skyrim:Temple of Mara") spread the cause of love throughout Skyrim.
- **[Buy Dwarven artifact](/wiki/Skyrim:Buy_Dwarven_artifact "Skyrim:Buy Dwarven artifact")**: Bring your newly-obtained [Dwarven](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven "Skyrim:Dwarven") artifact to Calcelmo in [Markarth](/wiki/Skyrim:Markarth "Skyrim:Markarth"). ([radiant](/wiki/Skyrim:Radiant "Skyrim:Radiant"))
- **[Delivery to Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_to_Calcelmo "Skyrim:Delivery to Calcelmo")**: Deliver a ring to Calcelmo.
- **[Hard Answers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hard_Answers "Skyrim:Hard Answers")**: Help translate [Gallus's journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal").
- **[The Lost Expedition](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Lost_Expedition "Skyrim:The Lost Expedition")**: Recover the journals from the expedition in [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").
- **[My Pet Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:My_Pet_Mudcrab "Skyrim:My Pet Mudcrab")**[CC](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab"): Buy a [Dwarven Mudcrab](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarven_Armored_Mudcrab_(creature) "Skyrim:Dwarven Armored Mudcrab (creature)").
- **[Nimhe, the Poisoned One](/wiki/Skyrim:Nimhe,_the_Poisoned_One "Skyrim:Nimhe, the Poisoned One")**: Kill the giant frostbite spider blocking access to [Nchuand-Zel](/wiki/Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Nchuand-Zel").

## Dialogue

When first approached, he'll say:

:   *"What are you doing here? The excavation site is closed. I don't need any more workers or guards."*

You'll now have three options:

| Your Dialogue | Calcelmo's Reply | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Excavation site?** | *"Nchuand-Zel? The ruins underneath Markarth? The wealth of artifacts that I've based two human lifetimes of research on?"* |
| **Are you a wizard? I wanted to buy some spells.** | *"Magic. That's what they always want. Never history. Never the secrets of the lost races. No, just little spells and enchantments."* |
| **I was looking for you, actually.** | *"I told you I'm not hiring any more guards. Why do you people always bother me when I'm trying to finish my research?"* |

Either way, he'll then say:

:   *"You idiot. Do you even know who I am? The most recognized scholar on the Dwemer in all of Tamriel, and you people keep bothering me! I... I'm sorry I... I got too excited. I'm in the middle of some very... stressful work, and I shouldn't have yelled. How can I help you?"*

:   **Why do you need guards?**
:   *"To protect my research, for one. There are more cutthroat scholars out there who would steal my findings if they got the chance. And the excavations into Nchuand-Zel are dangerous. Dwemer machines and traps still function even after thousands of years."*

:   **You're researching the Dwemer?**
:   *"Yes. Their history and culture is all around us in Markarth. A race of stonecutters, artisans, and engineers. They invented machines and built elaborate underground cities where they researched powers to rival the gods themselves. And then, at a time we are still not sure when, they disappeared. The whole people, all at once. Leaving behind only their works."*

His normal greetings:

:   *"I have things to study, what is it?"*
:   *"The artifacts I've discovered in Nchuand-Zel will make history one day."*
:   *"I've only ever lost a few guards to Steam Centurions. Good odds, considering..."*
:   *"I used to travel so much before all this [Forsworn](/wiki/Skyrim:Forsworn "Skyrim:Forsworn") nonsense. Such an inconvenience..."*
:   *"Ah yes, my matchmaker. What is it I can do for you?"*

When exiting conversation, he'll say:

:   *"What? Oh, goodbye."*
:   *"Yes, yes. I have a lot of research to do."*

## Conversations

He can often be seen having the following conversations with Aicantar:

**Calcelmo**: *"Next season, nephew. Next season for sure...."*
**Aicantar**: *"'Next season for sure...' What? Uncle Calcelmo, I don't understand what you mean."*
**Calcelmo**: *"The excavation, Aicantar! Right after I finish my book. We'll start excavating Nchuand-Zel again."*
**Aicantar**: *"Could I maybe, skip the excavation, Uncle Calcelmo? I, uh, I just think you won't need me."*
**Calcelmo**: *"Nonsense, you're a vital part of my research team. You'll be there, have no fear! Now, I don't want to hear another word of protest."*

**Aicantar**: *"Uncle Calcelmo...."*
**Calcelmo**: *"What is it nephew? Can't you see I'm trying to think here?"*
**Aicantar**: *"I just wanted to know if you needed anything."*
**Calcelmo**: *"Um, no. Nothing. Nothing at all."*
**Aicantar**: *"Are you sure?"*
**Calcelmo**: *"Stop bothering me Aicanter*[[sic](/wiki/UESPWiki:Spelling#Books_and_Direct_Quotes "UESPWiki:Spelling")]*!"*

### Nimhe, the Poisoned One

If you try to enter the [Dwemer Museum](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum"), a guard will stop you and point you to Calcelmo for entrance. When you approach Calcelmo telling him you heard he owns the Dwemer Museum, he'll say:

:   *"Correct. It's a private place where I can catalog my research. Occasionally, the Jarl will come in and have questions, but that's thankfully rare."*
:   **I'd like to see the excavation site.**
:   *"Persistent aren't you? Oh, very well. Who am I to stand in the way of curiosity? I'll let you in if you agree to something for me. There's a giant spider in Nchuand-Zel. My workers call her 'Nimhe,' the poisoned one. If you deal with Nimhe, I'll let you into both the excavation site and my Dwemer Museum. What do you say?"*

:   :   **That spider is as good as dead.**
    :   *"Enthusiasm. Good. Here's the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Nchuand-Zel "Skyrim:Key to Nchuand-Zel") to the dig site."*

:   :   **Not interested.**
    :   *"Oh, very well. Probably safest that way."*

When you return after having killed Nimhe:

:   **I've killed Nimhe.**
:   *"You have my gratitude. That spider had been interfering with my excavations for months. As promised, here's the [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Museum_Key "Skyrim:Dwemer Museum Key") to the Dwemer Museum. Mind the displays. Some of them are quite fragile."*

### Delivery to Calcelmo

If you bring him a [delivery](/wiki/Skyrim:Delivery_to_Calcelmo "Skyrim:Delivery to Calcelmo") from [Kerah](/wiki/Skyrim:Kerah "Skyrim:Kerah"):

:   **I have a delivery from Kerah.**
:   *"Oh, that's right. I keep forgetting to pick that up. Poor Kerah, such a patient woman. Now, you're supposed to get something for your trouble, aren't you? How about some gold? People seem to like that, I notice."*

### The Book of Love

During the quest, [Dinya Balu](/wiki/Skyrim:Dinya_Balu "Skyrim:Dinya Balu") will send you to help Calcelmo. When you approach him:

:   **I've been sent by Mara to aid you.**
:   *"I was beginning to lose faith that any help would come. Eh... You see... I've been thinking about Faleen quite a bit. You know Faleen?"*

:   :   **Yes, I do.**
    :   *"Then you know what a beauty she is."*

:   :   **I'm sorry, I don't know her.**
    :   *"Well, suffice to say she is resplendent, but not without resolve. Striking, in all senses."*

Either way, he'll then continue:

:   *"The trouble is that I can't seem to speak around her. My mouth goes dry, and I start to shake. I could never hope to approach her."*

:   :   **You just need to have something to talk about.**
    :   *"That's the trouble. I know Faleen from the Keep, but I have no idea what sorts of things she likes. It's not a simple matter. I could offend her fairly easily by bringing up the wrong subject. I've seen it happen before."*

:   :   **You're probably overthinking this.**
    :   *"That may be the case. But she is as volatile as a sabre cat. One wrong word, and I've seen her turn on a man so quickly..."*

Either leads to:

:   **Is there anyone who knows what she likes?**
:   *"There is one... Yngvar. He's quite popular with the ladies. Thankfully Faleen is not quite his type, but they've been friends for some time, and he may have some ideas. Please, ask him what she likes. It's my only chance."*

Calcelmo and Faleen

When you hand him Faleen's [letter](/wiki/Skyrim:Faleen%27s_Letter_to_Calcelmo "Skyrim:Faleen's Letter to Calcelmo"):

:   **I have a letter from Faleen.**
:   *"This is... more than I could have hoped for. Have you really done this for me? I have to see her. Please, excuse me."*

He'll then run to Faleen and have the following conversation:

**Calcelmo**: *"Faleen... I..."*
**Faleen**: *"Sssh. It's all right. You don't need to say anymore. I had no idea you were so... nuanced."*
**Calcelmo**: *"I love you."*
**Faleen**: *"So I hear. Come here, you."*

### Buy Dwarven Artifact

If you acquire a Dwarven item you may get a [letter from Calcelmo](/wiki/Skyrim:Letter_from_Calcemo "Skyrim:Letter from Calcemo"). You can then speak to him regarding it:

:   **I'm here about the <Alias=Item>.**
:   *"You are? Very good.... may I see it?"*

:   :   **Actually, I'm not sure I have it anymore.**
    :   *"Oh... what a terrible shame. Well, if you think you know where you left it and can retrieve it, I'll be here."*

:   :   **Sure. Take a look.**
    :   *"Excellent. Very good. This is exactly what I need to complete a series of studies I'm doing on Dwemer craftsmanship and magical resonance. I simply must have this! I'll pay you double what it's worth."*

You'll now have a few options:

| Your Dialogue | Calcelmo's Reply | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Sounds fair. Here you go. (Gain gold)** | *"Wonderful. You've just made an important contribution to the advancement of a Dwemer scholarship."* |
| **Not good enough. I'll hold onto this. You'll need to find another one.** | *"Oh... well... I can see you have no appreciation for scholarship."* |
| **Not good enough. I'll shake the extra coin out of you if I must. (Intimidate)** | **Passed**: *"Hold on, there. I suppose, in the uh, interest of research... I can spare a few more coins. Double and a half its value. That's all I can muster."* **Failed**: *"Ha! I'll see to it the Jarl hears of your abuse of a court scholar. Shame on you."* |
| **I think you can do better than that. (Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"Well... I suppose important research is worth every coin. All right. You have yourself a deal. How's double and a half its value in trade?"* **Failed**: *"With this the world could have a better understanding of the Dwemer! Come now, where's your sense of propriety? Extorting an old man like this."* |

If you successfully persuaded or intimidated him you can tell him not good enough, getting the same response as above, or say his offer sounds fair, to which he'll respond:

:   *"I'm glad we could come to an agreement."*

Note that if it is a Dwarven arrow or bolt he is attempting to buy from you, you can't actually sell it to him if you have more than one in your inventory. Drop or store all of the Dwarven arrows or bolts but one, and the appropriate dialogue will appear.

If you go through the dialogue until you persuade him, then exit the conversation, you can level up your Speech skill which can be repeated endlessly.

### Hard Answers

During this quest, [Enthir](/wiki/Skyrim:Enthir "Skyrim:Enthir") will point you to Calcelmo to translate [Gallus's Encoded Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Gallus%27s_Encoded_Journal "Skyrim:Gallus's Encoded Journal"), which is in the Falmer language. When you approach him, he'll have a greeting based on whether you have completed his portion of The Book of Love:

:   *"Ah yes, my matchmaker. What is it I can do for you?"* or *"Look, I'm very busy, so this better be important."*
:   **I hear you're the authority on ancient Falmer.**
:   *"Then you were well informed. I am at this very moment on the cusp of completing my magnum opus on the subject. I'm calling it 'Calcelmo's Guide to the Falmer Tongue.' It will revolutionize the way we understand those ancient beings."*
:   **Perhaps I could view your work?**
:   *"Preposterous! That research represents years of personal toil in some of the most dangerous Dwemer ruins in Skyrim! You must be mad to think I'd allow anyone to see it before it's completed."*

You'll now have a few options:

| Your Dialogue | Calcelmo's Reply | |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Even after everything I did for you and Faleen?**† | *"Well, I'm not blind to the fact that you've been instrumental in improving my affairs of the heart. If you wish, you may enter my tower to view the museum section, but I'm afraid the laboratories are still off limits. That's the best I can offer."* or, if you already have the museum key, *"I've already provided you a key to the museum. You should consider it an honor. Few are allowed to browse my collection. I'm sorry, but that's as far as my generosity extends."* |
| **Even after slaying your troublesome spider?**†† | *"I've already provided you a key to the museum. You should consider it an honor. Few are allowed to browse my collection. I'm sorry, but that's as far as my generosity extends."* |
| **But I'm a great admirer of your work. (Persuade)** | **Passed**: *"What kind of a mentor would I be if I denied a potential student a glimpse at his master's ingenuity! Here, this key will provide access to my museum. Feel free to browse for as long as you wish. However, I must insist that my laboratory remains strictly off limits."* **Failed**: *"While I appreciate the sentiment, I still have to decline. Being an admirer, I'm sure you can appreciate the need to keep my research a secret."* |
| **What will it cost to change your mind? (Bribe)** | **Failed**: *"I'm not certain how many scholars you're accustomed to dealing with, but I can assure you that personal wealth is our lowest priority."* |
| **Grant me access or you'll regret it. (Intimidate)** | **Failed**: *"Do you realize that at a snap of my fingers I can bring the entire Markarth city guard to my defense? You best rethink this course of action or you may find yourself on the executioner's block."* |
| **Forget it. Maybe I'll come back later.** | *"Very well. Perhaps when my research is complete, I'll feel more comfortable discussing my findings with you."* |

†Only available if you completed his portion of The Book of Love.

††Only available if you completed Nimhe, the Poisoned One.

When exiting conversation while the key is in your possession, he'll say:

:   *"I hope you enjoy touring the museum. Just don't touch anything."*

If you don't have the key, he'll say:

:   *"Oh, be certain to purchase my Falmer translation tome when it's completed!"*
:   *"Now, stand aside, there's work to be done."*
:   *"Try not to disturb me in the future, I'm in the midst of groundbreaking research!"*

If you talk to him later without the key, he'll say:

:   *"What is it this time?"*
:   *"This better be important."*

If you talk to him later with the key, he'll say:

:   *"I've already provided you with the key to my museum, what else could you possibly want?"*

### The Lost Expedition

While searching Nchuand-Zel, you may find notes (like [this](/wiki/Skyrim:Alethius%27s_Notes "Skyrim:Alethius's Notes")) from dead scholars. If you show these to Calcelmo:

:   **I've found this expedition journal.**
:   *"Oh really? Hmm... this looks like someone from [Staubin](/wiki/Skyrim:Staubin "Skyrim:Staubin")'s little group. A brave scholar, but not very wise.... If you find Staubin, it would be good to see any [notes](/wiki/Skyrim:Staubin%27s_Diary "Skyrim:Staubin's Diary") he may have collected. I doubt you'll find him alive, though."*

When you bring him Staubin's diary:

:   **I've found this expedition journal.**
:   *"Let's see. Ah, so that's what happened to Staubin. Tragic, but I warned him he was leading those people on a fool's errand. Unfortunately, sometimes the stone of scholarship is built on the foundation of death. I'll inform the kin. Here, I usually pay researchers for their work when they emerge from the ruins, but they won't be needing it anymore."*

## Displayed Merchandise

The following items are sitting out in the store, for example on the store counters. They can be purchased from the merchant, or else can be stolen. Other items may also be present in the store, but those other items are not available for purchase. They [respawn](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") after ten days. Note: After completing his section of [The Book of Love](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Love "Skyrim:The Book of Love") quest, these items are free to take. They will show in his inventory for sell once the [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk is taken, but they are the same items and disappear from the store floor if purchased until the next respawn.

- Books: 1 *[Dwarves, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarves,_v1 "Skyrim:Dwarves, v1")*, 1 *[Dwarves, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarves,_v2 "Skyrim:Dwarves, v2")*
- Food (req. [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk): 1 [Red Apple](/wiki/Skyrim:Red_Apple "Skyrim:Red Apple")
- Ore/Ingots (req. [Merchant](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_(perk) "Skyrim:Merchant (perk)") perk): 1 [Bent Dwemer Scrap Metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bent_Dwemer_Scrap_Metal "Skyrim:Bent Dwemer Scrap Metal"), 1 [Dwemer Cog](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cog "Skyrim:Dwemer Cog"), 1 [Dwemer Gyro](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Gyro "Skyrim:Dwemer Gyro"), 1 [Dwemer Lever](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Lever "Skyrim:Dwemer Lever"), 1 [Large Decorative Dwemer Strut](/wiki/Skyrim:Large_Decorative_Dwemer_Strut "Skyrim:Large Decorative Dwemer Strut"), 1 [Large Dwemer Strut](/wiki/Skyrim:Large_Dwemer_Strut "Skyrim:Large Dwemer Strut"), 1 [Small Dwemer Plate Metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Small_Dwemer_Plate_Metal "Skyrim:Small Dwemer Plate Metal"), 2 [Solid Dwemer Metal](/wiki/Skyrim:Solid_Dwemer_Metal "Skyrim:Solid Dwemer Metal")

## Standard Merchandise

This is the merchandise found in Calcelmo's [merchant chest](/wiki/Skyrim:Merchant_Chest "Skyrim:Merchant Chest"). These items are only available if purchased from the merchant; they cannot be pickpocketed or stolen. They are [restocked](/wiki/Skyrim:Respawning "Skyrim:Respawning") every two days.

| Count | Item | Details |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | Complete set of Novice [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes") |  |
| 1 | Complete set of Apprentice [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Spell_Tomes "Skyrim:Spell Tomes") |  |
| 1 | Complete set of Adept [Conjuration](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration "Skyrim:Conjuration") [Spell Tomes](/wiki/Skyrim:Conjuration_Spells "Skyrim:Conjuration Spells") | Only if PC's skill level is high enough |
| 3 | *[Dwarves, v1](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarves,_v1 "Skyrim:Dwarves, v1")* |  |
| 2 | *[Dwarves, v2](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarves,_v2 "Skyrim:Dwarves, v2")* |  |
| 2 | *[Dwarves, v3](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwarves,_v3 "Skyrim:Dwarves, v3")* |  |
| ~4 | Leveled Robes (enchanted) | Max 5 (5@75%) |
| ~9 | Leveled [Scrolls](/wiki/Skyrim:Scrolls "Skyrim:Scrolls") | Max 12 (12@75%) |
| ~15 | Leveled [Soul Gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Soul_Gems "Skyrim:Soul Gems") (empty and full) | Max 20 (20@75%) |

## Notes

- NPCs in the game are not consistent in their pronunciation of his name. Some NPCs, including Enthir, pronounce it multiple ways during their course of dialogue.

## Bugs

- Calcelmo may sell the ring you delivered to him for Kerah's favor quest.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3.3, addresses this issue. He will equip the ring so that it is no longer visible for purchase in his merchant inventory.
- At some point after purchasing a Dwarven item, you will receive a note from Calcelmo in Markarth. If you go through the dialogue until you persuade him, then exit the conversation, you can repeat endlessly to level up your Speech skill.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.5, fixes this bug.

Calder

**Calder** is a [Nord](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord "Skyrim:Nord") [warrior](/wiki/Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H "Skyrim:CombatWarrior1H") from [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm").

Once you have purchased the home in Windhelm, [Hjerim](/wiki/Skyrim:Hjerim "Skyrim:Hjerim"), and attained the rank of [thane](/wiki/Skyrim:Thane "Skyrim:Thane") of Windhelm, Calder is appointed your [housecarl](/wiki/Skyrim:Housecarl "Skyrim:Housecarl") and will automatically appear in Hjerim.

Calder wears a set of [steel armor](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Armor "Skyrim:Steel Armor"), a pair of [steel Nordic gauntlets](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Nordic_Gauntlets "Skyrim:Steel Nordic Gauntlets"), and a pair of [steel cuffed boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Cuffed_Boots "Skyrim:Steel Cuffed Boots"). He is equipped with a [steel war axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_War_Axe "Skyrim:Steel War Axe") and a [steel shield](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Shield "Skyrim:Steel Shield").

He will wait in the home until he is ordered to [follow](/wiki/Skyrim:Followers "Skyrim:Followers") you. If he is dismissed he will return to Hjerim and resume waiting.

He is also a potential candidate for [marriage](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").

## Related Quests

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[Rebuilding the Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Rebuilding_the_Blades "Skyrim:Rebuilding the Blades")**: Recruit new members for the [Blades](/wiki/Skyrim:Blades "Skyrim:Blades").

## Bugs

- He may attack you for no apparent reason. **?**
  - Gaining a bounty in a hold, then paying it off, seems to work.
- Calder will address you as a stranger (i.e. "You lost?") whenever you enter Hjerim if he is not a current follower.

Calixto Corrium

**Calixto Corrium** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [rogue](/wiki/Skyrim:Rogue "Skyrim:Rogue") living the life of leisure in [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"). He used to go adventuring with his sister Lucilla until she passed away. After that, he settled down and opened [Calixto's House of Curiosities](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto%27s_House_of_Curiosities "Skyrim:Calixto's House of Curiosities") to put on display the assortment of curiosities he had collected, such as [The Book of Fate](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Fate "Skyrim:The Book of Fate") and [Ysgramor's Soup Spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Soup_Spoon "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Soup Spoon"). For more information, see the [lore article](/wiki/Lore:Calixto_Corrium "Lore:Calixto Corrium").

Calixto wears a set of merchant [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223c "Skyrim:Clothing") along with a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothing#0004223d "Skyrim:Clothing"). He wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger") and carries [Calixto's key](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto%27s_Key "Skyrim:Calixto's Key") along with a selection of [upper-class loot and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Rich "Skyrim:Leveled Lists").

## Related Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.

## Dialogue

His greetings:

:   *"If you've got some time, stop by my House of Curiosities. I promise you'll see wonders!"*
:   *"My sister and I once traveled the world to assemble our collection. Such adventures we had!"*
:   *"I don't care much for the war one way or the other."*
:   *"It bothers me that fewer people come to Windhelm these days."*

When you enter his house during opening hours, he will give you a warm welcome:

:   *"Welcome, friend, to Calixto's House of Curiosities!"*

When spoken to:

:   *"Welcome to the House of Curiosities! I offer a brief tour for a few coins, or you can simply browse at your leisure."*
:   **How did you assemble this collection?**
:   *"My sister and I inherited a modest sum of money. We decided to travel and seek out whatever adventures we could find. As we journeyed across Tamriel, we encountered tales of exotic and wondrous artifacts. We decided to collect as many as we could. My sister passed away some years ago, so I settled down here and opened the House of Curiosities. I think she would be happy to know that our collection has brought smiles to faces both young and old."*

:   **You mentioned a tour?**
:   *"Indeed I did! For a few septims, I'll tell you about some of the most interesting curiosities in my collection."*

:   :   **Another time, maybe.**
    :   *"Very well. If you change your mind, you can usually find me here. In the meantime, feel free to look around."*

:   :   **I'll take the tour. (2 gold)**
    :   *"Splendid! If you'll just follow me, I'll tell you tales and show you wonders such as you've never seen."*

Calixto will then get out of his chair and walk over to a set of shelves with various [embalming tools](/wiki/Skyrim:Embalming_Tool "Skyrim:Embalming Tool"):

:   *"These tools were found in a crypt outside Windhelm. They belonged to the ancient Nords who dwelt in Skyrim before the days of the First Empire. Most scholars believe that the Nords of old used these implements to prepare their dead for burial. What macabre mysteries would these tools reveal if they could but speak?"*

On the next set of shelves sits *[The Book of Fate](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Fate "Skyrim:The Book of Fate")*:

:   *"Here is the Book of Fate, discovered in a secret room in the Arcane University. The writing in the book describes the destiny of its reader, so the words change from one person to the next. Some see only blank pages, and nobody knows why. Perhaps some of us are born with no destiny, or maybe the blank pages signify an imminent death."*

The next curiosity is [Ysgramor's Soup Spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Soup_Spoon "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Soup Spoon"):

:   *"Ah, now here is an item out of legend. This is Ysgramor's Soup Spoon. Now, I know what you're thinking - this is no spoon, it's a fork! Nobody can eat soup with a fork! Well, my friend, you did not know Ysgramor."*

He will then proceed to the next odd item, the [Dancer's Flute](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dancer%27s_Flute "Skyrim:The Dancer's Flute"):

:   *"Don't let this innocent-looking flute fool you, for this is the Dancer's Pipe. Legend holds that the Dancer's Pipe has won wars, toppled empires and changed the very course of history. None know its origins, but the stories say that men who hear its music are compelled to dance uncontrollably, no matter the peril. To activate this strange power, one must only speak the magic words, which are... Oh my, I very nearly got us both into a nasty predicament, didn't I?"*

He will then end the tour with a farewell:

:   *"And with that, the tour is over. I thank you for your patronage, and I hope to see you again soon!"*

His goodbyes:

:   *"A most pleasant chat. Until the next!"*
:   *"I bid you safe travels."*

## Conversations

Calixto will randomly have brief conversations with Elda at Candlehearth Hall:

*"Calixto, do you know if there's any truth to these rumors of dragons?"*

:   **Elda**: *"Calixto, do you know if there's any truth to these rumors of dragons?"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Eh. I try not to trouble myself with stories of the outside world. Now if someone brings me a dragon scale, that's a different story."*
:   **Elda**: *"But how would you know it's real?"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Ah, I can't reveal all my secrets to you. But rest assured, I would know."*

:   **Elda**: *"Calixto, someone left an interesting ring in here a few weeks ago. Would you like a look?"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Of course, my dear. It may prove to be quite the curiosity! One must always be alert."*
:   **Elda**: *"Well, I seem to have misplaced it at the moment. But it was white, like alabaster, with three bright rubies set in it."*
:   **Calixto**: *"Be very careful with that. It sounds as if it may be the Death Ring of Dro'farahn. A ring of the most dangerous sort."*
:   **Elda**: *"Oh dear. What should I do?"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Bring it to me straight away when you find it. Don't dally. I can keep it safe."*
:   **Elda**: *"Oh, thank the gods you're in Windhelm, Calixto!"*
:   **Calixto**: *"Think nothing of it."*

### Blood on the Ice

Calixto Corrium at the scene

Calixto Corrium appears at the scene of Susanna the Wicked's murder:

:   *"Always a shame when someone has to die."*
:   **Did you see what happened here?**
:   *"Sorry. I thought I saw a fellow running away, but didn't get a good look at him."*

After reading *[Beware the Butcher!](/wiki/Skyrim:Beware_the_Butcher! "Skyrim:Beware the Butcher!")*:

:   **I found this poster in Hjerim.**
:   *"Oh, good, more of those. Did you know Viola Giordano wanted to put one of them on my front door? "Everyone will see it!" she said. Of course! That was my problem with it. If you want to ask her about them, good luck. But I'm not going near her."*

After investigating Hjerim and finding the [strange amulet](/wiki/Skyrim:Quest_Items#Strange_Amulet "Skyrim:Quest Items"):

:   **Do you know anything about this amulet?**
:   *"Let me see... ah, yes. This is the Wheelstone. It's an heirloom symbol of the power of Windhelm. Traditionally it's carried by the court mage. I would... eh... be interested in acquiring it. If you're willing to part with it, that is. For a piece like that, I could pay... 500 gold?"*

:   :   **You have yourself a deal, sir.**
    :   *"Wonderful. This will be a splendid addition to my private collection."*

:   :   **Shouldn't the court mage have it?**
    :   *"Wuunferth? Bah. It's purely ceremonial, and he has no use for it. Besides, I wouldn't want to be the one to give it to him. Gives me the creeps. They say he dabbles in necromancy."*

:   :   **I think I'll hold on to it for the time being.**
    :   *"Suit yourself. It's only of value to collectors, though. Good luck finding anyone else who will appraise it that highly!"*

If you didn't sell the amulet you can speak to him again about it:

:   **About that amulet...**
:   *"The Wheelstone? Have you decided to sell it, yet?"*

## Notes

- Calixto becomes unessential when he draws his blade during the related quest.

## Bugs

- Calixto may give his tour even if you don't have any money.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.2, fixes this bug.
- Pickpocketing the key from Calixto allows access to knowing his true purpose in Blood on the Ice without being able to tell anyone about it.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 2.0.1, addresses this issue. His key will now be a death item instead of an inventory item.

# Skyrim:Calixto's House of Curiosities

## Overview

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| |  | | --- | | Home: Calixto's House of Curiosities ([view on map](https://gamemap.uesp.net/sr/?world=Skyrim&centeron=Calixto%27s+House+of+Curiosities)) | | |
