Calixto's House of Curiosities located in Windhelm.

**Calixto's House of Curiosities** is the home of [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium"), who also uses it as a museum of odd and curious items.

Calixto's House of Curiosities is found in the east side of [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm"), before entering the Gray Quarter. It contains only one zone; *[Calixto's House of Curiosities](#Calixto.27s_House_of_Curiosities)*.

## Residents

| Residents |
| --- |
| [Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium") |

## Related Quests

- **[Blood on the Ice](/wiki/Skyrim:Blood_on_the_Ice "Skyrim:Blood on the Ice")**: [Windhelm](/wiki/Skyrim:Windhelm "Skyrim:Windhelm") is plagued by a shadowy killer.

## Calixto's House of Curiosities

The interior of the House of Curiosities

[Calixto Corrium](/wiki/Skyrim:Calixto_Corrium "Skyrim:Calixto Corrium") and his sister Lucilla inherited a considerable fortune from their parents, and decided to travel across [Tamriel](/wiki/Lore:Tamriel "Lore:Tamriel") years ago. During their travels, they collected a number of curious and, some might say, legendary items. When his sister died, he settled in Windhelm and opened his collection for public viewing.

While Calixto is awake between 5am and 12am, his door is only unlocked from 9am until 8pm, the same as a regular store. Outside of these hours, it is locked with a leveled lock. During the opening hours, you can enter the house and look around, or pay Calixto 2 [septims](/wiki/Skyrim:Gold "Skyrim:Gold") for a guided tour, on which he points out the most intriguing items in his collection and proceeds to give a little background story on each of them.

Upon entering, in the northwest corner, under the stairs that lead up to a small loft area, is a table holding an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger"), an [iron mace](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Mace "Skyrim:Iron Mace"), and a copy of *[Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?](/wiki/Skyrim:Nightingales:_Fact_or_Fiction%3F "Skyrim:Nightingales: Fact or Fiction?")*. Against the north wall are two sets of shelves holding a bowl of [void salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Void_Salts "Skyrim:Void Salts"), a [salt pile](/wiki/Skyrim:Salt_Pile "Skyrim:Salt Pile"), two bowls of [troll fat](/wiki/Skyrim:Troll_Fat "Skyrim:Troll Fat"), two bowls of [frost salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Frost_Salts "Skyrim:Frost Salts"), a collection of Ancient Nord [Embalming Tools](/wiki/Skyrim:Embalming_Tool "Skyrim:Embalming Tool") (the first item shown by Calixto during his guided tour), a bowl of [fire salts](/wiki/Skyrim:Fire_Salts "Skyrim:Fire Salts"), a bowl of [bone meal](/wiki/Skyrim:Bone_Meal "Skyrim:Bone Meal"), some [slaughterfish scales](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Scales "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Scales"), seven [slaughterfish eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Slaughterfish_Egg "Skyrim:Slaughterfish Egg"), three [spider eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Spider_Egg "Skyrim:Spider Egg"), three [chaurus eggs](/wiki/Skyrim:Chaurus_Eggs "Skyrim:Chaurus Eggs"), and a bowl of [mammoth cheese](/wiki/Skyrim:Mammoth_Cheese_Bowl "Skyrim:Mammoth Cheese Bowl"), with a bottle of [Frostbite venom](/wiki/Skyrim:Frostbite_Venom "Skyrim:Frostbite Venom") on top of the left-hand shelving unit.

Against the east wall is a third set of shelves holding three [iron ingots](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Ingot "Skyrim:Iron Ingot"), an empty [lesser soul gem](/wiki/Skyrim:Lesser_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Lesser Soul Gem"), two empty [petty soul gems](/wiki/Skyrim:Petty_Soul_Gem "Skyrim:Petty Soul Gem"), a [potion of minor stamina](/wiki/Skyrim:Potion_of_Minor_Stamina "Skyrim:Potion of Minor Stamina"), a sample of [hagraven feathers](/wiki/Skyrim:Hagraven_Feathers "Skyrim:Hagraven Feathers"), and [The Book of Fate](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Book_of_Fate "Skyrim:The Book of Fate"). The Book of Fate is a unique book in which each reader sees their own destiny, unless it is blank, which is suggested by Calixto to be caused either by the reader having no predetermined destiny, or by imminent death. This is the second item shown on the guided tour. To the right of these shelves, in the southeast corner of this part of the shop, is a round wooden table and chair, with two [giant's toes](/wiki/Skyrim:Giant%27s_Toe "Skyrim:Giant's Toe") and some bones on the table. Beside it is a wooden support, with three [garlic](/wiki/Skyrim:Garlic "Skyrim:Garlic") braids hanging from it.

Calixto's bedroom

Around the corner, against the east wall, is another set of shelves holding a bunch of [lavender](/wiki/Skyrim:Lavender "Skyrim:Lavender"), a collection of Dwemer items including [cups](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Cup "Skyrim:Dwemer Cup"), [plates](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Plate "Skyrim:Dwemer Plate"), and a [dish](/wiki/Skyrim:Dwemer_Dish "Skyrim:Dwemer Dish"), and [Ysgramor's Soup Spoon](/wiki/Skyrim:Ysgramor%27s_Soup_Spoon "Skyrim:Ysgramor's Soup Spoon"). The spoon is the third item on the guided tour, and appears to actually be a fork and not a spoon. To the right is a long wooden table holding [The Dancer's Flute](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Dancer%27s_Flute "Skyrim:The Dancer's Flute") among some skulls and bones. The flute is the fourth and final item on the guided tour. Under the table is an unlocked respawning chest, which is empty. To the right, against the south wall to the left of the doorway into Calixto's bedroom, is another set of shelves holding a [woodcutter's axe](/wiki/Skyrim:Woodcutter%27s_Axe "Skyrim:Woodcutter's Axe") and a respawning [knapsack](/wiki/Skyrim:Knapsack "Skyrim:Knapsack") which contains leveled items, with a barrel containing foodstuffs beside it.

Through the doorway is his bedroom, which contains an owned single bed along the east wall, which remains owned even after his death. Against the north wall is a tall wardrobe containing [clothes](/wiki/Skyrim:Clothes "Skyrim:Clothes"), and opposite, against the south wall, is a square wooden table holding a bottle of [Nord mead](/wiki/Skyrim:Nord_Mead "Skyrim:Nord Mead"). Against the west wall is a [cooking pot](/wiki/Skyrim:Cooking_Pot "Skyrim:Cooking Pot") on a stand. Climbing the stairs to the loft area in the main room, there is a locked non-respawning chest tagged Calixto's Chest, which contains the [Butcher Journal](/wiki/Skyrim:Butcher_Journal "Skyrim:Butcher Journal"), a [steel dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Steel_Dagger "Skyrim:Steel Dagger"), and some embalming tools. There is a second loft that is only reachable using the Whirlwind Sprint shout; however, it only contains a large stack of crates and four food barrels.

## Bugs

- If you ask Calixto for a guided tour when the shop is closed, the shop will be permanently locked.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.2.6, fixes this bug.

Camilla Valerius in Riverwood Trader

**Camilla Valerius** is an [Imperial](/wiki/Skyrim:Imperial "Skyrim:Imperial") [pawnbroker](/wiki/Skyrim:Pawnbroker "Skyrim:Pawnbroker"), and the sister of [Lucan Valerius](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius"), the owner of [Riverwood Trader](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Riverwood Trader") in [Riverwood](/wiki/Skyrim:Riverwood "Skyrim:Riverwood"). If Lucan dies, Camilla will take over the store. She is involved in a local [love triangle](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter") as the love interest of both [Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal") and [Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven"). She may be [married](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage") if her disposition towards you is high enough, giving you full access to the Riverwood Trader.

She wakes up at 7am for a one-hour breakfast, then starts working at the store for ten hours. At 6pm, she heads to [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn") for a drink and [chats](#Conversations) with other patrons. She stays there until 10pm, when she goes outside for a walk around Riverwood. She returns home at 12am to sleep.

She wears a [belted tunic](/wiki/Skyrim:Belted_Tunic "Skyrim:Belted Tunic") and a pair of [boots](/wiki/Skyrim:Boots#0001be1b "Skyrim:Boots"). She carries a [key](/wiki/Skyrim:Key_to_Riverwood_Trader "Skyrim:Key to Riverwood Trader") to Riverwood Trader as well as [common items and gold](/wiki/Skyrim:Leveled_Lists#Common "Skyrim:Leveled Lists"). She wields an [iron dagger](/wiki/Skyrim:Iron_Dagger "Skyrim:Iron Dagger").

## Related Quests

- **[The Bonds of Matrimony](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Bonds_of_Matrimony "Skyrim:The Bonds of Matrimony")**: Find someone in [Skyrim](/wiki/Lore:Skyrim "Lore:Skyrim") to [marry](/wiki/Skyrim:Marriage "Skyrim:Marriage").
- **[The Golden Claw](/wiki/Skyrim:The_Golden_Claw "Skyrim:The Golden Claw")**: A [shopkeeper](/wiki/Skyrim:Lucan_Valerius "Skyrim:Lucan Valerius") wants you to retrieve his [prized possession](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw") from a [bandit](/wiki/Skyrim:Arvel_the_Swift "Skyrim:Arvel the Swift").
- **[A Lovely Letter](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter")**: Use a forged letter to resolve a love triangle.

### The Golden Claw

When you enter the Riverwood Trader for the first time, you can witness an argument between Lucan and Camilla regarding the stolen [golden claw](/wiki/Skyrim:Golden_Claw "Skyrim:Golden Claw"):

**Camilla**: *"Well one of us has to do something!"*
**Lucan**: *"I said no! No adventures, no theatrics, no thief-chasing!"*
**Camilla**: *"Well what are you going to do then, huh? Let's hear it!"*
**Lucan**: *"We are done talking about this. Oh, a customer. Sorry you had to hear that."*

If Lucan is dead, you will have to get the quest from Camilla:

:   **What were you arguing about with Lucan?**
:   *"You mean before he died? We had a break in. Thieves didn't touch anything on the shelves, or any coin, just one thing. A solid gold ornament, in the shape of a dragon's claw."*
:   **I could help you get the claw back.**
:   *"Oh really? Well, I'm not going to hold my breath. The thieves are up in Bleak Falls Barrow, northeast of town. I'd take you there, but with Lucan gone, I'm busy with the store."*

If Lucan is alive you may offer to bring back the golden claw for him. Camilla will then question Lucan's plan of sending you to reacquire the claw:

**Camilla**: *"So this is your plan, Lucan?"*
**Lucan**: *"Yes. So now you don't have to go, do you?"*
**Camilla**: *"Oh really? Well I think your new helper here needs a guide."*
**Lucan**: *"Wh- no... I.... Oh, by the Eight, fine. But only to the edge of town!"*
**Camilla**: *"Now, if you're going to get those thieves, you should head to Bleak Falls Barrow, northeast of town."*

You can tell her if you want her to escort you or not:

:   *"If you're going after the claw, you'll need to know the way."*
:   **I don't need a guide.**
:   *"Oh, really? You're just like my brother. Fine, but if you change your mind, I'll be right here."*

:   **Lead on then.**
:   *"I'll meet you outside!"*

If you accept the offer, she will accompany you until the stone bridge to the north. She will make comments about the barrow, the thieves, and the claw as she directs you out of town:

:   *"Those thieves must be mad, hiding out there. Those old crypts are filled with nothing but traps, trolls, and who knows what else! I wonder why they only stole Lucan's golden claw. I mean, we have plenty of things in the shop that are worth just as much coin. Lucan found the claw about a year after he opened the store. He never quite explained where he got it. He's a tricky one."*

Somewhere in the middle of town, she will gesture towards the barrow and say:

:   *"We have to go through town and across the bridge to get to Bleak Falls Barrow. You can see it from here, though. The mountain just over the buildings."*

Once you reach the bridge, she will say:

:   *"This is the bridge out of town. The path up the mountain to the northwest leads to Bleak Falls Barrow. I guess I should get back to my brother. He'll throw a fit if I take too long. Such a child...."*

As she walks off she will say:

:   *"Good luck. Lucan and I will be waiting for you back in the shop."*

Once you return with the golden claw if you speak to her before speaking to Lucan:

:   *"You have the claw. Oh, you have to tell Lucan at once. Hurry!"*
:   *"Hurry up and tell Lucan you have the claw. He'll be so excited!"*

### A Lovely Letter

If you decide to help Faendal and give her the fake letter:

:   **I have a letter for you, from Sven. (Lie)**
:   *"Another poem, I'll bet. He does know how to make a girl blush. What's this? If that oaf thinks all I'm going to do is stay in that filthy house of his and clean, I'll.... You can tell Sven that he already has a mother. I'm not speaking to him anymore."*

If you decide to help Sven and give her the fake letter:

:   **I have a letter from Faendal. (Lie)**
:   *"From Faendal? That's strange. He's never written to me before. What, what is this? Is this what he really thinks about me? Well, you can tell that... that long-eared ass not to come around the store anymore. He's not welcome."*

If you decide to tell the truth about Sven's fake letter:

:   **Sven wanted to trick you into believing this letter was from Faendal.**
:   *"What are you talking about? What's in the letter? Oh my. He... he wanted me to think Faendal wrote this? Thank you for telling me the truth. Could you talk to Faendal, as well? I'm sure he'll want to thank you for standing up for him."*

If you decide to tell the truth about Faendal's fake letter:

:   **Faendal asked me to give you this letter, and say it was from Sven.**
:   *"He what? What are you talking about? Why that jealous idiot. Thought he could just manipulate me into never seeing Sven again? Thank you for telling me the truth. You should speak to Sven. I'm sure he'll want to thank you, too, for defending his name."*

## Dialogue

Her greetings can be:

:   *"You're a strapping young man. Don't be a stranger."* (If you're male)
:   *"The men here like my attention, and I like theirs. Best know your place."* (If you're female)
:   *"Thanks for bringing the claw back."*
:   *"It means so much to us to have the claw back where it belongs. Thank you!"*
:   *"You're not from around here. That makes two of us."*
:   *"I came here from the Imperial Province, to work with my brother Lucan."*
:   *"It got bad back in Cyrodiil. The war with the Thalmor ruined... everything."*
:   *"I came to Skyrim looking for a better life. So what did I get? Another war."*
:   *"I just want to find a good husband, and start a family of my own."*
:   *"Lucan's dead. I guess I'm in charge of the Riverwood Trader now."*
:   *"I guess Lucan will never see the golden claw again now."*

## Conversations

After the completion of the quest The Golden Claw, the two siblings can be seen having a conversation about the goods they sell. They will pick between one of three available dialogue:

| Dialogue |
| --- |
| **Camilla**: *"Lucan, we don't sell silver buckles, do we? One of the customers was asking."* |
| **Lucan**: *"No, dear sister. We do not."* |
| **Camilla**: *"Hmm. All right. Do you think... maybe we should?"* |
| **Lucan**: *"That's really not at the top of my list, no. Please, Camilla, I need you to focus."* |
| **Camilla**: *"Of course, Lucan. Of course. I was just, well... Never mind."* |
| **Camilla**: *"We don't sell any imports from Summerset Isle, do we, Lucan?"* |
| **Lucan**: *"I'm afraid not."* |
| **Camilla**: *"Well, I was thinking... we should. We could stock all kinds of specialty items. You know, to cater to some of our more.... 'eclectic' customers."* |
| **Lucan**: *"Dear sister, we talked about this sort of thing before. We sell dry goods, nothing more, nothing less."* |
| **Camilla**: *"Okay, okay. Just trying make this place a little less... boring."* |
| **Camilla**: *"Lucan, I was thinking we should have a grand sale. Lower the prices by half, maybe get some jugglers. We could attract lots of new customers."* |
| **Lucan**: *"A sale? To attract new customers? Camilla, everyone in Riverwood already shops here. There are no more customers."* |
| **Camilla**: *"Hmmm... Well, maybe we could go on a sort of trip. Take the wares on the road. Get some new customers."* |
| **Lucan**: *"Camilla, really? You don't have better things to do? Because I could certainly find quite a few tasks..."* |
| **Camilla**: *"I know, I know. My head's in the clouds again. Just... forget I said anything."* |

In the evening, Camilla may spend some time in the [Sleeping Giant Inn](/wiki/Skyrim:Sleeping_Giant_Inn "Skyrim:Sleeping Giant Inn"). Depending on who is present with her in the inn, she may have conversations with two different people.

[Hod](/wiki/Skyrim:Hod "Skyrim:Hod") advises Camilla about her [love triangle](/wiki/Skyrim:A_Lovely_Letter "Skyrim:A Lovely Letter") with [Faendal](/wiki/Skyrim:Faendal "Skyrim:Faendal") and [Sven](/wiki/Skyrim:Sven "Skyrim:Sven"):

**Hod**: *"You need to choose between those two boys. It ain't fair to Sven or Faendal to keep tuggin' on their heart strings like that."*
**Camilla**: *"It's bad enough my brother is harping on me to pick one. Don't you start too."*
**Hod**: *"I'm just sayin' you should pick one to settle down with."*

Camilla compliments Sven on his performance:

**Camilla**: *"You play so well."*
**Sven**: *"With you as my muse, how could I not?"*
**Camilla**: *"Oh, Sven. You do know how to turn a girl's head."*

## Notes

- Her gold is shared with her brother; if you sell to her, then her brother will also lose gold.
- If you complete the Lovely Letter quest, she will retain the letter forever.

## Bugs

- If you invest 500 gold into the shop (using the [Investor](/wiki/Skyrim:Investor "Skyrim:Investor") perk), regardless of if it's operated by Lucan or Camilla, it adds 10,000 gold instead of 500 gold to their inventory.
  - The [Official Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim:Patch "Skyrim:Patch"), version 1.9, fixes this bug.
- If you marry her, Faendal or Sven may still visit her at your house occasionally (depending on whom you helped in the related quest).
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.0, fixes this bug.
- Even after you marry her, she may continue to thank you for returning the golden claw.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Patch"), version 1.3, fixes this bug.
  - Adopting a child with her may also fix it.
- If you marry her and have built a house with the [Hearthfire](/wiki/Skyrim:Hearthfire "Skyrim:Hearthfire") add-on, she may not move. Furthermore, you will not be able to ask her to move anywhere else.
- If you marry her and do not move from Riverwood, she may lack the dialogue where she says she has opened up a shop, and so Camilla will not have a trading menu nor will she give you 100 daily septims. **?**
- If A Lovely Letter is still running when marrying Camilla, it is still possible to finish it by delivering the letter on behalf of one or the other even though this scene no longer makes sense to allow.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.1, addresses this issue. Marrying Camilla while the quest is still active will now cause it to fail.
- Camilla can sometimes get stuck in front of the Sleeping Giant Inn, possibly due to the space between her AI markers being too far apart.
  -  The [Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch](/wiki/Skyrim_Mod:Unofficial_Skyrim_Legendary_Edition_Patch "Skyrim Mod:Unofficial Skyrim Legendary Edition Patch"), version 3.0.8, fixes this bug.
